### [51] [DualMem: Bypassing the Objectness Bottleneck for Calibrated Unknown-Stream Filtering in Open-World Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23634)
*Yingjun Xiao,Xi Chen,Gang Fang,Siyuan Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究开放世界目标检测（OWOD）中未知物体预测的噪声问题，发现强OWOD检测器的未知预测流被大量背景误检污染。作者提出DualMem，一种基于冻结SigLIP特征空间的非参数似然比检验后处理过滤器，利用正负记忆库和Neyman-Pearson校准选择阈值，在不损害已知类别性能的前提下，显著降低每图像背景类假未知预测44.9%-66.3%，平均减少56.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OWOD检测器在未知物体预测中存在严重误判，尤其是背景误检占未知预测的46-71%，而真正未来任务中的正例不足10%。这并非信息缺失，而是源于物体置信度头的信息瓶颈。因此需要一种能有效分离真实未知与背景干扰的后处理方法。

Method: 提出DualMem，一种校准的后处理过滤器：利用小规模独立标注的校准集构建正样本记忆库（保护未来任务对象）和负样本记忆库（抑制背景类似提案），在冻结的SigLIP特征空间中进行k近邻似然比测试，并通过Neyman-Pearson准则确定决策阈值，实现对假未知的精准抑制。

Result: 在M-OWODB Task 1上，DualMem将背景型假未知预测减少44.9%-66.3%，平均降低56.6%；相比K-means原型基线，提升超过一倍；同时保持已知类别mAP不变，因已知检测绕过该过滤器。

Conclusion: DualMem成功缓解了OWOD中未知预测的严重污染问题，证明了在冻结特征空间中进行非参数校准的有效性，为未来增量学习提供了更可靠的未知样本筛选机制。

Abstract: Open-world object detection (OWOD) requires detectors to localize known classes while identifying unknown objects for future incremental learning. We find that the unknown prediction streams of strong OWOD detectors are heavily polluted: on M-OWODB, across PROB, OW-DETR, and HypOW, future-task positive unknowns make up less than 10% of unknown predictions, whereas background false positives account for 46-71%. We show that this is not a missing-information problem, but an information bottleneck at the objectness head. On PROB Task 1, a linear probe on the 256-D decoder query achieves an AUROC of 0.908 for positive-versus-negative unknown discrimination, but the final one-dimensional objectness scalar drops to 0.642. A frozen SigLIP feature, without access to the detector, independently recovers much of this proposal-level separability at the filtering stage (AUROC = 0.871).
  Motivated by this finding, we propose DualMem, a calibrated post-hoc filter that assumes a small image-disjoint annotated calibration split of held-out future-task objects and performs a non-parametric likelihood ratio test in frozen SigLIP feature space. DualMem uses a k-nearest-neighbor positive memory to protect future-task objects and a negative memory to suppress background-like proposals. Its decision threshold is chosen by Neyman-Pearson calibration, giving users an explicit trade-off between false-unknown suppression and novel recall.
  Across PROB, OW-DETR, and HypOW on M-OWODB Task 1, DualMem reduces background-type false unknown proposals per image by 44.9%-66.3%, with a mean reduction of 56.6%. On PROB Task 1, it more than doubles the reduction achieved by a natural K-means prototype baseline, while leaving known-class mAP unchanged because known detections bypass the filter.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉搜索方法在覆盖率与效率之间存在权衡：专家辅助搜索虽高效但易遗漏信息，而扫描式搜索虽全面却计算冗余且语义碎片化。为解决这一矛盾，需一种既能保障覆盖又高效灵活的搜索机制。

Abstract: High-resolution (HR) image perception presents a key bottleneck for multimodal large language models (MLLMs). While visual search offers a promising solution, existing methods struggle with the trade-off between coverage and efficiency. Visual expert-assisted search is efficient but prone to blind spots when proposals fail, whereas scan-based search guarantees coverage at the cost of computational redundancy and semantic fragmentation. To address this dilemma, we introduce CVSearch, a training-free adaptive framework that dynamically schedules search strategies via an Assess-then-Search workflow. Specifically, CVSearch first invokes expert-assisted search when global information is insufficient, and only triggers a novel semantic-aware scanning mechanism upon failure. Distinct from rigid grid partitioning, this efficient scanning paradigm incorporates Semantic Guided Adaptive Patching to decompose images into semantically consistent regions, effectively mitigating object fragmentation. Furthermore, we devise a Dynamic Bottom-Up Search strategy driven by a Visual Complexity prior to enable efficient and precise iterative exploration of local details. Extensive experiments on HR benchmarks demonstrate that CVSearch achieves state-of-the-art accuracy while substantially improving search efficiency. Code is released at https://github.com/liliupeng28/ICML26-CVSearch.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Rigid-aware 4D Gaussian Splatting (RiGS)，包含静态、刚性与瞬态三类高斯原语；设计对象级动态掩码以聚合长程时空运动信息；通过基于时间持续性的刚性到瞬态高斯转换机制，结合场景流监督，实现多尺度运动联合建模。

Abstract: Reconstructing dynamic 3D scenes from monocular videos is a fundamental yet highly challenging task, as real-world motions often involve both long-term smooth transformations and short-term complex deformations. Existing methods either struggle to maintain temporal consistency or fail to capture high-frequency dynamics due to limited motion modeling capacity. In this work, we present Rigid-aware 4D Gaussian Splatting (RiGS), which simultaneously captures motions across multiple temporal scales. Specifically, RiGS introduces three types of Gaussian primitives: static, rigid, and transient, which represent static backgrounds, long-term low-frequency motions, and short-term high-frequency dynamics, respectively. An object-wise dynamic mask is proposed to aggregate long-range spatiotemporal motion information and guide the decomposition of static and dynamic regions. To jointly model motion across scales, rigid Gaussians are allowed to transition into transient Gaussians based on their temporal duration, and both are optimized under scene flow guidance, providing dense 3D motion supervision. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RiGS achieves state-of-the-art performance on novel view synthesis benchmarks. ### [54] [CRONOS: Benchmarking Counterfactual Physical Consistency in Video Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23699)
*León Begiristain,Olaf Dünkel,Adam Kortylewski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CRONOS是一个基于干预的基准测试，用于评估视频生成模型在物理事件上的反事实一致性，通过控制视角、场景、物体类别和外观等变量来检验模型是否理解因果结构而非仅依赖视觉相关性。实验发现现有模型在这些干预下表现不稳定，尤其对视角变化敏感，表明其缺乏真正的物理理解。该基准提供了一个可控、可复现的测试平台，推动开发更鲁棒的视频生成模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视频预测模型可能仅依赖表面视觉相关性进行未来预测，而非学习真实的因果物理结构，因此需要一种能够有效评估模型对物理事件理解能力的基准测试。

Method: 构建一个基于Unreal Engine的高保真视频生成环境，系统性地对视角、场景、物体类别和外观四类因素进行干预，同时保持物理事件类型（如碰撞、遮挡、掉落）不变，以评估模型预测的一致性。

Result: 大多数开源视频生成模型在面对不同干预条件时表现出显著性能下降，特别是在视角变化下，说明它们未能真正理解底层物理规律，而是依赖于特定视觉特征。

Conclusion: CRONOS为评估视频生成模型的反事实物理一致性提供了有效的工具，有助于推动开发具备更强泛化能力和因果理解的通用世界模型。

Abstract: Video prediction is increasingly viewed as a path toward generalizable world models, yet it remains unclear whether these systems learn underlying causal structure or merely exploit superficial visual correlations for future prediction. We introduce CRONOS, an intervention-based benchmark designed to evaluate counterfactual physical consistency: whether a model's predictions of physical events respond appropriately to controlled changes in the visual input, such as variations of scene context, viewpoint, object appearance, and object category. Built in a photorealistic Unreal Engine environment, CRONOS enables controlled, high-fidelity generation of videos across diverse scenes and dynamics. In contrast to previous benchmarks, CRONOS systematically intervenes on four key factors - viewpoint, scene, object category, and object appearance - while keeping the underlying physical event type, such as a collision, occlusion, or fall, fixed. Our evaluation of recent open-source video generators reveals substantial failures in counterfactual physical consistency: prediction quality for the same physical event type is affected by appearance, environment, and, particularly by viewpoint changes. CRONOS provides a controlled and reproducible testbed for diagnosing how the quality of generated videos changes for different interventions, establishing a concrete target for developing models that perform consistently across changes of multiple conditions. The dataset and code are available at our project page.

### [55] [Weierstrass Positional Encoding for Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23719)
*Zhihang Xin,Rui Wang,Xitong Hu,Xiaojun Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于魏尔斯特拉斯椭圆函数的二维位置编码方法WePE，通过复数域映射实现图像块坐标的紧凑四维特征表示，利用双周期性和晶格结构自然匹配图像网格几何，有效建模空间距离关系并支持任意两块间的相对位置推导。该方法即插即用且分辨率无关，在不增加计算或内存开销的情况下显著提升ViT性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉变换器（ViT）使用可学习的一维位置编码，弱化了图像在分块后固有的二维空间结构；传统位置编码缺乏几何约束，无法保持欧氏空间距离与序列索引距离之间的单调关系，限制了对空间邻近先验的利用。

Method: 将归一化的二维图像块坐标映射到复平面，利用魏尔斯特拉斯椭圆函数及其导数构建紧凑的四维位置特征。该方法具有双周期性，能以代数加法公式直接推导任意两块间的相对位置信息。

Result: 大量实验表明，WePE在多数设置下均带来一致的性能提升；通过预计算查找表，改进无额外计算或内存开销。消融研究和额外分析进一步验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: WePE是一种数学上严谨、可即插即用、分辨率无关的位置编码方法，能够更准确地建模二维空间关系，显著增强视觉变换器的空间感知能力。

Abstract: Vision Transformers have achieved remarkable success in computer vision, but their common use of learnable one-dimensional positional encodings weakens the inherent two-dimensional spatial structure of images after patch flattening. Existing positional encodings often lack geometric constraints and do not preserve a monotonic relationship between Euclidean spatial distances and sequential index distances, limiting ViTs' ability to exploit spatial proximity priors. Motivated by the usefulness of periodicity in positional encoding, we propose Weierstrass elliptic Positional Encoding (WePE), a mathematically grounded method for encoding two-dimensional coordinates in the complex domain. WePE maps normalized 2D patch coordinates onto the complex plane and constructs compact four-dimensional positional features using the Weierstrass elliptic function and its derivative. The double periodicity provides a principled representation of 2D positions, and its intrinsic lattice structure naturally matches the regular geometry of image patch grids. Its nonlinear geometric properties help model spatial distance relationships more faithfully, while the algebraic addition formula enables relative positional information between arbitrary patch pairs to be derived directly from their absolute encodings. WePE is plug-and-play and resolution-agnostic, allowing seamless integration into existing ViTs. Extensive experiments show that WePE brings consistent performance gains in most settings. With precomputed lookup tables, these improvements introduce no noticeable computational or memory overhead. Additional analyses and ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of the proposed method.

### [56] [Decomposing Queries into Tool Calls for Long-Video Keyframe Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23826)
*Michal Shlapentokh-Rothman,Prachi Garg,Yu-Xiong Wang,Derek Hoiem*

TL;DR: 提出ToolMerge方法，通过大语言模型分解问题并合并多工具结果，用于长视频问答中的关键帧选择。构建M2M基准测试，验证其在多种任务上的性能，尤其在字幕检索上优于其他方法5%。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关键帧选择方法要么对每个问题评分所有帧，要么使用固定模式评估单一视觉工具，无法灵活适应不同查询需求。需要一种能根据问题动态分解并整合多工具结果的方法。

Method: 使用基于LLM的规划器将问题分解为工具调用，并指定如何用布尔运算合并各工具的排名结果，实现更精准的关键帧检索。

Result: 在问答、问题检索和字幕检索任务中表现良好，尤其在字幕检索上比其他方法高出5%，证明了该方法的有效性与竞争力。

Conclusion: ToolMerge通过智能分解与融合策略，显著提升了关键帧选择的准确性与灵活性，适用于多样化视频理解任务。

Abstract: Keyframe selection is a direct way to provide verifiable visual evidence for long-video question answering (QA). Queries differ in what they require, and finding the right frames depends on knowing what to look for. Existing keyframe selectors either score every frame against a single query, or decompose the query into a fixed schema evaluated by a single visual tool. We propose ToolMerge, a keyframe retrieval method based on decomposition and merging: an Large Language Model (LLM) based planner decomposes the query into tool calls and specifies how their per-tool rankings are merged using boolean operators. To evaluate retrieval directly, we construct Molmo-2 Moments (M2M), a benchmark in which every question is anchored to a specific time interval by construction. Across QA, question retrieval, and caption retrieval, ToolMerge is competitive with prior keyframe selectors, most notably on caption retrieval, outperforming other methods by 5%. Code and data can be found at https://github.com/michalsr/ToolMerge .

### [57] [Revitalizing Dense Material Segmentation: Stabilized Vision Transformers and the Generalization Paradox](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23747)
*Allan Kazakov,Duygu Cakir,Hilal Kurt İrfanoğlu,Yavuz İrfanoğlu*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出包含高保真对数投影、查询熵正则化及领域特定物理合规增强的稳定训练方案；评估SegFormer与Mask2Former架构，优化SegFormer-B5模型性能。

Conclusion: 材料感知仍远未解决，当前进展受限于评估偏差。应坚持使用原始严格数据划分，避免虚假性能提升，以推动真正具有物理根基的人工智能研究。

Abstract: Material segmentation, the pixel-wise classification of physical surface properties, remains a challenging problem in computer vision, requiring physicochemical understanding distinct from object-centric parsing. Despite the introduction of the rigorous Apple Dense Material Segmentation (DMS) dataset, the benchmark has suffered from attrition and stagnation, increasingly overshadowed by geometry-biased foundation models. In this paper, we revive the Apple-DMS benchmark to establish a modern Vision Transformer baseline. We conduct an exhaustive evaluation of SegFormer and Mask2Former architectures, revealing that standard training paradigms fail on amorphous texture fields due to high-variance gradients. To address this, we introduce a stabilized training recipe featuring High-Fidelity Logit Projection, Query Entropy Regularization, and a domain-specific, physics-compliant augmentation pipeline. Our optimized SegFormer-B5 achieves a new State-of-the-Art (SOTA) of 0.4572 mIoU on the original dataset split, significantly surpassing the prior convolutional baseline. Furthermore, we identify a critical "Generalization Paradox": while re-partitioning the dataset into a data-rich 80/10/10 split inflates the metric to 0.5276 mIoU, expert qualitative analysis reveals this induces distributional homogenization, severely degrading real-world, out-of-distribution performance. By releasing our recovered dataset index and robust training framework, we demonstrate that material perception is far from solved and urge the community to leverage the rigorous original split to drive genuine progress in physically grounded artificial intelligence.

### [58] [ETCHR: Editing To Clarify and Harness Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23897)
*Beichen Zhang,Yuhong Liu,Jinsong Li,Yuhang Zang,Jiaqi Wang,Dahua Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ETCHR introduces a reasoning-aware image editor that decouples image editing from understanding models, improving visual reasoning in multimodal LLMs by addressing language and generation gaps in off-the-shelf editors. It uses two-stage training: reasoning imitation via supervised fine-tuning and reasoning enhancement with VLM-derived rewards. ETCHR boosts Pass@1 scores across multiple tasks and models without requiring retraining.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing multimodal reasoning methods are limited by textual chain-of-thought bottlenecks or noisy image edits from unified models. Off-the-shelf image editors fail as reasoning assistants due to poor mapping of abstract questions to visual transformations and declining edit quality with deeper reasoning.

Method: ETCHR employs a decoupled architecture with a dedicated image editing model trained in two stages: (1) Reasoning Imitation via supervised fine-tuning on edit trajectories, and (2) Reasoning Enhancement using VLM-derived rewards for edit correctness and downstream reasoning accuracy. The editor is training-free when integrated into different MLLMs.

Result: ETCHR improves Pass@1 performance by +4.82 (Qwen3-VL-8B), +5.47 (Gemini-3.1-Flash-Lite), and +4.61 (Kimi K2.5) across five task families: fine-grained perception, chart understanding, logic reasoning, jigsaw restoration, and 3D understanding.

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models have advanced visual reasoning, yet a purely textual chain of thought remains a bottleneck for questions that require fine-grained focus or view transformations. The ''think with images'' paradigm narrows this gap, but existing approaches are either constrained by fixed predefined toolkits or produce noisy intermediate images from unified multimodal methods. We pursue a third option: using a dedicated image editing model and decouple it with an understanding model. However, off-the-shelf image editors fail as reasoning assistants with two complementary gaps: a language-side gap, where editors trained as passive instruction-followers cannot map an abstract question to an appropriate visual transformation, and a generation-side gap, where edit correctness degrades as reasoning depth grows. Guided by this analysis, we introduce ETCHR (Editing To Clarify and Harness Reasoning), a question-conditioned, reasoning-aware image editor decoupled from the downstream understanding model and trained with a two-stage recipe targeted at the two gaps: Reasoning Imitation via supervised fine-tuning on edit trajectories, followed by Reasoning Enhancement with VLM-derived rewards for edit correctness and downstream reasoning accuracy. Since the editor is decoupled, ETCHR plugs into different open- and closed-source MLLMs in a training-free manner. Across five task families (fine-grained perception, chart understanding, logic reasoning, jigsaw restoration, and 3D understanding), ETCHR raises average Pass@1 from 55.95 to 60.77 (+4.82) with Qwen3-VL-8B, from 65.08 to 70.55 (+5.47) with Gemini-3.1-Flash-Lite, and from 76.55 to 81.16 (+4.61) with the 1T-parameter MoE model Kimi K2.5.

### [60] [Not Too Generative, Not Too Discriminative: The Human Alignment Sweet Spot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23819)
*Jorge Chang Ortega,Bastien Le Lan,Thomas Serre,Victor Boutin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究通过使用联合能量模型（JEMs）在固定架构下连续插值生成式与判别式学习，隔离学习目标的影响。结果表明，在多个涉及感知相似性、光泽感知、人类反应不确定性等的人类对齐基准测试中，中间混合点的模型表现最佳，说明生成式与判别式学习的平衡比单一目标更能产生类人视觉表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究常将学习目标与架构、规模、训练数据混淆，难以判断学习目标本身是否驱动人类对齐。本研究旨在分离学习目标的影响，明确其在形成类人视觉表征中的作用。

Method: 采用联合能量模型（JEMs），通过调节单一混合系数，在固定架构下连续切换生成式与判别式学习，从而隔离学习目标的影响，并在六项人类对齐基准上评估模型表现。

Result: 在所有评估任务中，人类对齐度在生成式与判别式学习的中间混合点达到峰值，而非两端；混合模型结合了判别式学习的类别结构和生成式学习对输入结构的敏感性，表现出更接近人类的视觉行为。

Conclusion: 人类对齐的视觉表征并非来自选择生成式或判别式学习之一，而是源于两者的平衡。因此，生成式与判别式二分法不是理解类人视觉的关键轴线，关键在于两者的协同作用。

Abstract: A central question in computational vision is whether human-like visual representations are better explained by discriminative or generative learning. Existing comparisons, however, often confound the learning objective with architecture, scale, and training data, leaving open whether the objective itself drives alignment. We address this confound using Joint Energy-Based Models (JEMs), which interpolate continuously between discriminative and generative training within a fixed architecture. By varying a single mixing coefficient, we isolate the effect of the learning objective and evaluate the resulting models across six human-alignment benchmarks spanning perceptual similarity, gloss perception, human response uncertainty, robustness, shape-texture cue conflict, and diagnostic feature attribution. Across this diverse suite, human alignment is consistently maximized at intermediate points of the generative-discriminative continuum, rather than at either endpoint. Hybrid JEMs combine the categorical structure induced by discriminative learning with the sensitivity to input structure induced by generative learning, yielding more human-like behavior across multiple levels of vision. These results suggest that the generative-discriminative dichotomy is the wrong axis for understanding human-aligned vision: alignment emerges not from choosing one objective over the other, but from balancing both.

Abstract: Data-driven learning approaches for physics simulation, sometimes referred to as world models, have emerged as promising alternatives to traditional physics simulators due to their differentiable nature. Prior work has demonstrated impressive results in predicting the motions of rigid and non-rigid objects in complex scenes involving multiple interacting bodies. However, these models are typically trained in simulated environments because obtaining perfect state information such as complete scene point clouds and point correspondences over time is challenging in real-world settings. This reliance on synthetic data can limit their applicability when the sim-to-real gap is large. In this work, we aim to overcome these limitations by introducing a novel framework for training neural object dynamics models directly from unlabeled real-world videos. Specifically, we propose to learn a particle-based dynamics model compatible with a Gaussian splatting framework, which operates on dense particles derived from Gaussians (i.e., particles with scales and rotations) and predicts their position and rotation changes over time. The model is trained via rendering supervision, enabling learning from real-world videos without requiring particle-level labeled states. ### [62] [Vision Transformers Need Better Token Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23868)
*Linxiang Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文研究了视觉变压器（ViT）在长期训练中密集预测性能下降的现象，提出‘语义扩散’是主要原因之一，即全局语义信息过度传播至局部补丁。作者认为不应完全消除全局上下文，而应使令牌交互更具有选择性。为此，采用稀疏注意力（entmax-1.5）替代标准softmax注意力，在保持全局连接的同时减少冗余信息传播。实验表明，该方法在ImageNet线性探测任务上保持精度，同时显著提升语义分割性能：VOC mIoU从42.80提升至48.78，ADE20K从19.85升至21.97，Cityscapes从36.79增至37.87。结果证明，选择性令牌混合是一种简单有效的改进密集ViT表示的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究认为视觉变压器在长期训练中出现的密集预测性能下降主要由高范数伪影引起，但本文认为这一解释不充分；观察发现浅层特征虽更贴近前景区域，却仍不如深层特征表现好，且[CLS]标记始终对密集预测有互补作用，说明问题核心并非全局上下文本身，而是其传播方式缺乏选择性。因此需要探索如何让令牌间交互更加精准。

Method: 提出使用entmax-1.5作为稀疏注意力机制替代传统的softmax注意力，以实现选择性令牌混合。该方法保留了模型的全局连接能力，但通过引入稀疏性抑制非必要信息传播，从而缓解语义扩散问题。

Result: 在DINOv1 ViT-S/16模型上训练200个epoch后，使用entmax-1.5的模型在保持ImageNet线性探测准确率的同时，大幅提升了多个语义分割数据集的表现：VOC mIoU提升至48.78，ADE20K提升至21.97，Cityscapes提升至37.87，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 语义扩散是导致密集预测性能下降的重要因素，而通过引入稀疏注意力（如entmax-1.5）实现选择性令牌混合，可在不破坏全局连通性的前提下有效改善视觉变压器的密集表示能力，为未来设计高效、鲁棒的视觉模型提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) can learn strong image-level representations while their patch representations become less effective for dense prediction during prolonged training. We revisit this dense degradation phenomenon and argue that it is not fully explained by high-norm artifacts alone. Instead, we characterize \emph{semantic diffusion}: an optimization shortcut in which global semantic information spreads through patch tokens beyond what is locally justified. Our analysis shows that dense representation quality is not captured by locality alone: shallow features can remain better aligned with foreground regions yet underperform deeper features, and \texttt{[CLS]} features remain complementary for dense prediction. These observations suggest that the goal should not be to remove global context, but to make token interactions more selective. We therefore study sparse attention as a minimal intervention, replacing softmax attention with entmax-1.5 while preserving global token connectivity. On DINOv1 ViT-S/16 trained for 200 epochs on ImageNet-1K, this change preserves ImageNet linear probing accuracy and substantially improves semantic segmentation performance: VOC mIoU increases from 42.80 to 48.78, ADE20K from 19.85 to 21.97, and Cityscapes from 36.79 to 37.87. These results suggest that selective token mixing is a simple and effective bias for improving dense ViT representations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成模型在物理和运动一致性方面表现不足，而依赖外部模拟器或教师模型的方法存在局限性，因此需要一种无需额外标注或外部监督的自监督解决方案。

Method: LaMo构建了一个基于当前潜在表示和提示的帧间潜在变化的潜在运动先验，通过两个轻量级组件实现：训练阶段的运动漂移损失（Motion Drift Loss）和采样阶段的运动先验引导（Motion Prior Guidance），二者可无缝集成到现有视频扩散模型中。

Conclusion: 未标注视频中蕴含丰富的运动监督信号，可通过自监督方式有效提升现代视频扩散模型的物理真实性和运动一致性。

Abstract: Modern video generators produce visually compelling clips but still struggle with physical and motion consistency, limiting their use as reliable world simulators. Existing remedies often rely on external simulators, teacher models, or curated physics-focused data. We explore a complementary self-supervised direction: extracting motion cues from the unlabeled videos already used to train video diffusion models. We propose LaMo, which formulates a latent motion prior over frame-to-frame latent changes conditioned on the current latent and prompt. This prior is exposed through two lightweight readouts: a macro motion drift used during training as a Motion Drift Loss, and a learned micro motion field used during sampling as Motion Prior Guidance. Both components are plug-and-play with existing video diffusion backbones, requiring no architectural or I/O changes. On VideoPhy and VideoPhy2, LaMo improves CogVideoX backbones and outperforms recent physics-aware baselines that use external supervision. On VBench, it preserves overall generation quality while improving motion-related dimensions. These results suggest that unlabeled video contains useful motion supervision for improving physical fidelity in modern video diffusion models.

### [64] [PGT: Procedurally Generated Tasks for improving visual grounding in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23883)
*Rim Assouel,Amir Bar,Michal Drozdzal,Adriana Romero-Soriano*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为程序生成任务（PGT）的数据驱动框架，旨在提升多模态大模型在细粒度视觉理解任务中的表现，并作为低成本诊断工具识别感知失败的根源。通过在图像上叠加清晰的几何图形，PGT提供密集监督信号，将视觉定位能力与语义先验解耦。实验表明，PGT在多种架构和基准测试中均带来显著性能提升，如在What'sUp和CV-Bench-2D上分别实现最高+20%和+13.3%的改进，且不损害模型通用感知能力。研究揭示，空间推理缺陷主要源于监督信号不足，而非模型架构或分辨率限制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型在细粒度视觉理解任务中仍表现不佳，尤其在空间关系、数量判断和三维/深度理解方面存在明显短板。现有方法缺乏有效的细粒度监督信号，导致模型难以准确进行视觉定位与推理。因此亟需一种能提供密集、明确监督的新方法，以增强模型对细微视觉特征的理解能力，并帮助诊断其感知失败的原因。

Method: 提出程序生成任务（PGT）框架，通过在图像上自动叠加清晰、无歧义的几何形状（如圆形、矩形、线条等），生成具有精确位置和关系标注的合成数据。这些数据为模型提供密集的视觉定位监督，有效分离视觉感知与语义先验之间的耦合。随后将该数据用于指令微调或进一步微调现有MLLMs，从而提升其在细粒度理解任务上的表现。

Result: 在多个细粒度理解基准测试（包括What'sUp、CV-Bench-2D等）上，使用PGT数据训练后的模型表现出显著提升：指令微调后最大提升达+20%（What'sUp）和+13.3%（CV-Bench-2D）；直接微调先进模型也获得最高+5.5%（What'sUp）和+8.3%（CV-Bench-2D）的增益。同时，模型的通用感知能力保持不变。结果证明，细粒度感知瓶颈主要来自监督信号不足，而非模型结构或分辨率限制。

Conclusion: PGT是一种高效、低成本且可扩展的框架，能够有效提升多模态大模型在细粒度视觉理解任务中的表现。它不仅增强了模型对几何关系、数量和深度信息的敏感性，还为诊断感知缺陷提供了有力工具。研究结果表明，通过增加高质量、密集的视觉监督信号，可以显著缓解空间推理问题，为未来多模态模型的设计与训练提供新方向。

Abstract: Despite remarkable progress in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), these models still struggle with fine-grained understanding tasks. In this work, we propose Procedurally Generated Tasks (PGT), a simple data-driven framework that serves a dual purpose: inducing fine-grained visual understanding and acting as a low-cost diagnostic tool to identify the source of perception failures. By overlaying unambiguous geometric primitives on images, PGT generate additional dense supervision that disentangles visual grounding capability from semantic priors. Extensive experiments on relational, quantitative, and 3D/depth understanding benchmarks show that PGT yields remarkable gains across diverse architectures. Instruction tuning MLLMs on LLaVA-v1.5-Instruct augmented with PGT data results in improvements of up to +20% on the What'sUp benchmark and +13.3% on CV-Bench-2D, while maintaining general perception capabilities. Moreover, finetuning state-of-the-art MLLMs on PGT data leads to boosts of up to +5.5% on What'sUp and +8.3% on CV-Bench-2D. These findings demonstrate that PGT effectively address the bottleneck of fine-grained perception, revealing that many spatial reasoning deficits stem from inadequate supervision signals rather than inherent architectural or resolution limitations.

</details>


### [65] [GenRecon: Bridging Generative Priors for Multi-View 3D Scene Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23888)

Abstract: We introduce a new approach to high-fidelity 3D scene reconstruction from multi-view RGB images that tightly couples reconstruction with a strong generative 3D prior. We cast scene reconstruction as conditional 3D generation over a set of spatially-localized, overlapping chunks that together tile the scene, scaling generation to large scene extents. Crucially, we inherit the fidelity and completeness of state-of-the-art generative shape models -- we use Trellis.2 as an example -- which we generalize to the scene level. To this end, we propose a projection-based conditioning mechanism that lifts posed multi-view image features into a coherent 3D representation aligned with the generative model, independent of view ordering and spatially anchored to the scene, yielding high-fidelity, multi-view consistent generated geometry. This enables lifting the strong object-level prior of Trellis.2 to multi-view, scene-scale generation, producing faithful, editable PBR mesh reconstructions of indoor environments. ### [66] [HorizonStream: Long-Horizon Attention for Streaming 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23889)
*Chong Cheng,Peilin Tao,Nanjie Yao,Guanzhi Ding,Xianda Chen,Yuansen Du,Xiaoyang Guo,Wei Yin,Weiqiang Ren,Qian Zhang,Zhengqing Chen,Hao Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HorizonStream 是一种用于长时序 3D 重建的新型 Transformer 模型，通过显式分解几何传播中的证据影响核，解决现有方法在长时间序列中出现的漂移、抖动和崩溃问题。它采用几何线性注意力（Geometric Linear Attention）实现多时间尺度的稳定几何证据传播，结合时空旋转位置编码的局部注意力机制（Geometric Local Attention）提升匹配可靠性，并通过度量读出令牌恢复稳定的尺度与刚性位姿。该模型仅用 48 帧片段训练，即可在超过 10,000 帧的序列上保持恒定内存与线性时间复杂度，性能达到当前最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线 3D 重建方法在长序列中易出现漂移、抖动或崩溃，根源在于其架构对时间异质性的几何证据传播施加了统一且病态的影响模式，如滑动窗口的硬截断、无门控递归和因果注意力导致的缓存饱和与注意力尖峰。

Method: 提出将几何传播建模为证据影响核，设计 HorizonStream 模型：利用几何线性注意力学习通道级衰减率以实现多时间尺度的有界传播；采用带时空旋转位置编码的几何局部注意力进行可靠的 3D 匹配并抑制注意力尖峰；通过度量读出令牌直接从持久几何状态中恢复稳定尺度与刚性位姿。

Result: HorizonStream 在仅使用 48 帧训练数据的情况下，可稳定泛化至超 10,000 帧的长序列，保持常数内存占用与线性时间复杂度，显著优于现有方法，在流式 3D 重建任务中达到最新技术水平。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模几何证据的时间-空间异质传播特性，HorizonStream 成功解决了长期在线 3D 重建中的稳定性难题，为大规模、实时场景重建提供了高效且鲁棒的新范式。

Abstract: Online 3D reconstruction requires estimating camera pose and scene geometry under strict causal and bounded-memory constraints. Existing methods often suffer from drift, jitter, or collapse on long sequences. We trace these failures to a fundamental mismatch. Streaming geometry is inherently temporally heterogeneous, with evidence ranging from short-lived correspondences to persistent global scale. However, current architectures impose uniform and pathological influence patterns. For example, sliding windows enforce hard cutoffs, while ungated recurrence and causal attention cause cache saturation and spike-like attention sinks. To resolve this, we formalize geometric propagation as an \emph{evidence influence kernel} and propose HorizonStream, a long-horizon Transformer that explicitly factorizes this kernel. For the long-range temporal factor, Geometric Linear Attention learns channel-wise decay rates to enable bounded, multi-timescale propagation of geometric evidence. For the short-range spatial factor, Geometric Local Attention with Spatiotemporal RoPE performs reliable 3D matching while suppressing attention sinks. Finally, Metric Readout Tokens recover stable scale and rigid pose directly from the persistent geometric state. Extensive experiments show that HorizonStream, trained on only 48-frame clips, generalizes stably to sequences exceeding 10,000\ frames with constant memory and linear time, achieving state-of-the-art streaming 3D reconstruction performance. Project Page: https://3dagentworld.github.io/horizonstream/

Within this framework, the image stream synchronously guides the video generation process, while a \textbf{Closed-loop Feedback} mechanism is further incorporated to ensure robust insertion. Inevitably, integrating these diverse conditioning signals results in feature entanglement and style leakage. To tackle this issue, we design \textbf{Dual-World-View RoPE} to distinguish different signals via spatial-temporal offsets without incurring heavy training overhead. Furthermore, to facilitate spatial grounding and stylistic adaptation, we introduce a \textbf{Decoupled Guidance Module} that leverages a Vision-Language Model for semantic reasoning while preserving original temporal guidance with native text encoder. ### [68] [Good Token Hunting: A Hitchhiker's Guide to Token Selection for Visual Geometry Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23892)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两阶段令牌选择框架：1）跨帧选择，基于多样性策略筛选关键帧；2）帧内选择，采用层感知稀疏化并依据全局注意力熵进行冗余令牌剔除。

Result: 在500张图像的场景下，模型推理速度提升超过85%，同时保持或提升基线性能，验证了所提策略在速度-精度平衡上的优越性。

Conclusion: 所提出的令牌选择策略能有效缓解视觉几何变换器的计算瓶颈，具有良好的通用性和扩展性，对未来多视图3D重建应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Visual geometry transformers have become powerful architectures for multi-view 3D reconstruction, enabling joint prediction of multiple 3D attributes in a feed-forward manner. However, their computational cost grows quadratically with the input sequence length due to the global attention layers inside these models. This limits both their scalability and efficiency. In this work, we address this challenge with a simple yet general strategy: restricting the number of key/value tokens that each query interacts with during global attention. To achieve effective token selection, we introduce a two-stage framework. First, an inter-frame selection step operates at the frame level to identify frames that should be preserved. Second, an intra-frame selection step further discards more redundant tokens within the selected frames. Our analysis highlights the advantage of a diversity-based strategy for inter-frame selection, which ensures broad coverage of the scene. For intra-frame selection, we show that layer-aware sparsification is necessary, with the selection process guided by the entropy of the global attention pattern. Our approach offers a superior speed-accuracy trade-off compared to existing solutions. Extensive experiments show that it accelerates visual geometry transformers by over 85% for scenes with 500 images while maintaining, or even improving, baseline performance, which hints that how our token selection strategy can play a crucial role in future applications of visual geometry transformers. Our project website is available at https://zsh2000.github.io/good-token-hunting.github.io.

### [69] [From Activation to Causality: Discovery of Causal Visual Representations in the Human Brain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23895)
*Yuval Golbari,Navve Wasserman,Matias Cosarinsky,Roman Beliy,Aude Oliva,Antonio Torralba,Michal Irani,Tamar Rott Shaham*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BrainCause 是一种结合生成模型与脑成像模型的自动化框架，用于通过因果测试验证视觉概念在人脑中的神经表征。该方法通过生成目标概念图像、移除目标概念的反事实图像以及包含潜在相关干扰项的图像，利用图像到fMRI的编码模型预测脑响应，识别仅对目标概念特异性响应的脑区。实验表明，仅依赖激活强度会引入大量假阳性结果，而本方法可有效识别真实表征并提出后续实验建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅基于激活强度定位脑区，但强激活不等于概念表征，可能由相关视觉或语义线索引起。因此需要更严格的因果验证来确定哪些脑区真正代表特定概念。

Method: BrainCause 构建包含目标概念图像、反事实编辑图像（移除目标概念但保留其他内容）和候选干扰项图像的刺激集；使用图像到fMRI的编码模型预测脑响应；搜索对目标概念特异性响应且对相关干扰不敏感的脑区，实现因果验证。

Result: 成功复现已知功能定位，并发现多个新候选表征；在预测和实测fMRI数据上均表现良好；证明无因果验证时大量定位为假阳性，说明激活强度不足以作为表征证据。

Conclusion: BrainCause 提供了一种可靠的方法来验证视觉概念在大脑中的真实神经表征，强调了因果推理在认知神经科学中的重要性，为未来研究提供了可扩展的框架和实验指导。

Abstract: Identifying which brain regions represent a visual concept in the human brain is a central challenge in neuroscience. Existing approaches have localized coarse functional regions (e.g., faces, places) through activation maximization, identifying regions that activate strongly for a target concept relative to other concepts. Yet strong activation alone does not establish that a region represents the concept itself, as responses may instead be driven by correlated visual or semantic cues. We introduce BrainCause, an automated framework that combines generative and brain models to synthesize controlled stimuli and validate neural representations through targeted causal testing. Given a query specifying a concept of interest, our framework constructs targeted stimulus sets comprising concept images, counterfactual edits that remove the target concept while preserving other image content, and images with candidate correlated distractors. It then uses an image-to-fMRI encoding model to predict brain responses and searches for representations that respond specifically to the target concept over correlated alternatives. BrainCause returns validated candidate representations and proposes follow-up fMRI experiments to further test or extend its discoveries. Our approach successfully recovers known functional localizations and identifies new candidate representations across dozens of concepts, validated on both predicted and measured fMRI data. Critically, we show that without causal validation, a large fraction of localizations would be false positives, confirming that activation alone is insufficient evidence of representation.

### [70] [PiD: Fast and High-Resolution Latent Decoding with Pixel Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23902)
*Yifan Lu,Qi Wu,Jay Zhangjie Wu,Zian Wang,Huan Ling,Sanja Fidler,Xuanchi Ren*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PiD提出一种新的像素扩散解码器，将潜在空间解码重构为条件像素扩散，实现高效高分辨率图像生成。通过直接在像素空间去噪，可实现4×至8×超分辨率，仅需4步推理，支持多种潜在表示，速度比现有方法快6倍且质量更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高分辨率文本到图像系统依赖重建导向的解码器，其在百万像素尺度下效率低下且难以生成细节。需要更高效、更具表现力的解码范式。

Method: 引入PiD（Pixel diffusion Decoder），将解码过程建模为条件像素扩散；采用轻量级sigma感知适配器注入噪声潜变量，支持早期终止潜在扩散；结合DMD2进行模型蒸馏，压缩推理步骤至4步。

Result: PiD可在1秒内将512×512潜在表示解码为2048×2048像素，峰值内存仅13GB（RTX 5090），GB200上最快达210ms，较级联扩散超分方法快6倍，视觉质量更优。

Conclusion: PiD统一了解码与上采样，以极低延迟实现高质量高分辨率图像生成，适用于多种潜在空间表示，是高效解码的新范式。

Abstract: Most practical high-resolution text-to-image systems, including latent diffusion and autoregressive models, perform generation in a compact latent space, and a decoder maps the generated latents back to pixels. Yet the latent-to-pixel decoder is reconstruction-oriented, optimized to invert the encoder rather than synthesize more details, and becomes increasingly costly at megapixel scale. This drawback calls for a more expressive and efficient decoding paradigm. Motivated by recent progress in scalable pixel-space diffusion, we introduce PiD, a Pixel diffusion Decoder that reformulates latent decoding as conditional pixel diffusion, unifying decoding and upsampling into one generative module. By denoising directly in high-resolution pixel space, PiD synthesizes $4\times$ and even $8\times$ upscaled images with low latency. For latent conditioning, a lightweight sigma-aware adapter injects noise-corrupted latents into the pixel diffusion backbone, enabling PiD to decode partially denoised latents and terminate the latent diffusion process early. To further improve efficiency, we distill the model using DMD2, reducing inference to just 4 steps. PiD applies to both conventional VAE latents and semantic latents (e.g., SigLIP, DINOv2) used in recent RAE-based models. PiD decodes latents of $512 \times 512$ images into $2048 \times 2048$ pixels in under 1 second with 13 GB peak memory on a consumer RTX 5090, and as fast as 210 ms on a GB200 GPU, about $6\times$ faster than cascaded diffusion-based super-resolution pipelines with better visual fidelity.

### [71] [Geo-Align: Video Generation Alignment via Metric Geometry Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23903)

Method: 提出Geo-Align框架，基于预训练模型，采用尺度感知的感知奖励机制进行强化学习优化；引入3D估测器提取生成视频中的相机轨迹，对旋转和平移偏差进行惩罚；设计基于真实条件视频与合成数据目标轨迹的数据流水线，避免依赖成对数据。

Result: Geo-Align在相机可控性和视觉保真度方面均显著优于现有监督学习方法，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: Geo-Align作为首个专为相机控制视频重渲染设计的强化学习框架，有效缓解了真实世界视频泛化难题，提升了生成视频的物理一致性与可控性。

Abstract: Camera-controlled video generation has achieved remarkable progress in recent years. However, existing video-to-video re-rendering methods primarily rely on Supervised Fine-Tuning using synthetic datasets. At present, there is an extreme scarcity of synchronized, multi-view real-world video data. Consequently, the prevailing paradigm often exhibits limited generalization when processing out-of-distribution real-world videos, with models struggling to accurately adhere to physical scales and camera trajectories. To bridge this gap, we propose Geo-Align, the first Reinforcement Learning framework specifically designed for camera-controlled video re-rendering. Built upon a pretrained model, we optimize the model through a scale-aware perceptual reward mechanism. Specifically, we introduce a metric 3D estimator to extract precise camera trajectories from generated videos, explicitly penalizing deviations in rotation and translation. Furthermore, we meticulously designed a data pipeline strategy based on real-world conditioning videos and target camera trajectories derived from synthetic data, eliminating the reliance on paired data. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Geo-Align consistently outperforms existing supervised learning baselines in both precise camera controllability and visual fidelity, indicating the effectiveness of our method.

</details>

### [72] [Knowledge Distillation for Low-Resource Open-source Text-to-SQL Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22843)
*Tianhao Qiu,Xiaojun Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种知识感知的Text-to-SQL框架，通过构建包含模式语义、缩写、业务逻辑和查询模式的任务特定知识库，在训练和推理中注入知识，生成上下文相关的合成数据并增强推理能力。在七个基准测试上验证了该方法在低资源领域设置下显著提升开源与闭源大模型的性能，增强了泛化性、鲁棒性和适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景中，高质量标注的<问题, SQL>对稀缺，尤其在领域特定数据库中；同时存在模式定义不透明、缩写、隐含业务逻辑等挑战，现有数据合成和提示技术难以生成任务特定且语义一致的示例。

Method: 构建任务特定的知识库，涵盖模式语义、缩写、业务逻辑和查询模式，并将其注入训练与推理过程；利用知识库生成多样且上下文相关的合成训练数据，并在推理时进行针对性知识检索以提升表现。

Result: 在七个基准测试（包括通用和领域特定数据集）上，该方法显著提升了开源和闭源大语言模型在Text-to-SQL任务中的性能，尤其在低资源领域设置下效果突出，提升了模型的泛化能力、鲁棒性和适应性。

Conclusion: 所提出的知识感知框架有效应对了低资源环境下Text-to-SQL的挑战，通过引入任务特定知识显著提升了模型性能，具备良好的实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Text-to-SQL converts natural language questions into executable SQL queries, enabling non-technical users to access relational databases for analytics and intelligent data services. In real-world scenarios, performance is often constrained by low-resource settings, where high-quality annotated \texttt{<question, SQL>} pairs are scarce, particularly for domain-specific databases. Additional challenges include opaque schema definitions, abbreviations, and implicit business logic that are not explicitly encoded in the schema. Existing data synthesis and prompting techniques improve coverage but often fail to produce task-specific, semantically grounded examples aligned with database constraints. To address these challenges, we propose a knowledge-aware Text-to-SQL framework that constructs task-specific knowledge base including schema semantics, abbreviations, business logic, and query patterns, and injects them into both training and inference. This framework generates diverse, contextually grounded synthetic training data and enhances inference through targeted knowledge retrieval. Experiments on seven benchmarks, covering both general and domain-specific datasets, demonstrate that our approach substantially improves the performance of open-source and closed-source large language models in Text-to-SQL tasks, especially in low-resource domain-specific settings, enhancing generalization, robustness, and adaptability.

### [73] [RAS: Reflection-Augmented Scaling with In-Context Learning for Executable Cypher Query Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22937)
*Minseok Jung,Abhas Ricky,Muhammad Rameez Chatni*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在文本到Cypher查询生成中，如何有效分配推理时计算资源以减少不可执行查询。提出Reflection-Augmented Scaling（RAS）方法，利用先前执行反馈进行上下文学习，相比独立采样（IS）方法显著降低查询执行错误率41-50%（n=5），证明执行错误是可利用的反馈信号，而非简单丢弃。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未充分探索推理时计算资源的分配策略，尤其是对不可执行查询的反馈利用不足；语法错误虽与语义不准确不同，但其错误信息可作为有用反馈提升模型性能。

Method: 对比两种推理方法：独立采样（IS）和反射增强采样（RAS）。RAS通过将先前执行的错误反馈纳入上下文学习，指导后续尝试，实现更高效的查询生成。

Result: 在三个Neo4j数据集和五种代码专用语言模型上，RAS在n=5时将查询执行错误率降低41-50%，显著优于IS的32-38%。表明基于执行反馈的推理机制更高效。

Conclusion: 执行错误不仅是失败信号，更是可利用的反馈；将推理时计算资源围绕执行反馈结构化，比单纯增加独立样本数量更能有效提升查询的可执行性。

Abstract: Inference-time scaling can reduce errors in structured query generation, but methods to allocate the compute for query code generation remains underexplored. We study Text2Cypher, where language models generate Cypher queries that execute against property graph databases. Non-executable queries constitute a distinct syntactic failure separate from semantic inaccuracy: a syntax error triggers a system-generated error message from the database. These error messages are typically discarded at inference time rather than leveraged through in-context learning (ICL). We compare two inference methods: Independent Scaling (IS), which performs memoryless resampling, and Reflection-Augmented Scaling (RAS), which conditions each new attempt on prior execution feedback via ICL. Across three Neo4j datasets and five code-specialized language models, RAS reduces the Query Execution Error Rate by 41--50% at n{=}5, outperforming IS at 32--38%. Execution errors are not merely failures to discard but actionable feedback, and structuring inference-time compute around them is a more efficient path to executability than scaling independent samples.

</details>


### [74] [Learnability-Informed Fine-Tuning of Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22939)
*Shubham Parashar,Atharv Chagi,Jacob Helwig,Lakshmi Jotsna,Sushil Vemuri,James Caverlee,Dileep Kalathil,Shuiwang Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LIFT 是一种针对扩散语言模型（DLMs）的高效 SFT 后训练算法，通过在不同扩散时间步匹配学习难度与上下文可用性，提升模型推理能力。该方法在六个推理基准上超越现有 SFT 基线，最大相对提升达 3 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 SFT 方法在 DLMs 中表现不佳，因其忽略学习难易度（learnability），即在输入被大量掩码时难以学习稀有词，在输入未被掩码时学习常见词又无实际价值。

Method: 提出 LIFT 算法，根据扩散过程中的信息可用性动态调整训练策略：在多数输入被掩码时学习容易的词，在更多上下文可用时学习困难的词，从而与扩散时间步的信息状态对齐。

Result: LIFT 在六项推理基准测试中优于现有 SFT 方法，尤其在 AIME'24 和 AIME'25 上实现最高 3 倍的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: LIFT 有效解决了 DLMs 后训练中因忽视学习难易度导致的性能下降问题，证明了与扩散时间步信息状态对齐的训练策略在提升推理能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: We aim to improve the reasoning capabilities of diffusion language models (DLMs). While SFT is a popular post-training recipe for autoregressive models, its use in DLMs faces challenges and can even hurt performance, though the underlying causes remain understudied. Our analysis reveals that vanilla SFT overlooks learnability, namely what and when tokens are learned. Specifically, rare tokens are difficult to learn when most of the input is masked, whereas it is straightforward and thus of little value to learn common tokens when most of the input is unmasked. Motivated by our analysis, we propose LIFT, an efficient SFT-based post-training algorithm for DLMs. LIFT learns easy tokens when most of the input is masked and hard tokens when more context is available, thus aligning the training with the information available at different diffusion time steps. Our results show that LIFT outperforms existing SFT baselines across six reasoning benchmarks, achieving up to a 3x relative gain on AIME'24 and AIME'25. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/divelab/LIFT.

</details>


### [75] [Can AI Guess What You Know? Performance Comparison of Large Language Models for Human Domain Knowledge Estimation From Communication Logs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22971)
*Ko Watanabe,Shoya Ishimaru*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）能否从长期的Slack聊天记录中直接推断个人领域知识。基于43名用户27,188条消息的数据，评估了包括Gemini、Claude和GPT系列在内的七种模型，发现Gemini 2.5 Flash在零样本估计中误差最低（MAE 21.13%），而GPT模型表现较差。值得注意的是，推断准确性与消息数量关联较弱，表明文本量多并不等于推断更准。研究证实了自动化专家画像的可行性及其当前局限，强调需考虑隐私保护及更结构化的知识表示方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 员工常难以识别‘谁了解什么’，导致组织效率损失。为提升知识管理效率，探索利用LLMs从日常沟通记录中自动推断个体专业知识的可能性。

Method: 分析43名用户的27,188条长期Slack消息，采用七种主流LLM（如Gemini、Claude、GPT系列）进行零样本推断，并将模型输出与27名参与者自评技能评分对比，以评估推断准确性。

Result: Gemini 2.5 Flash表现出最低的误差（MAE 21.13%），GPT系列模型误差显著更高；推断准确率与消息总量相关性弱，说明仅增加文本量无法有效提升推断质量。

Conclusion: LLMs可实现一定程度的自动化专家知识映射，但存在局限性，未来需发展隐私保护机制和更具结构化的知识表示方法。

Abstract: Employees often struggle to identify ``who knows what,'' leading to organizational productivity losses. We investigate whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can infer individual domain knowledge directly from long-term Slack logs. Analyzing 27,188 messages from 43 users, we evaluated seven models (including Gemini, Claude, and GPT families) by comparing their zero-shot estimates against self-reported skill ratings from 27 participants. Gemini 2.5 Flash achieved the lowest error (MAE 21.13%), while GPT models showed significantly larger discrepancies. Notably, estimation accuracy depended only weakly on message volume, indicating that more text alone does not guarantee better inference. These findings demonstrate the feasibility and current limits of automated expertise mapping, highlighting the need for privacy-preserving deployments and richer, structure-aware representations of human knowledge.

</details>


### [76] [When AI Takes Sides on Questions of Faith: Persistent Asymmetries in AI-Mediated Faith Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22975)
*Brett Israelsen,Sheryl Carty,Josh Coates,Nancy Fulda,Julie Park,Pete Whiting*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理宗教转换问题时是否存在对称性，发现模型表现出系统性不对称：对某些宗教（如天主教、巴哈伊教、锡克教）更支持加入，而对其他宗教（如无神论、不可知论、耶和华见证人）则更倾向于劝阻加入。这种倾向在不同模型规模和提供商之间存在差异，且结果具有可重复性，表明不对称是模型行为的稳健特征，可能带来现实影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在处理宗教转换咨询时是否表现出对称性，揭示潜在的价值偏见及其社会影响。

Method: 通过人类验证的LLM-as-a-judge框架，测试20个商业和开源语言模型在182组宗教配对中的反应，采用模拟用户提问方式评估模型对信仰转换建议的倾向性，并分析多种提问变体下的结果一致性。

Result: 所有测试的LLM均表现出系统性不对称，偏好特定宗教，尤其以Grok 4.20表现最为明显；这些模式在不同提问方式和数据集下保持稳定，说明其非偶然性。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在宗教转换建议中存在可复制的不对称倾向，反映了潜在价值偏向，需警惕其大规模部署带来的现实影响。

Abstract: We ask whether large language models (LLMs) treat queries about religious conversion symmetrically. The answer is no. When asked for advice on hypothetical faith transitions from one religion to another, then asked the reversed question, models exhibited consistent asymmetries, favoring some religions while subtly discouraging conversion to others. On average Catholic, Bahá'í, and Sikh religions were broadly favored (high support for joining, low support for leaving), while Atheists, Agnostics, and Jehovah's Witnesses were primarily disfavored. Patterns varied by model size and model provider, with Grok 4.20 exhibiting the strongest asymmetries.
  We tested 20 commercial and open-source language models across 182 religion pairings using a human-verified LLM-as-a-judge framework. Each model was probed via interactions with a simulated user asking for advice on a potential faith conversion. Models tended to use more encouraging language for some faith transitions over others; these patterns were systematically repeatable across multiple trials.
  All LLMs tested exhibited reproducible asymmetry, though the pattern of preferences differed for each. Overall preferences persist across multiple question phrasings and variations in the religious pairing dataset. Taken together, these results suggest that asymmetry is a robust property of model behavior rather than an artifact of how the models' answers were scored. It is important to consider that any imbalances deployed and reproduced en masse can have real-world implications.

</details>


### [77] [A Reproducible Universal Dependencies-Style Pipeline for Katharevousa Greek Parliamentary Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22978)
*George Mikros,Fotios Fitsilis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套可复现的工作流程，用于构建和评估古希腊语（Katharevousa）议会提问的句法解析资源。该工作流结合了OCR修复、基于大模型的标注、自动验证、CoNLL-U格式化、固定分割评估与模型比较，最终形成包含1,697句的冻结参考数据集（训练1,357句，测试340句）。在多种模型对比中，XLM-R表现最佳，达到0.8893的UPOS准确率、0.7250的依存关系F1、0.6098的UAS和0.5162的LAS，显著优于现有外部基线（如spaCy Greek的LAS为0.4183）。特征型模型在词性标注和关系标注上也表现良好，说明在小规模数据下显式特征仍具价值。研究贡献不仅在于性能提升，更在于提供一套可审计、可复用的历史文本NLP基础设施。所有代码、标注、分拆和评测报告均开源发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Katharevousa希腊语在法律、行政及议会档案中具有重要地位，但当前自然语言处理工具对其支持不足。由于历史文本的复杂性（如手写体、印刷错误、语言演变），其处理面临挑战，亟需专门的标注与解析资源。本研究旨在填补这一空白，建立一个高质量、可复现的句法分析基准。

Method: 提出一个端到端的可复现工作流：包括OCR感知的文本重建、基于大模型的受限标注、自动验证机制、确定性的CoNLL-U格式输出、固定训练/测试分割，并统一采用相同评估协议比较多种模型（包括off-the-shelf希腊语与古希腊语解析器、特征型模型、mBERT、XLM-R以及自训练Stanza）。整个流程确保结果的可比性和可审计性。

Result: 构建了一个包含1,697句的冻结参考数据集，其中训练集1,357句，测试集340句。在统一评估下，最佳模型为XLM-R，其依赖关系解析的LAS达0.5162，比最强外部基线（spaCy Greek）高出0.0980。特征型模型在词性标注和关系标注方面表现稳定，显示传统特征仍具价值。所有数据与工具均以开放获取形式发布。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建并验证了首个面向古希腊语议会文本的可复现句法解析资源。该成果不仅提升了对特定语言变体的处理能力，还提供了透明、可审计、可复用的NLP基础设施，为历史文献的数字化与分析奠定了基础。所有成果均开源，支持后续研究与应用。

Abstract: Katharevousa Greek remains poorly served by contemporary NLP pipelines despite its importance for legal, administrative, and parliamentary archives. We present a reproducible workflow for building and evaluating a Universal Dependencies-style parsing resource for Katharevousa parliamentary questions from Greece's early post-junta period. The pipeline links OCR-aware reconstruction, schema-constrained LLM-assisted annotation, automatic validation, deterministic CoNLL-U snapshotting, fixed-split evaluation, and model-family comparison. The frozen automatically validated reference set contains 1{,}697 sentences, split into 1{,}357 training sentences and 340 held-out test sentences. We compare off-the-shelf Greek and Ancient Greek parsers, a feature-based parser, mBERT, XLM-R, and custom Stanza training under the same scoring protocol. Off-the-shelf systems show substantial register mismatch: the strongest external baseline, spaCy Greek, reaches 0.4183 LAS. The best structural parser, an XLM-R model, reaches 0.8893 UPOS accuracy, 0.7250 dependency-relation F1, 0.6098 UAS, and 0.5162 LAS, an absolute LAS gain of 0.0980 over the best external baseline. The feature-based model remains competitive for UPOS and relation labeling, indicating that transparent lexical-context features still matter at this data scale. Beyond scores, the paper contributes an auditable methodology for turning difficult historical parliamentary OCR into reusable syntactic NLP infrastructure. The entire pipeline -- code, schema, frozen reference annotations, fixed train/test split, and per-model benchmark reports -- is released as an open-access companion to this paper.

</details>


### [78] [Memorization Dynamics of Fill-in-the-Middle Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22981)
*Tobias von Arx,Tanguy Dieudonné*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了填空中间（FIM）预训练目标对因果语言模型中记忆行为的影响，使用匹配的Llama 3.2模型在包含重复古腾堡文本的FineWeb-Gutenberg语料上进行训练。结果显示，与标准左到右（LTR）训练相比，FIM更倾向于恢复短或部分匹配的文本片段，而LTR则更常对长的精确延续赋予高置信度。随着重复次数增加，FIM下的原文提取能力近似线性增长。此外，仅依赖后缀上下文不足以实现有效记忆，原文召回仍强烈依赖前缀上下文。研究强调，单一跨度长度或探测格式可能忽略记忆行为的关键细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索填空中间（FIM）预训练目标对语言模型中原文记忆行为的影响，尤其是在重复文本场景下的动态变化，以揭示其与传统左到右（LTR）训练的差异。

Method: 在控制环境下，使用相同规模的Llama 3.2模型分别采用FIM和标准左到右（LTR）目标在FineWeb-Gutenberg语料上进行预训练，该语料包含重复的古腾堡文本。通过前缀引导的探针评估模型对短、长跨度文本的恢复能力，并分析不同上下文结构（前缀/后缀）对记忆表现的影响。

Result: FIM模型更倾向于恢复短或部分匹配的文本段落，而LTR模型对长且完全一致的延续更具信心；原文提取能力随重复次数呈近似线性增长；后缀上下文不足以支持有效的原文回忆，记忆仍高度依赖前缀信息；单一跨度或探测方式会掩盖关键的记忆行为特征。

Conclusion: FIM预训练虽增强了模型的填空能力，但其记忆机制与传统方法存在显著差异，尤其在原文复现方面表现出对前缀强依赖性，且记忆强度随重复次数线性增强。研究强调应采用多维度评估方法以全面理解模型记忆行为。

Abstract: Fill-in-the-middle (FIM) is a pretraining objective widely used to equip causal language models with infilling ability, yet its effect on verbatim memorization remains underexplored. We study the memorization dynamics of FIM in a controlled setting by pretraining matched Llama 3.2 models with FIM and standard left-to-right (LTR) objectives on a FineWeb-Gutenberg corpus containing repeated Gutenberg excerpts. With prefix-based probes, FIM more often recovers short or partially matching spans, while LTR more often assigns high confidence to long exact continuations. We observe that verbatim extraction under FIM-training grows approximately linearly with repetitions over the tested range. Evaluating native FIM-format probes reveals that suffix context is not sufficient: verbatim recall under FIM-training remains strongly anchored in prefix context. Our results also show that evaluating only one span length or probing format can miss important nuances in memorization behavior.

</details>


### [79] [A Proactive Multi-Agent Dialogue Framework for Assessing Social Language Disorder Traits in Autism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22993)
*Chuanbo Hu,Minglei Yin,Bin Liu,Wenqi Li,Lynn K. Paul,Shuo Wang,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为TPA（Think, Plan, Ask）的主动多智能体对话框架，用于自闭症诊断观察量表模块4（ADOS-2）的语言评估部分。该框架通过医生智能体在提问前主动推理未观察到的语言特征，并据此选择临床合理的策略生成针对性问题，从而系统性地揭示社交语言障碍（SLD）的潜在表现。患者智能体基于真实临床数据构建，支持可重复评估。在35名患者的484个对话片段上测试，TPA在所有主要指标上均优于六种基线方法，达到82.1%的SLD特征覆盖率，比自动回放临床对话高出16.6%（65.5%），且每轮诊断效率显著提升（AUCC：0.628 vs. 0.458，绝对提升0.170）。结果表明，主动提问策略选择能大幅提升自动化SLD特征评估的效率，具有推动AI辅助大规模临床筛查的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交语言障碍（SLD）在自闭症谱系障碍中的典型语言特征（如回声式重复、代词错用、刻板媒体引用）通常在自发对话中不显现，仅在特定对话条件下出现。因此，提问策略的选择成为影响诊断信息获取的关键因素，但该问题在现有研究中未受足够重视。如何利用大语言模型（LLM）主动选择能有效激发这些隐性特征的提问策略，尚缺乏探索。

Method: 提出TPA框架，包含两个核心智能体：医生智能体负责基于当前对话状态推理未观测到的SLD特征，并规划相应提问策略；患者智能体基于真实ADOS-2临床数据构建，确保对话行为与真实患者一致。整个过程实现主动推理—计划—提问的闭环，以提升诊断信息的挖掘效率。

Result: 在35名患者的484个对话片段上，TPA在各项指标上均显著优于六种竞争性基线模型，实现82.1%的SLD特征覆盖率，较自动回放临床对话提升16.6个百分点（65.5%），同时每轮对话的诊断效率（AUCC）达0.628，比基线高0.170，证明主动策略选择可大幅提高评估效率。

Conclusion: TPA框架通过主动推理和规划提问策略，能够有效激发并捕捉自闭症患者中潜藏的社交语言障碍特征，显著提升自动化语言评估的诊断效率与覆盖度，为实现可扩展的AI辅助临床筛查提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Characteristic linguistic behaviors associated with Social Language Disorder (SLD) in autism spectrum disorder, including echoic repetition, pronoun displacement, and stereotyped media quoting, are largely absent from spontaneous conversation and only emerge under specific conversational conditions. In structured clinical assessments, this latency means that questioning strategy selection is a critical yet underappreciated determinant of how much diagnostic information a conversation yields. Whether large language models (LLMs) can be guided to proactively select questioning strategies that systematically surface these latent traits remains largely unexplored. Here we present TPA (Think, Plan, Ask), a proactive multi-agent dialogue framework applied to the language assessment component of the Autism Diagnostic Observation Schedule Module 4 (ADOS-2), in which a doctor agent explicitly reasons about which traits remain unobserved before selecting a clinically grounded strategy and generating a targeted question. A patient agent grounded in real ADOS-2 clinical data enables reproducible evaluation without real patient participation, validated across three independent experiments confirming adequate fidelity to real patient language. Evaluated on 484 episodes from 35 patients, TPA outperforms six competitive dialogue planning baselines across all primary metrics, achieving 82.1% SLD trait coverage, 16.6% higher than automated replay of real clinical dialogues conducted by trained clinicians (65.5%), with substantially greater per-turn diagnostic efficiency (AUCC: 0.628 vs. 0.458, absolute gain +0.170). These results demonstrate that proactive questioning strategy selection substantially improves the efficiency of automated SLD trait assessment, with direct implications for scalable AI-assisted clinical screening.

</details>


### [80] [Brain-LLM Alignment Tracks Training Data, Not Typology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23032)
*Dongxin Guo,Jikun Wu,Siu Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析英、中、法三语的fMRI数据与七种LLM的对比，发现脑-语言模型对齐并非英语固有优势，而是由训练语言主导性决定；中文主导模型在大脑对齐上表现优于英语，且语法类型差异和分词特性显著影响对齐效果，尤其在额下回（IFG）区域表现出更强的跨语言梯度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究脑-大语言模型（LLM）对齐是否跨语言通用，以及其变化背后的驱动因素，特别是验证‘英语优势’是否源于语言本质或训练数据组成。

Method: 使用来自112名参与者（涵盖英语、中文、法语）的fMRI数据（基于《小王子》语料库），结合七种不同架构的LLM（包括英语主导、中文主导及多语言模型），分析脑区活动与模型编码层之间的对齐模式，并量化训练语言主导性、语言类型学距离、分词特性等因素的影响。

Result: 中文主导模型（Baichuan2-7B）在与中国大脑匹配时表现最佳，而在与英语大脑匹配时最差，完全逆转了传统英语优势模式；语言类型学距离独立影响对齐质量，语法相关脑区（如IFG）的对齐梯度是词汇语义区（PTL）的2.3倍；分词灵活性解释了约60%的最优编码层跨语言迁移差异。

Conclusion: 所谓的‘英语优势’在脑-LLM对齐中实为训练数据构成的产物，而跨语言对齐的剩余变异主要反映真实语言类型结构，尤其集中在语法处理区域。

Abstract: Brain-LLM alignment is well established in English, yet the brain's language network is neuroanatomically universal across languages. Does alignment also generalize cross-linguistically, and what governs the variation? We test this using fMRI data from 112 participants across English, Chinese, and French (the Le Petit Prince corpus) and seven LLMs spanning English-dominant, Chinese-dominant, and multilingual architectures. Our central finding is that training-language dominance, not an inherent property of English, drives the alignment pattern: a Chinese-dominant model (Baichuan2-7B), architecture-matched to LLaMA-2-7B, reverses the gradient entirely, aligning best with Chinese brains and worst with English. Beyond training dominance, formal typological distance independently covaries with alignment degradation, syntax-associated brain regions (IFG) show $2.3\times$ steeper typological gradients than lexico-semantic regions (PTL), and tokenization fertility accounts for $\sim$60% of a cross-linguistic shift in optimal encoding layer. These results reveal that the apparent "English advantage" in brain-LLM alignment is an artifact of training data composition, while the remaining variation reflects genuine typological structure concentrated in syntactic processing.

### [81] [Sparse Autoencoders Map Brain-LLM Alignment onto Cortical Semantic Topography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23035)
*Dongxin Guo,Jikun Wu,Siu Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过将稀疏自编码器（SAEs）与神经编码模型结合，解析GPT-2 XL和Llama-3.1-8B的中间层，发现语义特征可解释94%的人脑语言响应峰值性能，并在跨语言（英语、中文、法语）中具有泛化能力。进一步验证了五类语义子类别与大脑特定区域的对应关系，揭示了大脑语义组织的精细结构，且这些特征还能预测阅读时间及意外语义内容的编码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型的中间层能有效预测人类大脑对语言的反应，但其内在机制尚不明确。本研究旨在从可解释性角度揭示为何中间层具有如此强的预测能力，特别是语义特征在其中的核心作用。

Method: 采用稀疏自编码器（SAEs）对GPT-2 XL和Llama-3.1-8B进行分解，提取每层16K–32K个可解释特征；构建人类验证的语义分类体系（κ≥0.74），并评估这些特征在预测人脑活动、阅读时间以及与已知脑区拓扑结构一致性方面的表现。

Result: 语义特征单独即可恢复94%的编码性能（r=0.285），显著优于基线（p<0.001, d=1.31）；五类语义子类别与大脑区域的映射经正式检验一致（Spearman ρ=0.72, p<0.001；超几何检验 p=0.007）；特征还可预测阅读时间（ΔlogLik=38.4, p<0.001），并提示大脑可能编码意外语义信息。结果在多语言间保持一致。

Conclusion: SAE提取的语义特征不仅在神经编码中占据主导地位，还复现了大脑语义组织的精细拓扑结构，为理解语言模型与人脑之间的共性提供了机制性解释，推动了计算神经语言学的发展。

Abstract: Intermediate layers of large language models (LLMs) best predict human brain responses to language, one of the most robust findings in computational neurolinguistics, yet why remains mechanistically unexplained. We address this gap by bridging sparse autoencoders (SAEs) from mechanistic interpretability with neural encoding models, decomposing GPT-2 XL and Llama-3.1-8B into 16K-32K interpretable features per layer. A human-validated taxonomy ($κ\geq 0.74$) reveals that semantic features alone recover 94% of peak encoding performance ($r=0.285$), substantially exceeding variance-matched baselines ($p<0.001$, $d=1.31$). Beyond this aggregate dominance, we test a novel cortical topography prediction: five semantic subcategories derived a priori from three independent neuroscience programs should map onto distinct brain regions. A formal convergence test confirms this alignment (Spearman $ρ=0.72$, $p<0.001$; hypergeometric $p=0.007$), demonstrating that SAE-discovered features recapitulate known cortical semantic organization at a granularity inaccessible to prior methods. SAE features further predict human reading times beyond lexical controls ($Δ\mathrm{logLik}=38.4$, $p<0.001$), and an exploratory prediction-error analysis provides preliminary evidence that the brain additionally encodes unexpected semantic content. Results generalize across English, Chinese, and French.

### [82] [Do Language Models Know What Not to Say? Causal Evidence for Statistical Preemption in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23039)
*Dongxin Guo,Jikun Wu,Siu Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过计算实验首次在大型语言模型中直接区分了统计预占与固有强化假说，发现语言模型的不可接受性知识主要由竞争形式频率驱动，而非整体动词频率。结果显示，语言模型的意外度模式与人类可接受性判断高度相关（r = 0.79），且预占敏感性随模型规模呈幂律增长，通过微调干预证实了竞争频率对预占行为的因果影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨学习者如何在缺乏负面证据的情况下习得语言中哪些结构不可接受。传统理论难以解释这一过程，而构式语法提出统计预占机制作为可能解释。

Method: 采用四个实验，涵盖120个英语动词-构式配对（双宾、使役、处所），利用大型语言模型分析其意外度模式，并通过非循环偏相关和可控微调干预验证竞争形式频率的作用。

Result: 语言模型的意外度与人类可接受性判断高度相关（r = 0.79）；结果由竞争形式频率驱动，而非整体动词频率；预占敏感性随模型规模呈幂律增长；微调干预证实了竞争频率的因果作用。

Conclusion: 神经语言模型通过分布竞争获得负向语言知识，支持构式语法的核心机制——统计预占。

Abstract: How do learners acquire knowledge of what is unacceptable without negative evidence? Construction Grammar proposes statistical preemption: exposure to a conventional form (e.g., "donated the books to the library") preempts structurally possible but unattested alternatives ("*donated the library the books"). We present a computational study that, for the first time, directly dissociates statistical preemption from the competing entrenchment hypothesis in large language models within a single converging design. Across four experiments spanning 120 English verb-construction pairings (dative, causative, locative), we show that (1) LLM surprisal patterns correlate strongly with human acceptability judgments ($r = 0.79$), validated against three independent behavioral datasets; (2) these patterns are driven by competing-form frequency rather than overall verb frequency, confirmed by non-circular partial correlations; (3) preemption sensitivity scales as a power law with model size; and (4) a controlled fine-tuning intervention causally demonstrates that manipulating competing-form frequencies shifts preemption behavior in the predicted direction, with reverse-direction controls ruling out frequency-sensitivity confounds. These results provide converging evidence that neural language models acquire negative linguistic knowledge through distributional competition, the core mechanism posited by Construction Grammar.

</details>


### [83] [DreamerNLplus: Interpretable Modeling of Mental Health Dynamics from Social Media Timelines using Hybrid Rule-Based and RAG Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23052)
*Maryia Zhyrko,Daisy Monika Lal,Erik van Mulligen,Lifeng Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DreamerNLplus 是一个用于建模社交媒体时间线中心理健康动态的混合框架，针对 CLPsych 2026 共享任务中的三个子任务：心理状态建模、时间变化检测和序列级摘要。该系统结合 LLM 数据增强、DeBERTa 分类与随机森林回归进行结构化状态预测；采用少样本提示和本地部署的 Llama 3.1 模型检测短期时间上下文中的转换与恶化事件；在摘要任务中，基于 RAG 的方法在改善项上排名第一，恶化项上排名第三，表现出对心理变化模式的良好捕捉能力。分析揭示了分类与回归性能不匹配、时间过渡建模困难以及语义与相似性评估指标之间的分歧等挑战，强调了未来统一评估框架的重要性。代码与提示已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在建模社交媒体上的心理健康动态时面临多任务协同、时间变化检测与语义摘要生成的挑战，尤其在缺乏充分标注数据的情况下，如何有效融合不同模型优势并实现跨任务一致性是关键问题。

Method: 结合数据增强（LLM）、DeBERTa 分类、随机森林回归（任务1）；少样本提示 + 本地 Llama 3.1 模型（任务2）；规则基摘要与少样本 LLM 摘要（任务3.1），基于 RAG 的方法处理任务3.2。

Result: 任务1：结构化状态预测表现良好；任务2：成功检测切换与升级事件；任务3.1：排名第二；任务3.2：改善项第一，恶化项第三，显示对重复心理变化模式的有效建模能力。

Conclusion: DreamerNLplus 展现了在多任务心理健康动态建模中的有效性，但存在分类与回归性能不一致、时间过渡建模困难及评估指标冲突等问题，亟需建立统一的评估体系以推动后续研究。

Abstract: We present DreamerNLplus, a hybrid framework for modeling mental health dynamics from social media timelines in the CLPsych 2026 shared task. Our system addresses three tasks: psychological state modeling, temporal change detection, and sequence-level summarization.
  For Task 1, we combine LLM-based data augmentation, DeBERTa classification, and Random Forest regression for structured state prediction. For Task 2, we use few-shot prompting with a locally deployed Llama 3.1 model to detect Switch and Escalation events using short-term temporal context. For Task 3.1, we explore both a deterministic rule-based summarization pipeline and a few-shot LLM-based approach, ranking \textbf{2nd} officially. Our RAG-based method achieves strong performance in Task 3.2, ranking \textbf{1st} for Improvement and \textbf{3rd} for Deterioration, demonstrating its ability to capture recurrent psychological change patterns across timelines.
  Our analysis reveals key challenges, including the mismatch between classification and regression performance, the difficulty of modeling temporal transitions, and the disagreement between semantic and similarity-based evaluation metrics. These findings highlight the complexity of modeling mental health dynamics and motivate future work on unified evaluation frameworks. We share our code and prompts at https://github.com/4dpicture/CLPsych2026

### [84] [Model Collapse as Cultural Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23054)
*Dongxin Guo,Jikun Wu,Siu Ming Yiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过文化演化中的迭代学习理论解释了大语言模型在自训练过程中出现的模型坍缩现象，揭示了语法结构（尤其是组合性）随时间呈现非单调变化（先上升后下降）的规律，并验证了该理论的五个可证伪预测。实验在英语、德语和土耳其语中对LLaMA-2-7B和Mistral-7B进行10代自训练，发现只有任务相关的过滤才能维持组合性，而随机过滤无效。所有预测均得到强证据支持（效应量Hedges' g > 1.6；贝叶斯因子BF₁₀ > 100），且模型正则化梯度与人类行为数据高度一致（R² = 0.94）。研究将模型坍缩重新定义为文化传递过程，并提出可操作的自训练设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对模型坍缩的研究多停留在统计层面，缺乏对语言结构如何及为何退化的语言学解释。本研究旨在填补这一空白，引入迭代学习理论以提供可解释的机制框架。

Method: 基于迭代学习理论推导出五项可证伪假设，通过在三种语言上对LLaMA-2-7B和Mistral-7B进行10代自训练实验，系统测试这些假设。采用任务相关与随机过滤对比，分析组合性等语言特征的变化轨迹，并与人类行为数据进行比较。

Result: 组合性在自训练中呈现先升后降的非单调趋势，该现象在高规则性初始数据下依然存在，仅任务导向过滤能维持其稳定性。所有预测均被强有力证实，效应量大，且模型正则化模式与人类行为高度吻合（R² = 0.94）。

Conclusion: 模型坍缩本质上是文化传递中的压缩-通信权衡体现，该研究不仅提供了理论解释，还为构建更稳健的自训练系统提供了实证指导原则。

Abstract: Model collapse, the progressive degradation of LLMs trained on their own outputs, has been characterized statistically but lacks a linguistic explanation for which structures degrade, in what order, and why. We show that iterated learning theory from cultural evolution fills this gap. We derive five falsifiable predictions, distinguish those uniquely discriminative for the theory from confirmatory ones, and test them by self-training LLaMA-2-7B and Mistral-7B over 10 generations in English, German, and Turkish. The critical discriminative finding: compositionality follows a non-monotonic trajectory (initially rising, then falling) under unfiltered self-training. This signature persists with maximally regular seed data (ruling out noise removal) and is sustained only by task-grounded filtering, not random filtering, providing the first LLM-scale evidence for the compression-communication tradeoff. All predictions are confirmed with large effect sizes (Hedges' $g > 1.6$; $\mathrm{BF}_{10} > 100$), and LLM regularization gradients closely match human behavioral data ($R^2 = 0.94$). These results reframe model collapse as a cultural transmission phenomenon and yield concrete principles for self-training pipeline design.

</details>


### [85] [DFKI-MLT at SemEval-2026 TASK 7: Steering Multilingual Models Towards Cultural Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23069)
*Yusser Al Ghussin,Daniil Gurgurov,Yasser Hamidullah,Josef van Genabith,Cristina España-Bonet,Simon Ostermann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DFKI-MLT系统，通过激活引导技术在多语言大模型中引入语言特定的引导向量，实现推理时的跨文化适应，无需参数更新。在SemEval-2026任务7的多项选择赛道中取得86.96%准确率，排名第七。后验分析显示该方法在文化推理上提升有限且不一致，性能受层位置、语言-地区组合及提示设计显著影响，表明需联合优化提示与激活引导以实现真正文化感知的多语言推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在跨语言和跨文化场景中的应用日益广泛，但其文化知识分布不均，尤其在非主流语言和区域间存在明显短板。为提升模型的文化敏感性，亟需一种高效、可迁移的推理阶段适配机制。

Method: 采用基于平行语料（FLORES）提取的语言向量，对多语言大模型进行激活引导。通过在特定Transformer层的残差流中注入语言特定的引导向量，实现无参数更新的推理时适应。

Result: 在官方多项选择赛道中达到86.96%准确率，位列17支参赛队伍中的第7名；后验分析揭示激活引导带来有限且异质性的性能提升，部分配置甚至导致性能下降，且效果高度依赖于层位置、语言-区域组合和提示形式。

Conclusion: 激活引导可在一定程度上增强多语言模型的文化感知能力，但其效果不稳定，需与提示设计协同优化，才能实现可靠的跨文化推理。未来工作应聚焦于动态引导策略与提示工程的联合建模。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used across diverse linguistic and cultural contexts, yet their cultural knowledge remains uneven across regions and languages. We present the DFKI-MLT system for SemEval-2026 Task 7 on cultural awareness, where we apply activation steering to multilingual LLMs using language vectors extracted from parallel FLORES data. Our method performs inference-time adaptation by adding language-specific steering vectors to the residual stream at a selected transformer layer, without any parameter updates. We participated in both the short-answer (SAQ) and multiple-choice (MCQ) tracks; however, only our MCQ submission received an official score. In the official MCQ track, we achieved 86.96% accuracy, ranking 7th out of 17 teams. To better understand system behavior, we conduct post-hoc analyses on the shared-task MCQ and SAQ settings. These analyses show that activation steering yields modest and heterogeneous improvements on cultural reasoning: gains are strongly layer-sensitive, vary substantially across language-region pairs, with some configurations even degrading performance, and interact with prompt formulation, comparing generic and culturally conditioned prompts. Our findings suggest that prompt design and activation steering should be jointly optimized for culturally aware multilingual inference.

</details>


### [86] [The Efficiency Frontier: A Unified Framework for Cost-Performance Optimization in LLM Context Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23071)
*Binqi Shen,Lier Jin,Hanyu Cai,Lan Hu,Yuting Xin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为'效率前沿'（The Efficiency Frontier）的统一框架，用于在大型语言模型（LLM）上下文管理中实现成本-性能优化。该框架将上下文策略选择建模为一个考虑任务性能、令牌成本和预处理重用的部署感知优化问题，通过摊销成本建模实现对不同策略的系统性比较。在5,000个HotpotQA实例上的评估揭示了不同操作区域及策略间的转换边界，表明部署感知优化可在保持性能（F1≈0.78）的前提下降低约25%的有效令牌使用量；而摊销式内存压缩在高绩效场景下相比全上下文提示可降低超过50%的令牌成本。该框架为构建可扩展、高效且可持续的LLM系统提供了原则性和实践性的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文处理方法（如检索和记忆压缩）通常独立评估性能与效率，缺乏系统性比较和部署导向决策支持，导致难以在实际应用中选择最优策略。

Method: 提出'效率前沿'框架，通过摊销成本建模联合考虑任务性能、令牌成本和预处理重用，将上下文策略选择转化为部署感知优化问题，支持在不同运行条件下进行策略偏好分析。

Result: 在HotpotQA数据集上，部署感知优化使有效令牌使用减少约25%，同时保持F1≈0.78的性能；摊销内存压缩在高性能场景下比全上下文提示降低超过50%的令牌成本。框架识别出不同策略的运作区域和转换边界。

Conclusion: 该框架为大规模、高效、可持续的LLM系统提供了系统化、实用的评估与部署决策支持工具，推动上下文管理从孤立评估走向整体优化。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly rely on long-context processing, but expanding context windows introduces substantial computational and financial costs. Existing context reduction approaches, including retrieval and memory compression methods, are typically evaluated using performance and efficiency metrics independently, limiting systematic comparison and deployment-aware decision-making.
  This paper introduces The Efficiency Frontier, a unified framework for cost-performance optimization in LLM context management. The framework models context strategy selection as a deployment-aware optimization problem that jointly accounts for task performance, token cost, and preprocessing reuse through amortized cost modeling. Unlike existing evaluations that compare methods in isolation, the proposed framework enables decision-oriented analysis of when different context management strategies become preferable under varying operational conditions. Evaluated on 5,000 HotpotQA instances, the framework reveals distinct operational regimes and transition boundaries between retrieval-based and preprocessing-based strategies. Results show that deployment-aware optimization reduces effective token usage by approximately 25% at comparable performance ($F1 \approx 0.78$), while amortized memory compression achieves over 50% lower token cost relative to full-context prompting in higher-performance settings. Overall, the proposed framework provides a principled and practical foundation for evaluating and deploying scalable, efficient, and sustainable LLM systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Topic modeling in applied psychology increasingly spans two methodological traditions: probabilistic bag-of-words models and newer embedding-based approaches. Yet many evaluations of these methods rely on longer and cleaner benchmark corpora, leaving less guidance for short, open-ended survey responses. This paper compares Structural Topic Models (STM), a probabilistic topic model, and BERTopic, an embedding-based model, for analyzing open-ended survey responses. Results indicate that BERTopic consistently produced higher topic coherence than STM, with contextual augmentation yielding the strongest performance gains. In contrast, higher-dimensional embeddings alone did not improve coherence and were associated with greater data loss. Qualitative evaluation showed that BERTopic generated more interpretable and stable topics, while STM topics were often broader and more mixed. However, STM provides stronger support for inferential covariate analysis, whereas BERTopic covariate comparisons are primarily descriptive. We conclude with practical guidance for selecting and combining topic modeling approaches in applied social science research.

### [89] [As X, Do Y: How Persona and Task Combine in Instruction-Tuned LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23147)
*Eric Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究发现角色提示（如'作为X，做Y'）在残差流的特定位置（提示到回答的过渡处）表现出可分解的线性结构，其中人格和任务通过部分正交的加法方向贡献。虽然可以构建纯人格（Δ_X）和纯任务（Δ_Y）效应，并用其替换干净残差以获得接近原始输出的结果，但这种局部加法结构并不意味着提示可压缩。实验表明，即使使用缓存的预测或理想干净残差注入基线提示，也无法逼近完整长人格提示的效果，因为人格引导的多标记生成会通过注意力机制回传至人格文本位置，而单点残差无法复制这一分布式机制。因此，局部加法性支持可解释性和精细调控，但不支持提示压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索角色提示在大模型残差流中的表示机制，理解其是否可通过局部加法结构实现高效压缩，进而提升可控性和可解释性。

Method: 通过分析Gemma-2-2B-IT和Qwen-2.5系列模型在短网格与长人格网格下的残差流，定位提示到回答过渡处的线性分解结构，构建纯人格与任务效应向量，并进行残差替换实验，验证缓存向量能否复现原始行为。

Result: 在特定层带的提示-回答过渡点，人格与任务贡献可分解为部分正交的加法方向；尽管局部替换能保持下游输出相近，但注入缓存残差或理想残差均无法复现完整长人格提示的行为，说明人格条件生成依赖于跨层的分布式提示/KV机制。

Conclusion: 局部残差流中的加法结构虽支持可解释性和精细控制，但并不意味着角色提示可压缩为单一缓存向量。人格引导行为依赖于整个提示的分布式注意力机制，局部激活算术无法替代。

Abstract: Role prompts of the form As X, do Y admit a clean linear decomposition at one specific site in the residual stream: the prompt-to-answer transition -- the last prompt token together with the first two generated tokens -- in an early/mid layer band. There, persona and task contribute through partially orthogonal additive directions. Forming a pure persona effect $Δ_X$, a pure task effect $Δ_Y$, and substituting $h_{BB} + Δ_X + Δ_Y$ for the clean residual yields downstream output within a small KL of clean on Gemma-2-2B-IT and Qwen-2.5-\{1.5B, 3B\}-Instruct, across a 12-cell short grid and a 48-cell long-persona grid, with persona-specific behavioral markers preserved.
  The natural inference from this additive structure is that the role prompt can be compressed into a single cached residual vector. \emph{We show it cannot.} Injecting the cached additive prediction -- or even the oracle clean residual $h_{XY}$ -- into a baseline host prompt with the persona text removed does not approach the clean long-persona target, at one site or at many layers. Persona-conditioned multi-token generation flows through attention back to the persona-text positions throughout the prompt, which no residual at one site reproduces.
  Local additivity in the residual stream does not imply prompt compressibility. The additive structure at the prompt-to-answer transition supports interpretability and fine-grained steering of persona or task contributions; persona-conditioned behavior across the full continuation depends on a distributed prompt/KV mechanism that local activation arithmetic does not displace.

</details>


### [90] [When Symptoms Are Not Enough: Evidence-Weighting Patterns in Large Language Model Psychiatric Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23148)
*Jianfeng Zhu,Megan Korhummel,Ruoming Jin,Karin G. Coifman*

  <summary>Details</summary>
