Method: 构建一个基于SCID的基准数据集，包含555个半结构化访谈与对应的诊断参考标签，采用零样本任务特定提示方法，评估五种前沿大语言模型在四种精神障碍分类任务中的表现，并通过子群体分析与证据整合分析探究模型错误类型及其成因。

Result: 模型性能在任务与模型间差异明显，准确率范围为0.49–0.86，马修相关系数为0.16–0.38。GPT-4.1 Mini和GPT-5 Mini在各障碍分类中表现最一致。男性参与者抑郁分类准确率高于女性，年龄无明显趋势，种族间存在小幅不均衡。假阴性案例中常含明确症状，但伴随功能完好、应对能力或社会支持等保护性线索，这些因素使模型更倾向于负面分类。

Conclusion: 大语言模型具备支持大规模精神健康筛查的潜力，但其在面对功能完好或保护性背景时对症状证据的忽略现象需在临床部署前进行严格验证，以避免误判。

Abstract: As demand for mental health care outpaces clinician-delivered assessment, scalable screening tools are increasingly needed. Large language models (LLMs) may identify psychiatric risk from patient narratives, but their reliability across diagnoses, demographic subgroups, and evidence-use patterns remains uncertain. We introduce a SCID-anchored benchmark of 555 semi-structured experiential interviews paired with diagnostic reference labels for anxiety disorder, major depressive disorder, post-traumatic stress disorder, and any current mental health disorder. Using zero-shot task-specific prompting, we evaluated five state-of-the-art LLMs and examined whether false-negative errors reflected missed psychiatric evidence or differential weighting of symptom, functional-impairment, and protective-context cues. Performance varied across tasks and models, with accuracy ranging from 0.49 to 0.86 and Matthews correlation coefficients from 0.16 to 0.38. GPT-4.1 Mini and GPT-5 Mini showed the most consistent disorder-specific accuracy. Subgroup analyses found higher depression-classification accuracy among male than female participants, no consistent age-related pattern, and modest non-uniform variation across race strata. Evidence-integration analyses showed that false-negative anxiety and PTSD classifications often contained explicit symptom evidence but were accompanied by preserved functioning, coping ability, or social support. Functional-impairment evidence shifted model outputs toward positive classifications, whereas protective-context evidence shifted outputs away. These findings suggest that LLMs may support scalable psychiatric screening, but their tendency to discount symptom evidence in the presence of preserved functioning or protective context requires careful validation before clinical deployment.

### [91] [Same Model, Different Weakness: How Language and Modality Reshape the Jailbreak Attack Surface in Frontier MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23157)
*Casey Ford,Madison Van Doren,Sicheng Jin,Emily Dix*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地比较了美国英语（en-US）与墨西哥西班牙语（es-MX）在跨语言、多模态红队测试中的越狱漏洞，发现语言并不以统一方式影响模型脆弱性。通过在四个前沿多模态大模型上进行52,272次危害评分和攻击成功判断，结果表明：角色扮演类语言攻击在西班牙语中效果显著下降，而视觉明显的多模态攻击则更有效，说明语言与视觉的对齐失败机制不同。这导致安全排名在不同语言间不一致，如Qwen Omni在西班牙语下比Pixtral Large更易受攻击，且各代模型攻击成功率虽下降但差距未缩小。因此，现有将语言与模态视为独立维度的安全评估框架存在根本缺陷，必须重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型（MLLM）的安全评估多基于英文语境，缺乏跨语言视角；本研究旨在揭示语言如何影响模型对齐失败的机制，暴露现有评估体系的盲区。

Method: 采用固定对抗基准测试集（363个多样化提示场景），在纯文本与多模态条件下分别对四款前沿模型进行红队测试；每语言组由9名母语者标注，收集危害评分与攻击成功二元判断；使用贝叶斯混合效应模型分析语言与攻击类型之间的交互作用。

Result: 语言并非均匀放大或缩小漏洞；角色扮演类攻击在西班牙语中有效性降低，而视觉驱动攻击增强；模型安全排名在不同语言间发生反转（如Qwen Omni在es-MX下比Pixtral Large更脆弱）；攻击成功率随模型代际下降，但语言间差距持续存在。

Conclusion: 语言与模态的对齐失败机制相互分离，现有将二者独立处理的安全评估框架无法准确刻画真实攻击面，必须重新设计以纳入语言-模态交互因素。

Abstract: The attack surface of a multimodal large language model (MLLM) is language-dependent in ways that reveal the mechanistic structure of alignment failures. We present the first systematic cross-lingual, multimodal red-teaming study comparing jailbreak vulnerability in US English (en-US) and Mexican Spanish (es-MX) across four frontier MLLMs: Claude Sonnet 4.5, GPT-5, Pixtral Large, and Qwen Omni. Using a fixed adversarial benchmark of 363 diverse prompt scenarios administered in text-only and multimodal conditions, we collected 52,272 harm ratings and binary attack success judgements from matched panels of nine native-speaker annotators per language group. Our central finding is that language does not scale vulnerability uniformly. Bayesian mixed-effects analyses reveal that linguistic framing attacks such as role-play become substantially less effective under Spanish prompting, while visually explicit multimodal attacks become more effective, which directly implicates the prompt-language interface rather than global annotator leniency. This dissociation indicates that linguistic and visual alignment failures operate through distinct mechanisms, and that switching language is sufficient to expose that separation. The practical consequence is that safety rankings are not preserved across languages. Qwen Omni overtakes Pixtral Large as the most vulnerable model among es-MX participants, a rank reversal no scalar correction of English-condition scores could recover, and absolute attack success rates have declined across model generations without closing the gaps between them. These findings demonstrate that safety evaluation frameworks treating language and modality as independent dimensions fundamentally misspecify the attack surface of globally deployed MLLMs, and must be redesigned accordingly.

### [92] [Hidden Human-Like Nature of Machine-Generated Texts: Theory and Detection Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23190)
*Chenwang Wu,Yiu-ming Cheung,Bo Han,Defu Lian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了机器生成文本中隐藏的人类写作特征，并提出一种模型无关的堆叠增强框架，通过迭代过滤高度人类化的子序列来提升检测性能。该方法在不需重新训练的情况下也能有效工作，具有良好的灵活性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有段落级检测方法将机器生成文本视为完全机器化，忽略了其中可能存在的高度符合人类写作特征的片段。这些隐藏的人类化片段增加了检测难度，因此需要新的方法来应对。

Method: 将片段级别的保留决策建模为潜在变量问题，采用类似硬EM的优化过程，使检测器迭代地过滤出置信度高的类人类子序列，并在剩余文本上自我优化。

Result: 实验表明，所提框架在多种大语言模型和实际场景下均能一致提升现有检测器的性能，且支持无需训练的部署方式，具备良好的实用价值。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了机器生成文本中隐藏的人类化特征对检测任务带来的挑战，并提出了一个高效、灵活且可广泛部署的增强框架，显著提升了检测效果。

Abstract: Machine-generated texts (MGTs) produced by large language models (LLMs) are increasingly prevalent across various applications, while their potential misuse in fake news propagation and phishing has raised serious concerns, highlighting the need for MGT detection. Existing paragraph-level detection methods commonly treat MGTs as entirely machine-like, overlooking the hidden human-like nature of machine-generated texts: even fully machine-generated texts may contain spans that are highly consistent with human writing. To this end, we first reveal the existence of such hidden human-like spans, and then theoretically analyze their impact on detection. Our analysis shows that these spans increase the sentence complexity for detection, thereby making MGT detection intrinsically harder. Based on this finding, we propose a model-agnostic stacked enhancement framework that improves existing detectors by reducing the influence of hidden human-like spans. Specifically, we model span-level retention decisions as a latent-variable problem and instantiate the optimization with a hard-EM-inspired procedure, where the detector iteratively filters confidently human-like subsequences and refines itself on the remaining text. Extensive experiments across various LLMs and practical scenarios demonstrate that the proposed framework consistently enhances existing detectors. Notably, the framework can also work in a training-free manner, offering flexibility and scalability for practical deployment.

### [93] [When Is Next-Token Prediction Useful? Marginalization, Ergodicity, Mixture Identifiability, Local Sufficiency, RAG, Tools, and Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23278)
*Francesco Corielli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文区分了语言模型训练中常被混淆的三个概念：基于潜在情境的完整条件语言过程、通过积分掉这些情境得到的仅文本的边缘过程，以及从有限观测语料库中学习到的模型诱导分布。文章指出，将模型训练解释为估计仅文本的边缘规律需要强假设（如平稳性、代表性、遍历性），这些假设在异质语料中往往不成立。即使假设成立，仅文本的边缘规律也仅在观察前缀是相关潜在情境的近似充分统计量时才有用。信息论上，这要求给定已知文本后，下一个词与被忽略的情境之间的残余条件互信息较小。最后，文章将检索增强生成（RAG）和工具使用视为实现条件充分性的手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清语言模型训练中对条件分布理解的误区，强调真实语言生成不仅依赖于先前文本，还受非文本因素影响，现有建模方法在处理异质语料时存在理论局限。

Method: 通过形式化分析三种不同概率分布的关系，引入信息论框架评估条件充分性，并以RAG和工具使用为例说明如何缓解模型对隐含情境的忽视问题。

Result: 揭示了当前语言模型训练范式中的理论缺陷，证明仅基于文本的边际建模在异质语料下不可靠；提出通过外部信息补充来提升条件充分性，从而改善生成质量。

Conclusion: 语言模型不应被简单视为学习文本边际分布，而应理解为在特定条件下逼近完整条件过程的近似工具；检索增强与工具使用可有效弥补模型对隐含情境的缺失，是迈向更鲁棒生成的重要路径。

Abstract: Language models trained on observed sequences are often described as learning the conditional distribution of the next token given previous tokens. This description is only conditionally correct. A model trained on realized token trajectories does not observe full conditional laws; it receives sampled continuations. Moreover, real language generation is conditioned not only on previous words but also on non-textual circumstances: facts, events, intentions, goals, beliefs, social context, and task-specific constraints. This paper distinguishes three objects that are often conflated: the full conditional language process conditioned on latent circumstances, the marginal text-only process obtained by integrating those circumstances out, and the model-induced distribution learned from finite observed corpora.
  The paper argues that interpreting model training as estimating the marginal text-only law requires strong assumptions of stationarity, representativeness, and ergodicity, assumptions that are standard in statistical estimation but problematic when applied to heterogeneous language corpora. Even if these assumptions hold, the marginal text-only law is useful only when the observed prefix is an approximately sufficient statistic for the latent circumstances relevant to continuation. In information-theoretic terms, usefulness requires that the residual conditional mutual information between the next token and the omitted circumstances, given the observed text, be small.
  The paper then extends this argument to heterogeneous training corpora.
  Finally, the paper interprets Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) and tool use as conditional sufficiency devices.

</details>


### [94] [Convergence Without Understanding: When Language Models Agree on Representations but Disagree on Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23315)
*Muhammad Usama,Dong Eui Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型在不同训练目标和架构下是否在推理过程上也表现出相似的内部表示。通过对16个来自8个模型家族（参数量从1.5B到72B）的模型在800个涵盖数学、科学、常识和真实性的问题上进行分析，发现尽管模型在共享表示上存在收敛，但其推理过程存在三种分离现象：难度反转（失败问题上的表示相似性更高）、代际差距（决策前表示一致而决策后发散）、以及表象正确性（信息可跨模型解码但对预测影响极小）。结果表明，表示收敛反映的是输入处理约束的共性，而非共享推理策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在推理过程中的表示是否随模型差异而收敛，以理解其推理机制的本质。

Method: 在800个多样化任务上评估16个不同规模和架构的语言模型的表示相似性，按问题难度、计算阶段和因果相关性分层分析，并使用中心核对齐（CKA）等指标量化表示相似性，结合消融实验检验因果影响。

Result: 发现三类表示分离：难度反转（失败问题上表示相似性更高，CKA=0.897 vs. 0.830）、生成代际差距（预决策表示对齐，后决策发散，CKA=0.875 vs. 0.274）、以及表象正确性（信息可跨模型解码，但对预测影响微弱，翻转率仅1.5%-5.5%）。

Conclusion: 语言模型的表示收敛主要源于共同的输入处理约束，而非共享的推理策略。这一发现对集成设计、可解释性迁移和模型相似性评估具有重要意义。

Abstract: Large language models trained under diverse objectives and architectures have been shown to develop increasingly similar internal representations, an observation formalized as the Platonic Representation Hypothesis. Whether this representational convergence extends to the reasoning processes that operate over shared representations remains untested. We evaluate representational similarity across 16 language models from 8 families (1.5B to 72B parameters) on 800 reasoning problems spanning mathematics, science, commonsense, and truthfulness, stratifying by problem difficulty, computational stage, and causal relevance. Our analysis reveals three dissociations: a difficulty inversion, where models converge more on problems they collectively fail (Centered Kernel Alignment [CKA] = 0.897) than on those they solve (CKA = 0.830); a generation gap, where pre-decision representations align (CKA = 0.875) while post-decision representations diverge (CKA = 0.274); and epiphenomenal correctness, where shared information is decodable across models (66% transfer accuracy) but exerts minimal causal influence on predictions (1.5% to 5.5% flip rate across ablation protocols). These results indicate that representational convergence in language models reflects shared input processing constraints rather than shared reasoning strategies, with direct implications for ensemble design, interpretability transfer, and evaluations of model similarity. Code is available at https://github.com/Usama1002/convergence-without-understanding.

</details>


### [95] [AraHopeCorpus: Annotation Guidelines and Dataset for Hope Speech in Arabic Social Media Crisis Discourse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23325)
*Esra'a Sharqawi,Wajdi Zaghouani*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对冲突中社交媒体的研究多聚焦于仇恨言论和虚假信息，而对促进韧性、团结与乐观的希望言论，尤其在阿拉伯语语境下，研究不足。亟需系统性数据支持相关分析。

Method: 从2023–2024年加沙战争相关YouTube评论中收集1万条文本，构建AraHopeCorpus；采用多维度标注框架，将评论分类为希望言论、无希望言论、中性或模糊内容；评估标注一致性（Cohen's Kappa=0.71），并对比人类标注者与ChatGPT的表现。

Result: 希望言论占64%以上，主要体现为宗教鼓励、集体团结与对正义的乐观；无希望言论占约13%；标注一致性达较高水平，但方言、讽刺和隐含意义带来挑战；大语言模型可辅助标注，但在文化与方言理解上仍有局限。

Conclusion: AraHopeCorpus是首个阿拉伯语希望言论数据集，填补了该领域空白，有助于推动对建设性数字话语的理解，支持希望言论检测、危机沟通与社会韧性研究，并将在非商业开放许可下发布。

Abstract: Social media has become a crucial arena for shaping public narratives during armed conflicts, providing space for both harmful and constructive communication. While hate speech and misinformation have been widely studied, expressions that promote resilience, solidarity, and optimism remain underexplored, particularly in Arabic contexts. This paper introduces AraHopeCorpus, the first annotated dataset of Arabic hope speech collected from ten thousand YouTube comments related to the war on Gaza between 2023 and 2024. Using a detailed annotation framework, comments were classified into three categories: hope speech, no hope speech, and neutral or unclear discourse. The dataset shows that hopeful language dominates, accounting for more than sixty four percent of all comments. These expressions of hope appear mainly as religious encouragement, collective solidarity, and optimism for endurance and justice. No hope speech, representing about thirteen percent, reflects despair and disillusionment, while the rest of the comments contain neutral or mixed content. Inter-Annotator Agreement reached substantial levels (Cohen's Kappa equals 0.71), though dialectal variation, sarcasm, and implicit meaning posed annotation challenges. A comparative analysis between human annotators and ChatGPT revealed that large language models can support annotation but remain limited in handling dialectal and culturally embedded expressions. AraHopeCorpus will be released for research purposes under an open and non commercial license. It provides a valuable resource for studying constructive digital discourse, enabling further research on hope speech detection, crisis communication, and resilience in Arabic social media.

Each post includes rich contextual information such as language, timestamp, page category, and interaction counts, enabling comprehensive analyses of public discourse around climate communication. The results reveal that emotional tone, post format, and page identity strongly influence audience engagement, with visually rich and emotionally charged content receiving the highest levels of interaction. The dataset also demonstrates how online discussions evolved in response to major events such as international climate summits and the COVID-19 pandemic period. ClimateChat-300K provides an open resource for reproducible and interdisciplinary research on polarization, misinformation, and the dynamics of digital climate discourse. By releasing this dataset, we aim to support transparent, data-driven research and contribute to a deeper un-derstanding of how public engagement with climate issues develops across time, geography, and institutional contexts.

Abstract: The integration of large language models into political discourse analysis creates new opportunities for comparative research, policy analysis, and civic technology, while introducing material risks for democratic accountability. This paper argues that cultural adaptation is a prerequisite for trustworthy deployment of large language models in political communication across diverse linguistic and institutional contexts. Current systems remain shaped by English dominant data, uneven multilingual coverage, and assumptions grounded in a narrow range of political institutions and discourse conventions, producing systematic errors when applied across cultures. We formalize cultural adaptation across translation, discourse, and ontology levels, identify recurring cultural failure modes in political NLP, and propose an operational evaluation matrix grounded in cultural fidelity, calibration, and democratic safety. We conclude by clarifying governance constraints and scope conditions under which culturally adaptive political NLP can support democratic legitimacy.

### [98] [From Correctness to Preference: A Framework for Personalized Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23382)
*Ranxu zhang,zeyang li,Jiacheng Huang,Rui Zhang,Xiaozhou Xu,sun zhe,Yanyong Zhang,Chao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种统一的个性化智能体强化学习框架PARPO，通过解耦通用任务奖励与个性化偏好奖励，并引入用户特定锚点稳定学习，结合偏好解耦奖励模型和偏好对齐技能演化图记忆，实现个性化行为优化。在ETAPP、ETAPP-Hard和SJAgent上实验表明该方法显著优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PARPO框架，解耦通用任务质量奖励与个性化偏好奖励，使用用户特定锚点稳定学习；设计两阶段偏好解耦奖励模型和偏好对齐技能演化图记忆（PSGM），构建偏好识别、策略优化与结构化技能积累的闭环系统。

Conclusion: 该框架成功将个性化嵌入训练过程，实现了对用户偏好的有效建模与适应，为复杂现实场景中的个性化智能体行为提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning (Agentic RL) has achieved strong progress in tasks with clear success signals. However, many real-world agent applications require user-conditioned behavior: the same query may call for different planning strategies and tool-use decisions across users. This setting raises key challenges: generic rewards cannot capture heterogeneous user preferences, observed behaviors are entangled with conformity effects, and flat memories cannot support personalized skill retrieval. To this end, we propose a unified personalized Agentic RL framework that embeds personalization into training-time optimization. At its core is \emph{Personalized Anchor Reward-Decoupled Policy Optimization} (\textbf{PARPO}), which decouples generic task-quality rewards from personalized preference rewards and uses user-specific anchors to stabilize learning under heterogeneous reward scales. We further introduce a two-stage preference-disentangled reward model and \emph{Preference-Aligned Skill Evolution Graph Memory} (\textbf{PSGM}) for personalized supervision and preference-aligned skill retrieval. Together, they form a closed loop of preference identification, policy optimization, and structured skill accumulation. Experiments on ETAPP, ETAPP-Hard, and SJAgent show that our framework consistently outperforms strong memory and RL baselines. Code and data are included in the supplementary materials.

### [99] [Metacognition as Reward: Reinforcing LLM Reasoning via Knowledge and Regulation Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23384)
*Sirui Chen,Lei Xu,Yuying Zhao,Yutian Chen,Yu Wang,Beier Zhu,Hanwang Zhang,Shengjie Zhao,Chaochao Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Metacognition-as-Reward（MaR）框架，通过元认知知识与元认知调控两个通用过程维度，引导大模型推理，实现无需特定实例的奖励设计，提升推理质量与泛化能力。在22个基准测试中表现优异，最高较基线提升7.7%，较DAPO提升11.0%，且在跨领域数据集上仍具优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法在大模型推理中的奖励设计存在局限：RLVR仅依赖最终结果反馈，缺乏对中间推理过程的指导；RaR虽能评估推理质量但需大量人工设计的评分标准。因此需要一种无需定制化规则、能有效引导推理过程的通用奖励机制。

Method: 引入元认知启发的奖励框架MaR，将推理过程分解为元认知知识（识别任务相关信 息）和元认知调控（规划与调整推理流程）两个维度，构建基于轨迹层面的奖励函数，综合考虑任务知识覆盖率、调控一致性与答案正确性，通过强化学习优化推理过程。

Result: 在22个基准测试中，MaR显著提升模型性能，最大提升达7.7%（相比基线）和11.0%（相比DAPO）；Qwen3.5-9B + MaR超越GPT-OSS-120B整体表现，并在多个任务上优于更强模型；过程分析显示推理质量明显改善，且在域外数据集上具有良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: MaR通过通用的元认知维度提供过程导向的奖励信号，有效提升了大模型的推理能力与可解释性，是一种高效、可扩展且具备强泛化能力的强化学习训练范式。

Abstract: Recent RL methods have substantially improved the reasoning abilities of LLMs. Existing reward designs mainly follow two paradigms: (1) Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) derives outcome signals from executable checks or ground-truth answers, but provides limited guidance for intermediate reasoning behaviors. (2) Rubrics-as-reward (RaR) goes beyond final-answer checking by using natural-language rubrics to assess reasoning quality and task compliance, but often requires instance-specific rubrics and substantial design effort. To address these issues, we introduce Metacognition-as-Reward (MaR), a metacognition-inspired RL framework that guides LLM reasoning through two general process dimensions: i) metacognitive knowledge, which identifies task-relevant information without hand-crafted instance-specific rubrics, and ii) metacognitive regulation, which plans and adjusts the reasoning process to provide reward guidance beyond final-answer outcomes. MaR scaffolds model rollouts into explicit metacognitive components and optimizes them with a trajectory-level reward over task knowledge coverage, regulation fidelity, and final-answer correctness. In this way, MaR extends reward feedback to reasoning trajectories while grounding the reward signals in general metacognitive dimensions. Experiments on 22 benchmarks show that MaR consistently improves model performance, achieving up to a 7.7% gain over the base model and up to an 11.0% gain over vanilla DAPO. Notably, Qwen3.5-9B + MaR narrows the gap to frontier models, surpassing GPT-OSS-120B on overall average and outperforming stronger models on several individual benchmarks. Process-level analysis further shows substantial improvements in reasoning process quality. MaR also generalizes to out-of-domain datasets, where MaR-trained models improve over their corresponding base models on average.

</details>


### [100] [EquiSumm : A Gender Bias-Aware Framework for Inclusive Tweet Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23412)
*Chaitanya Wanjari,Jessica Kamal,Riddhi Jain,Samruddhi Kurhe,Roshni Chakraborty*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出EquiSumm，一种在生成社交媒体新闻事件摘要时考虑性别代表性的自动摘要方法，以解决现有方法中缺乏人口统计学公平性的问题。实验表明，该方法在两个主要数据集上相较于现有研究具有更好的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动摘要技术虽能有效浓缩大量推文内容，但未显式考虑性别等人口统计学因素，导致摘要可能产生偏见，无法公平反映不同群体的观点。

Method: 提出EquiSumm方法，通过引入性别维度的公平性约束，在生成摘要时确保不同性别的观点得到均衡表达。

Result: 在两个主要数据集上的实验结果表明，EquiSumm在摘要质量和代表性方面优于现有方法，有效提升了摘要的公平性与信息全面性。

Conclusion: EquiSumm通过显式考虑性别代表性，显著改善了社交媒体摘要的公平性，为构建更公正、全面的自动化信息摘要系统提供了有效解决方案。

However, these algorithms do not explicitly consider demographic fairness. Several existing research works have developed automated summarization approaches that can provide a holistic overview of the key aspects and major opinions shared on social media platforms related to a news event. However, these approaches do not explicitly consider different forms of demographic representation, such as gender, which can lead to biased summary representation.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于解决方案匹配的框架，通过比较不同回应间的相似性来衡量社会规范一致性；定义了‘陈述同意准确率’和‘显式同意准确率’两种指标；构建包含3000个社会困境的丹麦语数据集，每个困境由三位文化背景评委提供参考解答；在模拟自然对话的交互设置中评估人类与大模型的回应一致性。

Result: 所提指标在不同大模型间产生了稳定且一致的排名；结果显示，在邻里冲突和共居等情境中，回应间的一致性更高；说明该框架能有效捕捉文化背景下的社会推理特征，并揭示不同类型社会困境的差异性。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了一个面向自然开放式对话的文化根基社会推理评估框架与数据集，支持跨主体（人-人、人-模型、模型-模型）的一致性测量，为未来研究社会规范与人工智能行为对齐提供了新工具。

Abstract: Social norms reflect shared expectations on acceptable behavior. Measuring social norms alignment remains challenging, with existing approaches typically relying on artificial closed-form evaluations such as multiple-choice questionnaires or measuring agreement with predefined statements. In the context of this work, social norms alignment refers to measuring an agreement between solutions with respect to the social problem or dilemma. We propose a framework for measuring social norm alignment in naturalistic, free-form settings through solution matching. The framework enables us to measure alignment between any two dilemma responses e.g., LLMs to a human, LLMs to LLMs, or human to human. We introduce two metrics: stated and explicit agreement accuracy, and construct a dataset of 3k non-trivial social dilemmas in Danish. All dilemmas are assigned reference solutions derived from three panelists, who serve as culturally grounded judges. We evaluate the agreement of several LLMs and human responses in an interaction setup that resembles natural user-model conversations. Our results show that the proposed metrics produce consistent model rankings and reveal variation in agreement across different types of dilemmas, with higher agreement observed for topics such as neighbor conflicts and shared living situations. Overall, our work introduces a dataset and evaluation framework for studying culturally grounded social reasoning in naturalistic open-ended conversations.

### [102] [SSDAU: Structured Semantic Data Augmentation for Joint Entity and Relation Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23440)
*Jiawei He,Mengyu Shi,Chunrong Fang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为结构化语义数据增强（SSDAU）的新方法，旨在解决联合实体与关系抽取（JERE）因低质量训练数据导致的泛化能力弱的问题。SSDAU通过基于实体标签分割文本、利用编码器捕捉上下文感知的实体语义特征，并进行实体语义重构来生成高质量的增强数据。为区分语义相似的实体，融合了上下文嵌入与传统相似度得分；同时采用BERTTopic模型过滤无关主题，确保主题一致性。实验表明，SSDAU在多种标注类型的数据集上显著优于七种主流基线方法，在抗歧义性方面表现更优（F1下降仅8.26% vs. 基线31.91%），全面提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据增强方法常忽略文本相关性，破坏语义结构和依赖关系，导致生成的数据无法有效提升模型泛化能力。因此需要一种能保持语义结构的同时生成高质量增强数据的方法。

Method: SSDAU首先根据实体标签对文本进行分段，使用编码器获取上下文感知的实体语义特征；接着执行实体语义重构以生成新数据；通过融合上下文嵌入与传统相似度分数来区分语义相近的实体；并引入BERTTopic模型去除无关主题，保证主题一致性。

Result: 在多个具有不同标注类型的基准数据集上，SSDAU在五种代表性JERE模型上的表现均显著优于七种现有数据增强基线方法。其生成的数据在面对歧义时更具鲁棒性（F1下降仅8.26%，而基线平均达31.91%），整体性能全面提升。

Conclusion: SSDAU是一种有效的结构化语义数据增强方法，能够有效保留原始文本的语义结构，生成高质量且主题一致的增强数据，显著提升联合实体与关系抽取模型的泛化能力。

Abstract: Joint Entity and Relation Extraction (JERE) is highly susceptible to weak generalization due to low-quality training data.
  Data augmentation is a common strategy to enhance model generalization across different domains.
  However, existing data augmentation methods often overlook text relevance and may disrupt semantic structures and dependencies, making it difficult to generate effective augmented data for improving model generalization.
  In this paper, we propose Structured Semantic Data Augmentation (SSDAU), a novel method designed to preserve the semantic structure of text during augmentation.
  SSDAU segments text based on entity labels and employs an encoder to capture semantic features of entities through context awareness.
  It then performs entity semantic restructuring to generate augmented data.
  To distinguish semantically similar entities, SSDAU fuses contextualized embeddings with traditional similarity scores.
  To mitigate potential topic ambiguity and information loss, we apply the BERTTopic model to filter out irrelevant topics, ensuring topic consistency.
  We evaluate SSDAU on datasets with different annotation types and compare its performance on five representative JERE models against seven popular data augmentation baselines.
  Experiments demonstrate that SSDAU generates semantically consistent data with superior robustness against ambiguity (8.26\% F1 decrease vs.\ 31.91\% for baselines), significantly outperforming all existing methods across all metrics.

### [103] [ARES: Automated Rubric Synthesis for Scalable LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23454)

Method: ARES 从原始预训练文本出发，将知识转化为自包含的问答对，并联合生成问题特定的加权评分标准；通过引入领域标签和人物设定进行条件生成，提升多样性与相关性；应用多项验证过滤机制（如问题自洽性、答案忠实性、评分标准有效性）确保数据质量；最终实现大规模、高质量的鲁棒评分数据构建。

Conclusion: ARES 成功实现了基于评分标准的强化学习数据的大规模自动化构建，克服了传统方法在可扩展性和评估粒度上的局限，为大语言模型在复杂开放任务中的能力提升提供了有效支持。

Abstract: Rubric-based rewards offer a promising way to extend reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models beyond tasks with automatically verifiable answers. However, scaling rubric-based RL remains challenging: existing approaches often rely on expert-written rubrics and manually constructed question sets, while fixed task-level rubrics may fail to capture the evaluation requirements of individual questions. We propose ARES (Automated Rubric synthEsis for Scalable RL), a framework for automatically constructing rubric-based RL data at scale. Starting from raw pretraining documents, ARES converts source knowledge into self-contained question-answer pairs and co-generates question-specific weighted rubrics, enabling instance-level reward supervision for open-ended responses. To improve diversity and quality, ARES conditions generation on domain labels and persona information, and applies validation filters for question self-containment, answer faithfulness, and rubric validity. Using ARES, we construct 100K rubric-annotated instances across ten domains. Experiments on seven benchmarks show that rubric-based RL trained with ARES, outperforms continual pretraining, supervised fine-tuning, and binary-reward RL, with the largest gains on multi-dimensional open-ended tasks such as healthcare and instruction following.

Result: SGER achieves 99.02% accuracy and 0.994 F1 on a held-out set of 50,000 real-world pairs in Indian identity data, surpassing GPT-4o few-shot prompting and single-stage fine-tuning approaches.

Abstract: Matching person names across heterogeneous records is a core challenge in entity resolution, especially within linguistically and culturally complex environments. While Large Language Models have shown promise in understanding natural language, they often struggle with the structured ambiguity present in such domain-specific settings. This paper introduces Structure-Guided Entity Resolution (SGER), a novel framework that fine-tunes an LLM through a two-phase curriculum. The model is first trained to parse the grammatical and semantic structure of personal names, then optimized for the downstream task of binary entity matching. We evaluate SGER in the challenging context of Indian identity data, one of the most linguistically diverse and noisy environments globally. SGER achieves 99.02% accuracy and an F1 of 0.994 on a held-out set of 50,000 real-world pairs, outperforming GPT-4o few-shot prompting and single-stage fine-tuning baselines. Result: GE2 achieves first place on all tasks: BEIR avg.nDCG@10 = 0.638 and IT-RAG-Bench nDCG@10 = 0.282, but has high latency (231.6 ms). mE5-L closely matches GE2 on Italian task (within 0.003 nDCG) with only 31 ms latency. A more striking finding concerns LaBSE, which, despite widespread multilingual deployment scores 0.188 average nDCG@10 on BEIR, below every dedicated retrieval model including mMPNet. Chunking experiments show that all six models saturate at 32-token chunks on our corpus, with semantic chunking providing measurable gains only at 16 tokens.

### [106] [How Human-Like Are Large Language Models? A Register-Aware Linguistic Evaluation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23651)
*Björn Nieth,Marianna Gracheva,Michaela Mahlberg,Bjoern Eskofier,Emmanuelle Salin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种上下文感知的评估框架，通过比较大型语言模型（LLM）生成文本与人类参考语料库在67个词汇语法特征上的分布差异，评估生成文本的人类相似性。采用最大均值差异（MMD）方法，在五个不同语域的英语数据集上测试七个指令微调的开源模型。结果显示，所有模型均偏离人类基准，但最接近人类语言的模型因语域而异，且不取决于模型规模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管事实正确性和任务表现是大语言模型研究的重点，但其生成文本在语言层面是否具有人类特性仍缺乏深入探索。语言使用本质上依赖于语境，不同交际语境下语言特征的频率和共现模式存在差异，即使内容正确，若不符合这些模式，也会降低可读性。因此需要一种能衡量生成文本与人类语言一致性的评估方法。

Method: 提出基于双样本检验的上下文感知评估框架，利用最大均值差异（MMD）量化LLM生成文本与人类语料库在Biber提出的67个词法-语法特征上的分布差异，以评估人类似性。

Result: 所有测试的LLM模型在不同语域下均显著偏离人类基准；最接近人类语言的模型因语域而异，且模型大小并非决定因素。

Conclusion: 语言模型生成文本的人类相似性高度依赖于具体语域，不能仅通过模型规模判断。该研究为评估大语言模型的语言自然性提供了新的、基于语境的量化方法。

Abstract: While factual correctness and task-performance have been in focus of Large Language Model (LLM) research for a long time, the fundamental question of how human-like generated texts are on a linguistic level has been underexplored. From a corpus-linguistic perspective, language production is inherently context-dependent, with distinct communicative contexts giving rise to differences in frequencies and co-occurrence patterns of linguistic features. A text failing to adhere to these patterns can be content-wise correct, but still be unfavorable to human readers. In this work, we propose a context-aware evaluation framework in which human-likeness is assessed using a two-sample problem between the linguistic feature distribution of a human reference corpus for a given register and a corresponding LLM-generated corpus. We implement this framework using the Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) and the 67 lexico-grammatical features introduced by Biber, which are commonly applied in corpus linguistics. In our experiments, we compare seven instruction-tuned, open-source models across five English-language datasets spanning distinct registers against a human baseline. While across all tested setups, LLMs deviate from the human baseline, which models are closest to human language depends on the register and is not dictated by model size.

### [107] [OpenSkillEval: Automatically Auditing the Open Skill Ecosystem for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23657)
*Jiahao Ying,Boxian Ai,Wei Tang,Siyuan Liu,Yixin Cao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 	extsc{OpenSkillEval}，一个用于评估技能增强型智能体系统及其技能的自动化评估框架。该框架通过动态生成真实世界应用中的任务实例（涵盖演示文稿生成、前端网页设计、海报生成、数据可视化和报告生成等五类），并基于超过600个任务实例与30个开源技能进行系统性评估，揭示了技能可用性不等于有效使用，技能增益高度依赖于底层模型与智能体框架，且许多流行技能并不优于无技能基线。研究强调了动态、任务驱动评估的重要性，并为技能的设计、选择与部署提供了实践指导。

Method: 提出 \textsc{OpenSkillEval} 框架，自动从五个下游应用领域的实时演化真实产物中构建动态任务实例；收集社区贡献的技能，在统一任务设置下进行可控比较；采用大规模动态任务与多模型/框架组合进行系统评估。

Result: 发现技能可用性并不保证有效使用；技能增益显著依赖于具体模型与智能体框架；大量公开流行的技能并未持续优于无技能基线；验证了动态、任务驱动评估的必要性。

Conclusion: \textsc{OpenSkillEval} 证明了在真实任务背景下评估技能的重要性，强调应避免盲目依赖热门技能，而需结合具体应用场景、模型能力和框架特性进行精细化选型与部署，为未来技能生态系统的发展提供关键参考。

Abstract: Skills, i.e., structured workflow instructions distilled for large language models (LLMs), are becoming an increasingly important mechanism for improving agent performance on real-world downstream tasks. However, as the open-source skill ecosystem rapidly expands, it remains unclear how different models and agent frameworks interact with skills, how to evaluate skill quality, and how users should select skills under practical cost-performance trade-offs. In this paper, we present \textsc{OpenSkillEval}, an automatic evaluation framework for both skill-augmented agent systems and the skills themselves. Instead of relying on static benchmarks, \textsc{OpenSkillEval} automatically constructs realistic task instances from evolving real-world artifacts across five categories of downstream applications: presentation generation, front-end web design, poster generation, data visualization, and report generation. It further collects and organizes community-contributed skills for controlled comparison under unified task settings. Using more than 600 dynamically generated task instances and 30 open-source skills, we conduct a systematic evaluation of state-of-the-art models and agent frameworks. Our results show that skill availability does not guarantee effective skill usage, that the benefit of skill augmentation depends strongly on both the underlying model and the agent framework, and that many publicly popular skills do not consistently outperform base agents without skills. These findings highlight the need for dynamic, task-grounded evaluation and provide practical insights into the design, selection, and deployment of skills for LLM agents. Additional cases and benchmark resources are available on the project website: https://yingjiahao14.github.io/OpenSkillEval-Web/.

*Jiangwang Chen,Bowen Zhang,Zixin Song,Jiazheng Kang,Xiao Yang,Da Zhu,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出OnePred，一种用于主动对话系统中预测用户下一步查询的方法。通过递归更新的记忆机制，仅用少量上下文实现高效且准确的预测，显著降低每轮令牌消耗（最高达22倍），同时在长对话中表现更优。作者还构建了NQP-Bench基准测试集，验证方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型对话系统是被动响应式的，无法主动预测用户后续问题。现有方法在完整历史与截断历史之间存在效率-质量权衡，缺乏专门的评估基准。因此需要一种既能保持高质量预测又具备高效率的方法。

Method: 提出OnePred框架，利用递归更新的记忆作为唯一的跨轮次上下文，避免重复读取原始对话历史；采用两阶段强化学习训练策略，分别学习预测目标和压缩方式，使记忆演变为面向预测的意图链。

Result: 实验表明，OnePred相比全历史输入将每轮令牌消耗减少最多22倍，且在所有基线中均取得更高预测精度，尤其在长对话中优势更明显。

Conclusion: OnePred实现了高效与高质量之间的良好平衡，为实现真正的主动对话系统提供了可行路径，并通过新构建的NQP-Bench基准推动该领域研究发展。

Abstract: Although large language model (LLM) conversational systems process millions of multi-turn dialogues daily, they remain fundamentally reactive: they respond only after the user types a query. A key step toward proactive interaction is next-query prediction, which anticipates the user's subsequent query based solely on the preceding dialogue. Progress on this task is hindered by the lack of dedicated benchmarks and a fundamental efficiency--quality trade-off: naively concatenating full dialogue history incurs linearly growing token consumption, while truncating to the latest turn discards crucial cross-turn context. Our key insight is that accurate prediction does not require re-reading raw history; it suffices to track the user's evolving intent trajectory across topics, unresolved needs, and interest shifts. We propose OnePred, which maintains a recursively updated memory as its sole cross-turn context, bounding the per-turn cost independently of conversation length. We train the model via a two-stage reinforcement learning pipeline that first teaches what to predict, then what to compress, shaping the memory into a prediction-oriented intent chain. To establish a rigorous testbed, we introduce NQP-Bench, spanning three diverse subsets. Experiments demonstrate that OnePred reduces per-turn token consumption by up to 22$\times$ compared to full-history inputs while consistently exceeding all baselines in prediction quality, with larger gains on longer conversations. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/ZBWpro/OnePred.

</details>


### [109] [ChartFI: Benchmarking Faithfulness and Insightfulness of Chart Descriptions from Multimodal Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23694)
*Fen Wang,Zekai Shao,Qiman Kang,Chunran Hu,Zhixuan Zhang,Lexu Xie,Chao Liu,Siming Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出ChartFI-Bench，一个用于评估图表描述生成质量的基准测试，涵盖事实准确性、显著特征强调、领域知识指导和图表-文本互补性四个维度。该基准包含896个复杂图表与丰富描述对，并设计了四个对应评估指标：忠实度、覆盖度、信息量和敏锐度，以系统评估多模态大模型的表现。实验揭示现有模型在描述质量上的普遍不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前图表描述生成的基准数据集过于简单，描述内容浅显；评估指标无法全面反映描述质量的多维特性，因此亟需更高质量的评测体系。

Method: 基于四个关键维度（事实准确性、显著特征强调、领域知识指导、图表-文本互补性）构建高质量的图表描述数据集，包含896个复杂图表与语义丰富的描述对，并设计四个匹配的评估指标：忠实度、覆盖度、信息量和敏锐度。

Result: 所提出的框架有效提升了对图表描述质量的评估能力，实验表明主流多模态大模型在描述忠实性和洞察力方面存在明显缺陷。

Conclusion: ChartFI-Bench为评估多模态大语言模型在图表描述任务中的表现提供了系统化、多维度的评测标准，有助于推动该领域向更精准、更具洞察力的方向发展。

Abstract: Chart descriptions are essential for accessibility, cross-modal retrieval, and assisting readers in extracting insights from complex visualizations. As multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly adopted for automated chart description generation, a critical question arises: how faithfully and insightfully do these models actually describe charts? Current benchmarks fall short on two fronts: existing datasets consist of simple, homogeneous charts paired with shallow, fact-enumerating descriptions; and prevailing metrics fail to capture the multi-faceted nature of description quality. To address these gaps, we present the Chart Faithfulness and Insightfulness Benchmark (ChartFI-Bench). We first summarize four dimensions that characterize high-quality chart descriptions: factual accuracy, salient feature emphasis, domain-informed guidance, and chart-text complementarity. Guided by these dimensions, we construct a high-quality benchmark comprising 896 chart-description pairs, which feature visually complex charts and semantically rich descriptions. Furthermore, we design four aligned evaluation metrics -- Faithfulness, Coverage, Informativeness, and Acuity -- to systematically assess the quality of descriptions across these dimensions. Experiments conducted on mainstream MLLMs demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework and reveal common weaknesses among existing models.

</details>


### [110] [Metadata Predictability Is Not Evidence Dependence: An Intervention-Based Audit for Weak-Label Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23701)
*Kan Shao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种协议级测试方法，用于评估弱标签基准数据集的可靠性，通过干预证据来检验模型输出是否敏感。结合元数据统计（MPDS）与证据干预统计（ΔEvi），揭示了仅依赖元数据筛选的局限性。实验表明，即使元数据主导性中等，证据干预仍可能无变化，说明需同时考虑证据敏感性和模型校准。建议在基准审计中报告元数据筛查、证据干预和读者校准三者结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有弱标签基准测试主要依赖元数据预测能力，但无法检测模型对真实证据的依赖程度。为更准确评估模型是否真正理解证据，需引入证据干预机制，以检验模型输出是否随证据变化而变化。

Method: 提出结合元数据优先主导得分（MPDS）与证据干预差异（ΔEvi）的联合评估方法。通过跨项目打乱证据身份，测量模型输出的变化，同时分析元数据对预测的影响力，并在多个模型和数据集上进行验证。

Result: 合成版HotpotQA显示，尽管MPDS为0.643（中等），ΔEvi为0，说明模型未真正依赖证据；强阅读器重运行发现校准问题导致结果反转，部分任务进入“问题主导”警告区域；FEVER表现良好，具有强证据敏感性。

Conclusion: 基准测试应整合元数据筛选、证据干预测试和模型校准评估，才能全面反映模型的真实能力，避免误判。

Abstract: We study a protocol-level test for weak-label benchmarks: whether benchmark outputs change when the provided evidence is intervened on. Metadata-only shortcut checks answer a different question, namely whether outputs are predictable from metadata priors. We therefore combine a metadata statistic, the Metadata Prior Dominance Score (MPDS), with an evidence-intervention statistic, ΔEvi, measuring sensitivity to evidence identity under cross-item shuffling. Synthetic HotpotQA gives a constructed counterexample to metadata-only screening: MPDS is only moderate (0.643), yet ΔEvi is zero. Stronger-reader reruns show why calibration belongs in the test procedure: SNLI shows a calibration reversal, reconstructed HotpotQA occupies a question-dominant warning region, and FEVER is a strongly evidence-sensitive positive control across four transformers. The practical lesson is simple: benchmark audits should report metadata-only screening, evidence intervention, and reader-strength calibration together.

</details>


### [111] [A graph-based analysis of semantic types and coercion in contextualized word embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23710)
*Long Chen,Deniz Ekin Yavas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于图的方法，利用BERT和语义增强嵌入分析词嵌入中词汇与上下文类型信息的反映情况。通过选取十类语义类型的名词，标注语料库中的类型匹配（匹配、强制、其他不匹配、无限制），构建图模型并引入邻居类型概率（NTP）和邻居类型熵（NTE）两个指标，结果显示语义增强嵌入构建的图更能反映语义类型信息，且能有效区分匹配与不匹配句子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究名词与其上下文之间的语义类型不匹配在强制现象中的核心作用，探索如何通过词嵌入捕捉这种类型信息。

Method: 选取十类语义类型的名词，对语料库实例进行类型匹配标注（匹配、强制、其他不匹配、无限制），使用BERT和语义增强嵌入构建图模型，并计算邻居类型概率（NTP）和邻居类型熵（NTE）以分析邻域类型分布。

Result: 语义增强嵌入构建的图能更准确地反映语义类型信息；所提出的NTP和NTE指标可有效区分匹配与不匹配句子。

Conclusion: 语义增强嵌入在捕捉词汇与上下文类型关系方面表现更优，基于图的分析方法结合NTP和NTE指标为理解强制现象提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Semantic type mismatch between a noun and its context is central to coercion phenomena. This paper introduces a graph-based method to examine how lexical and contextual type information is reflected in word embeddings. We select nouns from ten semantic types, annotate corpus instances for type matching (matching vs. coercion vs. other mismatch vs. unrestricted), and construct graphs using BERT and sense-enhanced embeddings. Two metrics -- Neighbor Type Probability (NTP) and Neighbor Type Entropy (NTE) -- are proposed to analyze neighborhood type distributions. Results show that graphs constructed with sense-enhanced embeddings reflect semantic type information better, and matching and mismatch sentences can be distinguished through the proposed metrics.

</details>

*Ehud Reiter*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To reflect on the evolution of NLG evaluation methods and anticipate future directions as NLG integrates more deeply into everyday use.

Method: Historical analysis of NLG evaluation practices across decades, with projection based on current trends in machine learning and societal adoption.

Result: Evaluation has shifted from linguistics-based to machine learning-driven; future focus will be on real-world impact, qualitative nuances, and safety.

Conclusion: As NLG technologies become pervasive, evaluation must expand beyond accuracy to include ethical, societal, and user-centered dimensions.

Abstract: Natural Language Generation (NLG) evaluation has changed dramatically since 1990, and will continue to evolve in the future. In 1990, when NLG had close ties to linguistics, there was very little formal experimental evaluation in the modern sense. In 2026, when NLG is closely linked to machine learning, experimental evaluation is expected and indeed fundamental to research. Many evaluation techniques were developed over this period, including most recently LLM-as-Judge. I expect NLG evaluation will continue to evolve in the future. In particular, impact, qualitative, and safety evaluation will become more important as large numbers of people routinely use NLG technology.

### [113] [Is a Document Educational or Just Wikipedia-Style? -- Pitfalls of Classifier-Based Quality Filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23721)
*Mateusz Klimaszewski,Piotr Andruszkiewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了基于分类器的质量过滤方法在构建预训练语料库中的一个关键漏洞：简单的维基百科式重排操作可显著改变模型对内容质量的评估，导致低质量内容绕过过滤阈值。实验表明，FineWeb-Edu CQF模型约有7%的文档会因此改变过滤决策，使本应被排除的内容进入语料库。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提升预训练语料库的质量，研究者采用基于分类器的过滤方法替代传统启发式规则。然而，该方法可能存在隐蔽的脆弱性，亟需评估其鲁棒性。

Method: 通过实施类似于维基百科的文本重排操作，系统性地测试分类器对文本质量判断的敏感性，并分析其在不同重排模式下的过滤决策变化。

Result: 发现经过简单重排后的文本能显著改变分类器的判断结果，导致原本应被过滤的低质量内容被错误接受，其中约7%的文档改变了原有过滤决策。

Conclusion: 基于分类器的质量过滤虽高效，但对文本格式高度敏感，存在被简单重排操纵的风险，需引入更鲁棒的评估机制以保障预训练数据质量。

Abstract: Classifier-based Quality Filtering has recently emerged as a fundamental technique in constructing pre-training corpora. The ability to deploy a single model that can replace or supplement a set of heuristics has proven effective across numerous Large Language Models. In this work, we expose a critical vulnerability in this approach by demonstrating how a straightforward Wikipedia-style reformatting operation can substantially alter a model's quality assessment and enable low-quality content to surpass filtering thresholds. Our analysis reveals that the FineWeb-Edu CQF model would reverse its filtering decision for approximately 7% of evaluated documents, thereby admitting content into the pre-training corpus that would otherwise have been excluded.

</details>


### [114] [Hierarchical Concept Geometry in Language Models Emerges from Word Co-occurrence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23821)
*Andres Nava,Matthieu Wyart*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种关于语义上位关系（即“是-一种”关系）在语言表征中几何编码的分布理论。基于词语在WordNet上越接近则共现频率越高的经验假设，理论分析了word2vec嵌入的词频共现矩阵谱特性。在共现核满足温和正性与衰减条件下，证明主特征向量首先区分大类分类分支，再逐步细化子分支，形成类似树状结构的层次分裂几何，具有从粗到细的谱组织特征。实验验证了该预测在多个WordNet子树中的有效性，并发现该特征在Gemma 2B的解码嵌入中也显著存在。结果表明，大型语言模型中的层次概念几何结构并非依赖特定层级机制，而是源于词语统计相关性的谱结构本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解语言模型中层次化语义结构如何由底层统计特性生成，特别是上位关系（hypernymy）在嵌入空间中的几何表现。

Method: 基于共现频率与图距离的关系假设，构建并分析词嵌入的Gram矩阵谱性质；通过理论推导证明其特征值分解具有分层结构；在WordNet子树及Gemma 2B解码嵌入中进行实证验证。

Result: 主特征向量呈现出从粗到细的层次分裂模式，与WordNet树结构高度一致；该谱结构在不同模型和数据集上均稳定存在，表明其源于通用统计规律而非特定设计。

Conclusion: 语言模型中的层次语义结构可自然地从词频共现的谱特性中涌现，无需专门的层级机制支持，说明其本质是统计相关性的几何体现。

Abstract: We propose a distributional theory of how hypernymy -- the ``is-a'' relation between general and specific concepts -- is encoded geometrically in language representations. Starting from the empirically verified assumption that words closer on the WordNet hypernym graph co-occur more often, we characterize theoretically the spectrum of the resulting embedding Gram matrix of word2vec embeddings. Under mild positivity and decay conditions on the co-occurrence kernel, we prove that the leading eigenvectors first separate broad taxonomic branches and then progressively finer sub-branches, producing a \emph{hierarchical splitting geometry} with a coarse-to-fine spectral organization that mirrors the tree. We confirm these predictions in word2vec embeddings across many sampled WordNet subtrees, and show that the same signature extends strikingly well to Gemma 2B unembeddings. Our results indicate that hierarchical concept geometry in LLMs need not reflect a hierarchy-specific functional mechanism, but emerges from the spectral structure of pairwise word statistics.

</details>


### [115] [Multilingual Knowledge Transfer under Data Constraints via Lexical Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23885)
*Anastasiia Sedova,Natalie Schluter,Skyler Seto,Maartje ter Hoeve*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LINK 是一种数据级干预方法，通过在预训练数据中使用双语词汇对高资源语言（如英语）的文本进行词级替换，以提升跨语言知识迁移效果。该方法无需额外模型训练或大量平行数据，仅需双语词汇表，可低成本应用于多种语言。在8种语言、5种模型规模上的实验表明，其在目标语言下游任务上表现显著提升，甚至可实现训练速度提升2倍以达到相同性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低资源语言缺乏足够训练数据的情况下，跨语言知识迁移对于构建高性能多语言语言模型至关重要。然而，现有方法通常依赖大量平行数据、翻译系统或额外训练阶段，这些资源在许多语言中难以获取。因此，亟需一种简单、高效且无需额外训练的跨语言知识迁移方法。

Method: 提出LINK方法，通过在高资源语言（如英语）的预训练数据中，随机选择部分词语并用其双语词汇表中的对应翻译词进行替换，从而在预训练阶段引入目标语言的知识表示。该方法不涉及模型训练，仅需一个双语词汇表，成本极低。

Result: 在8种不同语言和5种模型规模下的评估显示，该方法在目标语言的下游任务中均取得显著性能提升，且训练收敛速度加快，最快可实现2倍的加速效果，达到与基线模型相当的性能。

Conclusion: LINK是一种高效、低成本且无需额外训练的跨语言知识迁移方法，通过简单的词级替换策略，在预训练阶段即有效增强了低资源语言的表示能力，为多语言模型在资源匮乏语言上的应用提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Cross-lingual knowledge transfer is critical for building high-performing multilingual language models for languages with insufficient training data. When target language data is scarce, the knowledge required for many downstream tasks involving scientific reasoning, commonsense inference, and world knowledge must be acquired primarily from the high-resource language, making effective knowledge transfer essential. Existing methods for improving such cross-lingual knowledge transfer require large amounts of parallel data, translation systems, auxiliary models, or additional training stages that are largely unavailable for many languages. We propose LINK - a data-level intervention method that improves knowledge transfer during model pretraining through lexical substitutions in high-resource part of pretraining data using bilingual vocabularies. For a given replacement ratio, randomly selected words in a portion of the high-resource (English) training corpus are swapped with their word-level translations, requiring no additional model training and only a bilingual vocabulary, which can be obtained at near-zero cost for virtually any language. Evaluation on eight languages across five model sizes shows notable improvements on downstream tasks in the target language, with up to a 2x speedup in training to reach equivalent performance.

</details>

### [116] [Reading Calibrated Uncertainty from Language Model Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22864)
*Aliai Eusebi,Alexander Herzog,Xiaoyu Liang,Marie Vasek,Enrico Mariconti,Lorenzo Cavallaro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于模型内部激活路径几何特征的不确定性量化方法，通过追踪每一层MLP更新的累积轨迹，提取11个尺度不变的几何特征，并使用稀疏线性探测器进行建模。相比传统的最大softmax概率（MSP），该方法在选择性拒绝任务中表现更优，提升最高达21 AURC点，且其可解释性强，能揭示错误在哪些层级提前形成、发生矛盾或轨迹偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统最大softmax概率（MSP）虽计算高效但常出现校准偏差；现有方法依赖静态隐藏状态，忽略表示形成过程中的层间动态演化，而不同路径可能产生相似终点，因此需捕捉证据积累与变化的深层机制以揭示被最终概率掩盖的不确定性。

Method: 从每层MLP的更新中提取11个尺度不变的几何特征，用于表征激活路径的累积演化；将这些特征输入稀疏线性探测器，实现对不确定性的有效建模。

Result: 所提方法在选择性拒绝任务中显著优于MSP，AURC提升最高达21点，且提升幅度随基线校准偏差增大而增强；模型系数具有明确几何意义，可定位错误形成的层次位置及路径异常。

Conclusion: 通过分析模型内部表示形成的动态路径，结合几何特征与可解释性探测器，能够更准确地识别语言模型生成中的不确定性，为可信生成提供新工具。

Abstract: The maximum softmax probability (MSP) represents a default approach when evaluating uncertainty quantification for language model generation with structured output. Although cheap, it is often miscalibrated. Methods that probe the model's internal activations feed raw hidden states into opaque classifiers, reading activations as static snapshots and leaving implicit the layer-wise trajectory by which a representation is formed. Yet, similar endpoints can arise from very different paths, and how evidence accumulates, reinforces, or reverses across depth might reveal uncertainty that final probabilities obscure. We extract eleven scale-invariant geometric features, tracing the cumulative path of per-layer MLP updates, and feed them to a sparse linear probe. The probe outperforms MSP under selective abstention, with gains scaling with baseline miscalibration up to 21 AURC points. Because every feature has a closed-form geometric meaning, the probe's coefficients trace how and where along depth errors take shape -- which layers commit prematurely, which contradict the running state, where trajectories drift away from their endpoint.

</details>


### [117] [FusionSense: Tri-Stage Near-Sensor Learning for Runtime-Adaptive Multimodal Edge Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22868)
*Sanggeon Yun,Ryozo Masukawa,Minhyoung Na,Hyunwoo Oh,Yoshiki Yamaguchi,Wenjun Huang,SungHeon Jeong,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FusionSense 是一种融合感知智能传感框架，旨在解决边缘计算中多模态传感器数据处理的能效与延迟问题。通过轻量级近传感器分类器和运行时决策机制，实现跨模态信息的有效利用，显著降低计算与通信开销，在保持任务性能的同时大幅减少数据传输量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自动驾驶和智能制造系统对边缘计算需求增加，如何在能源、延迟和可靠性约束下高效处理多模态传感器数据成为关键挑战。现有方法或在服务器端融合数据（导致高通信开销），或仅使用单模态过滤（忽略模态间依赖），造成冗余传输或漏检事件。

Method: 提出三步训练流程：(i) 服务器端训练融合模型以学习下游任务；(ii) 通过滤除安全标签（FoS）量化各模态对融合决策的必要性；(iii) 将近传感器预测作为辅助信号压缩边缘端融合模型，构建可扩展的运行时决策层。

Result: 在双模态（RGB+深度/激光雷达）设置下，FusionSense 在数据压缩率更高时仍保持任务质量，相比单模态滤波器，能耗降低达33倍（1%误报率）、11倍（10%），在固定30%数据压缩下质量损失减少92.3%，能效比最优基线提升约1.5倍。

Conclusion: FusionSense 实现了高效的多模态融合感知，兼顾低功耗、低延迟与高可靠性，适用于大规模部署的智能边缘系统。

Abstract: Autonomous systems and smart-industry deployments increasingly split computation across near-sensor, edge, and cloud resources, where tight energy, latency, and reliability budgets demand run-time adaptivity. In practice, deciding what to compute and transmit at each point is pivotal; yet as multimodal sensor suites (cameras, LiDAR/depth, etc.) proliferate at the edge, most prior approaches either (i) fuse modalities on powerful servers or (ii) apply uni-modal near-sensor filters that ignore cross-modal dependencies, leading to redundant transmissions or missed events. We present FusionSense, a fusion-aware intelligent sensing framework for energy-constrained autonomous edge systems. Lightweight near-sensor classifiers are trained via a three-step procedure: (i) a server-side fusion model learns the downstream task, (ii) filter-out-safe (FoS) labels quantify each modality's necessity relative to the fused decision, and (iii) an edge-side fusion model is compacted by injecting near-sensor predictions as auxiliary signals. The result is a run-time decision layer that jointly reduces compute and communication while scaling linearly with sensor count. On a dual-modality (RGB+Depth/LiDAR) setup with SynDrone, FusionSense sustains task quality at substantially higher data-reduction rates than uni-modal filters and delivers large end-to-end gains: up to 33x lower energy at 1% FoI prevalence, 11x at 10%, a 92.3% reduction in quality loss at a fixed 30% data reduction, and roughly 1.5x higher energy savings than the best prior filtering baseline.

</details>


### [118] [FuRA: Full-Rank Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning with Spectral Preconditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22869)
*Yequan Zhao,Ruijie Zhang,Liyan Tan,Niall Moran,Tong Qin,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FuRA（Full-Rank Adaptation）框架，通过块张量-列车分解实现全秩谱预处理，在保持全秩更新表达能力的同时，显著提升参数效率与性能。相比传统全微调（Full FT）和LoRA，FuRA在多个任务中表现更优，包括大模型推理、强化学习和视觉指令调优，并且4比特量化版本QFuRA也超越QLoRA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全微调和参数高效微调方法（如LoRA）未考虑预训练阶段建立的谱结构，导致有限微调数据下的噪声梯度会破坏鲁棒的预训练特征。因此需要引入谱预处理机制以约束权重更新方向，保持预训练特征稳定性。

Method: 采用全秩奇异值分解（SVD）重参数化权重矩阵，冻结一个奇异基，使更新限制在预训练列空间内；提出基于块张量-列车分解W = LSR的FuRA框架，其中大核心L固定为预训练块级SVD基，仅优化紧凑核心R和块级奇异值S，实现全秩谱预处理与高效计算。

Result: FuRA在多个任务上均优于全微调（Full FT）和LoRA，例如在LLaMA-3-8B常识推理任务中提升1.37分；在数学推理强化学习和视觉语言模型指令调优中表现优异；其4比特量化版本QFuRA亦超越QLoRA，兼具参数、内存和训练时间效率。

Conclusion: 谱预处理是提升微调性能的关键，FuRA通过全秩谱约束与高效参数设计，在不增加可训练参数的前提下实现了更强的泛化能力和稳定性，是一种高效且通用的微调新范式。

Abstract: Both full fine-tuning (Full FT) and parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods such as LoRA introduce weight updates without accounting for the spectral structure established during pretraining. As a result, noisy gradients from limited fine-tuning data can perturb robust pretrained features. We identify spectral preconditioning as the missing ingredient: reparameterizing each weight matrix through its full-rank singular value decomposition (SVD) and freezing one singular basis constrains updates to the pretrained column space, yielding a preconditioned optimization scheme that outperforms unconstrained Full FT at the same trainable parameter count. Building on this insight, we propose FuRA (Full-Rank Adaptation), an efficient full-rank adaptation framework based on a block tensor-train factorization W = LSR, where the large core L is fixed to the pretrained block-wise SVD basis, while only the compact core R and the block-wise singular values S are optimized. This design simultaneously provides full-rank spectral preconditioning, preserves full-rank update expressivity, and achieves parameter, memory, and step-time efficiency comparable to LoRA. FuRA consistently outperforms Full FT across multiple settings, including LLM fine-tuning (+1.37 on LLaMA-3-8B commonsense reasoning), LLM reinforcement learning for mathematical reasoning, and visual instruction tuning for VLMs. Furthermore, the 4-bit quantized variant, QFuRA, also surpasses QLoRA. Code is available at https://github.com/olokevin/FuRA-NIPS

</details>


### [119] [When Do LLMs Reason? A Dynamical Systems View via Entropy Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22873)
*Wei Xia,Haoqing Wang,Zhi-Hong Deng,Yehui Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了链式思维（CoT）推理在实际应用中的悖论：尽管广泛使用，但其对事实性和开放性任务的增益有限且消耗大量token。研究发现，大语言模型的推理能力并非静态属性，而是一种在生成过程中动态演变的解码状态。通过分析早期解码阶段的熵动态变化，发现受益于CoT的任务表现出稳定的熵下降趋势，而其他任务则呈现不稳定或上升模式，类似于相变过程——从高熵探索态转向低熵结构化推理态。基于此，提出EDRM（基于熵动态的推理流形）框架，一种无需训练、轻量级的推理策略自适应路由机制。EDRM将熵轨迹映射为紧凑可解释的流形表示，支持零样本部署和实例级精细调整。在15个基准测试和4种不同规模与架构的LLM上，EDRM持续优于静态基线，在数据集层面实现41–55%的token减少并提升准确率，仅需50个校准样本；在实例层面进一步提升准确率达4.7%，同时保持27–45%的token节省。结果表明，应选择性启用推理而非默认使用，并验证了熵驱动解码控制在高效自适应推理中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 链式思维（CoT）虽被广泛用于增强大语言模型（LLM）能力，但其实际效果存在显著局限，尤其在事实性和开放性任务中常带来边际甚至负面收益，同时大幅增加计算开销。这引发根本问题：何时显式推理真正有益？现有方法多采用固定策略，缺乏对推理必要性的动态判断依据。因此，亟需一种能够识别推理潜力并自适应调度推理策略的新机制。

Method: 通过系统分析大语言模型在生成过程中的早期解码熵动态，识别出推理状态的演化特征。发现受益于CoT的任务具有稳定的熵下降趋势，而无效任务则表现为熵波动或上升。据此提出EDRM框架，利用早期熵轨迹构建一个轻量、无需训练的推理流形表示，实现对推理策略的动态路由：根据熵动态信号自动决定是否启用CoT推理。该方法支持零样本部署与实例级精细化控制。

Result: EDRM在15个基准测试和4种不同规模/架构的LLM上均表现优异。在数据集层面，实现41–55%的token减少，同时提升准确率，仅需50个校准样本即可生效；在实例层面，准确率最高提升4.7%，并维持27–45%的token节省。实验验证了熵动态作为推理有效性的可靠预测信号，以及EDRM在提升效率与性能方面的显著优势。

Conclusion: 推理不应作为默认策略，而应根据任务动态需求选择性启用。本研究揭示了推理是解码过程中的动态状态，并提出基于熵动态的EDRM框架，实现了高效、可解释、自适应的推理调度。该方法不仅显著降低资源消耗，还提升了推理准确性，为大模型高效推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has become the default strategy for enhancing LLM capabilities, yet its application raises a fundamental question: when is explicit reasoning actually beneficial? Empirical evidence reveals a striking paradox: CoT often provides marginal or even negative gains on factual and open-ended tasks while multiplying token consumption. In this work, we show that LLM reasoning is not a static property of tasks or models, but a \emph{dynamic decoding state} that emerges during generation. Through systematic analysis, we find early-stage entropy dynamics provide a reliable signal of this state: tasks benefiting from CoT exhibit consistent entropy reduction, while others display unstable or increasing patterns. This behavior can be interpreted as a phase-transition-like shift from a high-entropy exploratory regime to a low-entropy structured reasoning regime. Based on these insights, we propose \textbf{EDRM} (Entropy Dynamics-based Reasoning Manifold), a lightweight and training-free routing framework that leverages early decoding entropy to adaptively select inference strategies. EDRM embeds entropy trajectories into a compact and interpretable manifold representation, enabling both zero-shot deployment and fine-grained instance-level adaptation. Across 15 benchmarks and 4 LLMs of varying scales and architectures, EDRM consistently outperforms static baselines. At the dataset level, EDRM achieves \textbf{41--55\%} token reduction while improving accuracy with as few as 50 calibration samples. At the instance level, it further improves accuracy by up to \textbf{4.7\%} while maintaining \textbf{27--45\%} token savings. These results suggest that reasoning should be invoked selectively rather than by default, and demonstrate the effectiveness of entropy-driven decoding control for efficient and adaptive LLM inference.

</details>


### [120] [WeCon: An Efficient Weight-Conditioned Neural Solver for Multi-Objective Combinatorial Optimization Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22876)
*Xuan Wu,Jinbiao Chen,Yang Li,Lijie Wen,Chunguo Wu,Yuanshu Li,Yubin Xiao,Chunyan Miao,You Zhou,Di Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: WeCon提出一种高效的权重条件神经求解器，通过改进的编码器和解码器结构缓解权重信号稀释问题，并引入高效偏好优化（EPO）生成高质量解对以提升训练效率。在多个MOCOP变体上的实验表明，WeCon在保持与SOTA方法POCCO-W相当的超体积（HV）表现的同时，推理时间减少40%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经求解器在处理多目标组合优化问题时，存在权重注入时机不当导致上下文建模不足或权重信号在解码阶段衰减的问题；同时，偏好优化依赖随机采样生成解对，信息量低，训练效率差。

Method: 设计包含三个注意力模块和门控残差融合（GRF）块的编码器层，促进实例特征与权重的协同交互；在解码器中引入可插拔残差融合（RF）块以缓解权重信号稀释；提出高效偏好优化（EPO）机制，生成高质量解对以增强训练有效性。

Result: 在四种MOCOP变体上验证，WeCon在多种规模和分布模式下达到与SOTA方法POCCO-W相当的超体积（HV）性能，推理时间降低40%；消融实验证明各组件的有效性。

Conclusion: WeCon通过创新的权重条件建模与高效训练策略，在保持高性能的同时显著提升推理效率，为多目标组合优化问题提供了更优的神经求解方案。

Abstract: Existing neural solvers for Multi-Objective Combinatorial Optimization Problems (MOCOPs) commonly adopt decomposition-based strategies that scalarize an MOCOP into multiple subproblems associated with distinct weight vectors. However, they either inject weights only once during decoding, limiting weight-conditioned context modeling, or primarily during encoding, causing weight-signal dilution during decoding. Moreover, preference optimization methods rely on purely random sampling to construct solution pairs for training solvers, which often produces less informative pairs and thus leads to low training effectiveness. To better address these limitations, we propose an efficient Weight-Conditioned neural solver (WeCon). Specifically, we design an encoder layer with three attention blocks and our proposed Gated Residual Fusion (GRF) block to facilitate harmonious interaction between instance features and weights, thereby generating informative weight-conditioned context. We further introduce a plug-and-play Residual Fusion (RF) block in the decoder to alleviate weight-signal dilution. Finally, we propose Efficient Preference Optimization (EPO), which constructs high-quality solutions, thereby generating more informative pairs to improve training effectiveness. Experiments on four MOCOP variants across different problem scales and distribution patterns demonstrate that WeCon achieves HyperVolume (HV) values comparable to SOTA solver POCCO-W, while reducing inference time by 40%. Ablation studies validate the contributions of all designs.

### [121] [Tensor Cache: Eviction-conditioned Associative Memory for Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22884)
*Kabir Swain,Sijie Han,Daniel Karl I. Weidele,Mauro Martino,Antonio Torralba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Tensor Cache 是一种两层缓存机制，结合滑动窗口注意力（L1）与固定大小的外积快速权重记忆（L2），通过压缩淘汰的KV对形成每层矩阵A，利用线性注意力恒等式实现高效长程依赖建模。通过可学习门控融合L1和L2输出，并端到端训练衰减与写入率参数。该方法在长上下文建模、记忆容量诊断和可控关联回忆任务中优于现有有界状态基线，显著提升内存-质量权衡性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自回归Transformer的KV缓存随上下文长度线性增长，而滑动窗口缓存虽限制内存但完全丢弃窗口外信息，导致重要证据不可访问。需要一种既能控制内存使用又能保留远距离相关信息的机制。

Method: 提出两层缓存结构：第一层为滑动窗口注意力，保留近期精确注意力；第二层为基于外积的快速权重记忆，接收从窗口中淘汰的KV对，将其压缩为每层矩阵A，未来查询通过单次矩阵乘法读取。利用线性注意力恒等式 $q_t(k_i \otimes v_i)=\langle q_t,k_i\rangle v_i$ 实现高效计算。引入可学习门控融合两层输出，并训练每头的衰减与写入率参数。修正了训练中因分块平均带来的 $C^2-C$ 个虚假交叉项问题，采用并行加权扫描实现接近逐令牌写入的精度。

Result: 在多个系统规模、可控关联回忆、长上下文语言建模及内存容量诊断任务中，Tensor Cache 显著优于现有有界状态基线模型，在内存使用受限的前提下实现了更高的性能表现，有效提升了内存与模型质量之间的平衡关系。

Conclusion: Tensor Cache 通过将滑动窗口淘汰的KV对以外积形式编码至固定大小的记忆矩阵，并利用线性注意力机制高效读取，实现了对长距离信息的有效保留。其两层结构与端到端训练策略在保持低内存开销的同时显著增强模型长期记忆能力，是当前长序列建模中极具潜力的优化方案。

Abstract: Autoregressive Transformer KV caches grow linearly with context length; sliding-window caching bounds memory but discards evicted tokens entirely, so relevant evidence outside the window becomes inaccessible. We introduce \emph{Tensor Cache}, a two-level cache that pairs sliding-window softmax attention as a first-level cache (L1) with a fixed-size outer-product fast-weight memory as a second-level cache (L2) fed by KV pairs evicted from the window. Recent tokens remain in exact local attention; evicted pairs are compressed into a per-layer matrix $A$ and read by future queries through a single matrix multiplication, exploiting the linear-attention identity $q_t(k_i \otimes v_i)=\langle q_t,k_i\rangle v_i$. A learned scalar gate fuses the L1 and L2 outputs, and per-head decay and write-rate parameters are trained end-to-end. The outer-product memory and the read identity are well-known; our contribution is their use as an L2 cache fed exclusively by sliding-window evictions, plus identifying that the common chunked-mean training shortcut $A\!\leftarrow\!λA\!+\!η(\bar k\!\otimes\!\bar v)$ silently introduces $C^2{-}C$ spurious cross-token outer products per chunk, and closing the gap with a parallel weighted-sum scan equivalent to per-token writes within float32 epsilon. Across systems scaling, controlled associative recall, long-context language modeling, and memory-capacity diagnostics, Tensor Cache improves the memory--quality frontier over bounded-state baselines.

</details>


### [122] [Pointwise Metrics Mislead: An Evaluation Protocol for Multimodal Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22891)
*Mads H. Baattrup,Jörn Bach,Laurids Jeppe,Finn Labe,Alexander Grohsjean,Christian Schwanenberger,Peer Stelldinger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，科学重建中常用的点对点评估指标（如RMSE、MAE）在后验分布多模态时存在结构性缺陷，因为最小化这些指标会导致估计的边际谱比真实情况更窄，从而压缩了下游科学测量依赖的关键谱特征。为此，作者提出一个三部分评估协议：通过CRPS评估事件级分布准确性，通过谱保真度诊断评估群体水平边际准确性，通过覆盖率校准评估不确定性可信度。在合成基准和粒子物理中的真实多对一反问题上，模型排名在点对点与分布指标间反转，校准进一步区分了在CRPS上表现相近的架构。评估协议本身决定了科学结论，而非模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的点对点评估指标（如RMSE、MAE）在处理具有多模态后验的逆问题时存在结构性缺陷，会系统性地低估真实分布的宽度，导致关键谱特征被压缩，影响科学结论的可靠性。

Method: 提出三部分评估协议：1）使用CRPS评估每事件的分布准确性；2）设计谱保真度诊断以衡量群体水平的边际分布匹配度；3）通过覆盖概率校准评估不确定性的可信度。

Result: 在合成数据和真实的粒子物理逆问题中，模型按点对点指标和分布指标排序结果相反，且校准能进一步区分在CRPS上表现相似的模型架构。表明评估协议的选择直接影响科学结论。

Conclusion: 评估协议而非模型本身决定科学结论。在多模态逆问题中，仅依赖点对点误差指标会引入不可忽视的偏差，必须采用分布式评估框架才能准确反映模型性能并支持可靠科学推断。

Abstract: Evaluation in scientific reconstruction is dominated by pointwise metrics - RMSE, MAE, per-event resolution - under the implicit assumption that lower error means better reconstruction. We show that this assumption fails structurally for inverse problems with multimodal posteriors. By the law of total variance, point estimators trained to minimize MSE or MAE produce a marginal spectrum strictly narrower than the truth whenever the posterior has nonzero width. The resulting bias is independent of architecture, training, and dataset size, and it compresses precisely the spectral features - tails, modes, shapes - that downstream scientific measurements rely on. We propose a three-part evaluation protocol where each step targets a failure mode the others miss: per-event distributional accuracy via CRPS, population-level marginal accuracy via a spectrum-fidelity diagnostic, and uncertainty trustworthiness via coverage-based calibration. On a synthetic benchmark with an analytic posterior and on a realistic many-to-one inverse problem from particle physics, model rankings reverse between pointwise and distributional metrics, and calibration further separates architectures indistinguishable under CRPS. The evaluation protocol, not the model, determines the scientific conclusion.

</details>


### [123] [From Residuals to Reasons: LLM-Guided Mechanism Inference from Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22897)
*Mohammad R. Rezaei,Rahul G. Krishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MARICL is a multi-agent framework that enhances machine learning models by using LLMs to identify and correct base-model errors through iterative, interpretable refinements. It improves predictions across diverse scientific domains and demonstrates real mechanistic generalization by transferring learned corrections across experimental batches with consistent biochemical validity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing models struggle to balance prediction accuracy and interpretability, particularly in scientific applications where understanding feature interactions and refining explanations iteratively is crucial. Current methods are largely inspective, failing to explain how features interact or adapt to human insights.

Method: MARICL uses LLM agents to analyze high-residual examples from a base model, hypothesize missing structural components, and generate explicit correction terms via multi-turn textual gradient optimization. The framework anchors predictions on a base model and asks the LLM to focus on what is missing rather than predicting from scratch.

Result: MARICL consistently improves prediction performance over base models across nine diverse benchmarks (scientific, biomedical, socioeconomic, synthetic). When applied to Cell-Free Protein data, frozen formulas derived from one batch generalize effectively to others under the same reagent protocol (92% success), but fail when protocols change—demonstrating true mechanistic, not statistical, generalization.

Conclusion: MARICL enables both accurate predictions and interpretable, mechanistically grounded model improvements. Its ability to transfer corrections across batches based on biochemical consistency confirms that the learned corrections reflect real underlying structure, not noise.

Abstract: A persistent challenge in machine learning for scientific applications is jointly achieving prediction and understanding. Statistical models excel on structured data but operate as black boxes, while existing interpretability methods are largely inspective: they answer "which features matter?" but do not articulate how features interact or refine explanations iteratively alongside human understanding. Asking an LLM to predict the target directly forces it to search the entire output space; we instead anchor predictions with a base model and ask the LLM the narrower question of what that model is missing. We introduce Multi-Agent Residual In-Context Learning (MARICL), an agentic framework in which LLM agents analyze where a base-model fails, hypothesize missing structure from high-residual examples provided in context, and produce explicit correction terms refined through multi-turn textual gradient optimization. Across nine benchmarks spanning scientific, biomedical, socioeconomic, and synthetic settings, MARICL improves consistently over its base model on all datasets. To test whether these corrections reflect real structure or batch-specific noise, we freeze formulas learned on one experimental batch of the Cell-Free Protein dataset and apply them (with no retraining and no further LLM calls) to held-out batches. Within the same reagent protocol, the frozen formulas improve predictions in over 92% of cases; across a different protocol, they fail systematically. The success boundary aligns with the biochemistry, not the batch count; direct evidence of mechanistic generalization.

</details>


### [124] [FIRMA: FIbonacci Ring Model Aggregation for Privacy-preserving Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22898)
*Rachid Hedjam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FIRMA系列协议，解决联邦学习中无服务器、隐私保护分类头、环形拓扑和非对称邻居加权的结构性三难问题。通过斐波那契加权、精度门控抑制、2-opt环排列等设计，在28种配置下显著优于现有方法，尤其在标签偏斜和狄利克雷异构场景下表现卓越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习协议无法同时实现无服务器操作、永久私密分类头、环形拓扑和合理非对称邻居加权；存在单点故障、梯度反演风险或隐私泄露等问题。

Method: 提出FIRMA家族：1）FibFL，基于斐波那契权重的环形聚合与私密分类头；2）FibFLP，引入精度门控抑制，动态降低收敛差的邻居权重；3）FibFLPP，结合2-opt环排列、$K_g = \lceil N/2 \rceil$次通信、余弦退火自保留校准，优化多样性与覆盖性。

Result: 在28个配置中，FibFLPP在所有标签偏斜场景下优于FedAvg，CIFAR-10上最高提升20.7个百分点；在狄利克雷异构下为无服务器协议中帕累托最优，17/28配置准确率最高。

Conclusion: FIRMA系列，特别是FibFLPP，首次实现无服务器、私密头、环形结构与非对称加权的统一，具备理论收敛保障与实证优越性能，是当前最先进且安全的联邦学习框架之一。

Abstract: Federated learning protocols face a structural trilemma: canonical server-based aggregation~\cite{mcmahan2017} creates a single point of failure and gradient inversion risk; decentralised ring-gossip alternatives~\cite{hu2019segmented} expose classification heads to semi-honest peers via uninformed uniform weights; and personalised methods~\cite{collins2021exploiting} reintroduce central aggregation. No existing protocol simultaneously achieves server-free operation, permanently private heads, ring topology, and principled asymmetric neighbour weighting. We propose FIRMA (\textbf{FI}bonacci \textbf{R}ing \textbf{M}odel \textbf{A}ggregation), a family of three progressively enhanced federated learning protocols: 1) \fibfl\ establishes the foundation: server-free ring aggregation with Fibonacci-weighted neighbour blending and permanently private classification heads. 2) \fibflp\ augments this with accuracy-gated neighbour suppression, selectively down-weighting poorly-converged peers while preserving the Fibonacci directional bias. 3) \fibflpp, the full system, completes the family with a 2-opt ring permutation that maximises adjacent-client class diversity, global ring coverage via $K_g{=}\lceil N/2\rceil$ gossip passes, and cosine-annealed self-retention calibration. We establish a convergence rate bound and three supporting propositions governing normalisation, coverage, retention, and diversity optimality. Systematic experiments across 28 configurations -- four benchmarks crossed with seven heterogeneity regimes -- demonstrate that \fibflpp\ surpasses \fedavg\ in all 12 label-skew configurations, with a peak advantage of $+20.7$\,pp on CIFAR-10 at $K{=}1$. Under Dirichlet heterogeneity, \fibflpp\ is the Pareto-dominant method among all server-free protocols, achieving the highest accuracy in 17 of 28 configurations.

### [126] [MARGIN: Runtime Confidence Calibration for Multi-Agent Foundation Model Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22949)
*Joss Armstrong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MARGIN 是一种在线校准方法，用于多智能体系统中根据智能体的置信度进行决策。它通过任务流自身学习每个智能体在不同置信度区间内的校准因子，无需模型访问、独立数据集或重新训练。该方法采用对称指数加权移动平均与贝叶斯收缩融合，具有鲁棒默认超参数。在19个基础模型、8个基准测试和5万+观测中，MARGIN 在分布偏移下校准误差比最佳离线校准基线低3-6倍。在多智能体选择中，原始置信度表现甚至低于随机（45-56%），而MARGIN将其提升至70-89%，并在三个基准上超越了始终最优模型的基准。六个形式化命题验证了收敛性、跟踪速度及对称更新的最优性，均经实证支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于自报告置信度的多智能体协调方法存在严重校准偏差，尤其在困难任务上置信度与准确性呈负相关。传统设计时校准方法（如温度缩放）因依赖固定校准且无法适应分布变化，难以解决此问题。因此亟需一种无需额外数据、可实时适应的在线校准机制。

Method: MARGIN 采用对称指数加权移动平均结合贝叶斯收缩，从任务流中动态学习每类智能体在不同置信度区间的校准因子。其核心为增量式更新策略，避免重训练，并通过滑动窗口捕捉置信度与真实准确率的关系。算法设计具备三组鲁棒默认超参数，适用于异构智能体环境。

Result: 在19个模型、8个基准、超过5万次观测中，MARGIN 在分布偏移下校准误差显著优于所有设计时基线（降低3-6倍）。多智能体选择任务中，原始置信度表现差于随机（45-56%），而MARGIN将配对分辨能力提升至70-89%，并超越‘始终最优模型’的上限，在四个基准中的三个实现这一突破。

Conclusion: MARGIN 提供了一种高效、无需外部数据或模型修改的在线校准方案，能有效纠正基础模型置信度的系统性偏差。其在动态环境中的稳定性与性能优势使其成为多智能体部署中可靠决策的关键工具，同时理论分析支持其收敛性与优化特性。

Abstract: Foundation model agents increasingly operate in multi-agent deployments where a coordinator must decide which agent's response to trust. The standard approach weights agents by their self-reported confidence, but recent evidence shows that foundation model confidence is systematically mis-calibrated and, on hard tasks, inversely correlated with accuracy. Design-time calibration methods (temperature scaling, Platt scaling, histogram binning) cannot address this problem because they fit a fixed correction to held-out data and degrade under distribution shift.
  We present MARGIN (Multi Agent Runtime Grading via Incremental Normalization), an online calibration method that learns per-agent, per-confidence-band calibration factors from the task stream itself, requiring no model access, no held-out data, and no retraining. MARGIN uses symmetric exponentially weighted moving averages with Bayesian shrinkage blending, and has three hyperparameters with robust defaults. Across 19 foundation models, 8 benchmarks, and over 50,000 observations, MARGIN achieves 3-6x lower calibration error than the best design-time baseline under distribution shift. In multi-agent selection, raw verbalized confidence produces pairwise resolution worse than random (45-56%) on hard benchmarks. MARGIN corrects this completely, raising pairwise resolution to 70-89% and surpassing the always-best-model oracle on three of four benchmarks. Six formal propositions characterize convergence, tracking speed, and the optimality of symmetric updates for non-strategic agents, with all predictions illustrated empirically.

### [128] [Learned Relay Representations for Forward-Thinking Discrete Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22967)
*Benjamin Rozonoyer,Jacopo Minniti,Dhruvesh Patel,Neil Band,Avishek Joey Bose,Tim G. J. Rudner,Andrew McCallum*

TL;DR: 提出Learned Relay Representations (Relay)方法，通过可微分的逐标记通道在去噪步骤间传递潜在信息，避免重复计算，提升扩散语言模型的推理效率与性能。该方法在Sudoku规划任务和Fast-dLLM v2上验证有效，显著降低延迟并优于监督微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Masked Diffusion Models在迭代去噪过程中会丢弃掩码位置的内部计算信息，导致每一步都需重新计算，造成资源浪费和延迟增加。需要一种机制来保留并传递这些有价值的信息以提高效率。

Method: 引入可微分的per-token通道（Relay），通过截断反向传播时间（BPTT）训练，使模型能够向前传递潜在表示，实现跨去噪步骤的信息共享。该方法兼容块扩散和KV缓存等技术。

Result: 在Sudoku任务中验证了设计合理性；在Fast-dLLM v2上，相比标准监督微调，在编码任务上表现更优，且推理延迟降低最高达32%。证明了该方法能有效提升性能-延迟权衡。

Abstract: When Masked Diffusion Models (MDMs) generate sequences through iterative refinement, the rich internal computation over masked positions is discarded, forcing every subsequent refinement step to recompute the valuable internal information stored as model representations. To avoid a hard reset between denoising rounds, we propose Learned Relay Representations (Relay), a method that allows MDMs to be forward-thinking when denoising by explicitly learning how to propagate latent information for the benefit of future denoising steps. Relay introduces a differentiable per-token channel that passes information between forward passes and is trained via truncated backpropagation through time (BPTT). We show that this framework can be scaled to state-of-the-art Diffusion Language Models (DLMs), and is seamlessly compatible with techniques like block diffusion and KV caching. We first provide a thorough justification of the design choices in Relay on a challenging Sudoku-based planning task. We then scale Relay to Fast-dLLM v2, a state-of-the-art DLM, outperforming standard supervised finetuning on coding tasks while reducing inference latency by up to 32%. Our empirical results demonstrate that state-of-the-art DLMs can be explicitly trained to relay latent information forward across decoding steps, advancing the performance-latency Pareto frontier. We provide code for all our experiments.

Abstract: Humans, animals, and modern machine learning models exhibit impressive abilities to learn complex behaviors and generalize these behaviors to unseen situations.
