How do learning systems balance between learning general regularities and memorizing exceptions? We argue that a lack of task paradigms has hindered the study of this essential ability. To address this gap, we introduce a novel task, transitive inference with exceptions, that tests for relational generalization and memorization of an exception to the relational rule. We then analytically characterize the behavior of a simple, theoretically tractable model of neural network learning (kernel ridge regression) across a broad family of representations and task parameters. We find that these models can balance between relational generalization and memorization, but unlike for transitive inference without an exception, successful generalization is sensitive to the specific representational geometry. We explain why this task is more challenging mechanistically by drawing on our analytical theory. Finally, we validate our theoretical insights in pretrained language models that are finetuned on ordered relations, finding that these models successfully generalize according to the transitive rule, but also make the kinds of systematic mistakes predicted by our theory. Overall, our theory shows how learning systems can balance between relational generalization and memorization, explains how this can go wrong, and emphasizes the need for new task paradigms designed to probe this ability.

### [131] [Test-Time Training Undermines Safety Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22984)
*Simone Antonelli,Sadegh Akhondzadeh,Aleksandar Bojchevski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Test-Time Training (TTT) allows models to adapt during inference, improving performance but introducing new vulnerabilities. This paper identifies three threat models where attackers exploit TTT to bypass safety filters, significantly increasing Attack Success Rate (ASR) and ASR@10—up to 95% and 93% under LoRA. TTT-induced overfitting leads to degenerate outputs that skew evaluation results; the authors propose a validity-aware evaluation to address this. A lightweight detector based on perplexity shift is introduced, but robust defense requires dynamic alignment.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TTT enhances model performance in tasks like few-shot learning and reasoning but introduces new security risks by enabling adversarial manipulation during inference. Existing safety mechanisms may be bypassed due to dynamic parameter updates, necessitating an investigation into attack vectors and defenses.

Method: The study analyzes three threat models for TTT: few-shot adaptation, generation-phase adaptation, and production fine-tuning API exploitation. Experiments evaluate ASR and ASR@10 across multiple model families and scales using LoRA. Degenerate outputs caused by overfitting are identified and corrected via validity-aware evaluation. A provider-side detector using perplexity shift on a private harmful holdout is proposed.

Result: TTT increases ASR significantly—average ASR@10 reaches 95% (few-shot) and 93% (generation-phase). Vulnerabilities transfer to production APIs. Overfitting causes degenerate outputs that inflate ASR under standard judges. Validity-aware evaluation mitigates this bias. The proposed detector flags TTT requests effectively, though long-term defense requires dynamic alignment.

Conclusion: TTT creates a new attack surface that strengthens jailbreak attacks and undermines current safety guardrails. While a lightweight detector offers initial protection, robust defense demands dynamic alignment mechanisms to ensure safe and reliable model behavior during inference.

Abstract: Test-Time Training (TTT) is an emerging paradigm that enables models to adapt their parameters during inference, improving performance on tasks such as few-shot learning, retrieval-augmented generation, and complex reasoning. However, this dynamic adaptation introduces new vulnerabilities that adversaries can exploit to jailbreak models. We identify three threat models for TTT and demonstrate how attackers can leverage them to bypass safety filters. Our results show that TTT can significantly increase the Attack Success Rate (ASR) and the ASR over 10 generation trials (ASR@10). For example, under LoRA, the few-shot and generation-phase threat models achieve an average ASR@10 of 95% and 93% respectively, across models from different families and scales. These vulnerabilities transfer to production fine-tuning APIs. We also show that TTT-induced overfitting can produce degenerate outputs that inflate ASR under standard judges, and propose a validity-aware evaluation to correct for this. Our findings suggest that TTT exposes a new attack surface, strengthens attacks, and undermines existing safety guardrails. As a first step toward defense, we propose a lightweight provider-side detector that flags TTT requests via the perplexity shift on a private harmful holdout, but robust deployment will ultimately require dynamic alignment.

### [132] [Smoothed Elicitation Complexity for Approximate $Γ$-calibration of Discrete Classification Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23017)
*Jessica Finocchiaro,Victor Ganson,Drona Khurana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了多分类模型校准问题，提出通过性质（property）的近似校准来降低计算复杂度。针对离散性质（如众数、排序）难以进行近似校准的问题，作者引入连续的Lipschitz性质作为中介，首次实现了对强有序离散性质的近似校准，并构建了相应的算法，证明其可后处理还原原始离散性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多分类场景下因预测空间随类别数指数增长而面临计算复杂度爆炸问题；同时，已有近似校准理论主要限于连续标量性质，无法有效处理常见的离散性质（如模式、排名），因此亟需一种适用于离散性质的近似校准框架。

Method: 通过引入Lipschitz连续性质作为中介，构建可后处理还原原始离散性质的算法，利用强有序性特征对离散性质进行近似校准，并分析其Lipschitz可诱导复杂度。

Result: 首次实现对强有序离散性质的近似校准，证明了相关算法的有效性与可还原性，并给出了其在性质维度而非类别数上的低复杂度特性。

Conclusion: 该工作为离散性质的近似校准提供了理论基础和算法支持，显著降低了多分类模型校准的复杂度，拓展了校准理论的应用范围。

Abstract: One prominent method of evaluating machine learning model trustworthiness is the notion of calibration. In the binary outcome setting, a probabilistic predictor is calibrated if outcomes are realized according to a model's distributional prediction, conditioned on this prediction. Straightforward extensions of binary calibration definitions to probabilistic multiclass classifiers suffer from an exponential complexity blowup as the space of predictions grows exponentially in the number of classes $n$. As a remedy, Noarov and Roth (2023) propose multiclass calibration with predictions that are properties of the outcome distribution, reducing complexity from growing in the number of classes $n$ to the dimension $d$ of the property, called its elicitation complexity. Previous work on approximate property calibration is generally limited to continuous scalar properties, despite many relevant properties of interest being discrete, like the mode or rankings. We characterize the approximate property calibration of discrete properties which are strongly orderable by using Lipschitz continuous properties as an intermediary. This work is the first to our knowledge to provide approximate calibration results for discrete properties. Along the way, we characterize the Lipschitz elicitation complexity of strongly orderable discrete properties by constructing algorithms for designing these Lipschitz properties, which we prove can be post-processed to obtain the original discrete property.

Method: 提出基于变压器的生成式世界模型 World Machine，引入潜状态机制以降低计算复杂度，使模型能够根据输入数据量动态调整表示能力。采用端到端训练策略，结合多任务学习与自监督目标，增强模型对环境动态的预测能力和泛化性能。

Conclusion: World Machine 作为一种新型生成式世界模型架构，成功实现了对时序环境的高效建模与可控模拟，在保持结构化和通用性的同时，突破了传统变压器在上下文长度上的局限，为未来智能体的自主决策与环境理解提供了新范式。

Abstract: World models represent a paradigm shift in generative AI, pursuing predictive understanding and controllable simulation of environments in a structured and generalizable way. We present World Machine, a generative world-modeling architecture for time series. It is a transformer-based architecture with latent states that enables adaptation to different amounts of observed data and contexts. This shows an improvement over traditional transformers, which have a computational and memory cost that scales quadratically with the context. Experiments on a proposed synthetic dataset, Toy1D, validate the approach's feasibility, demonstrate capabilities not found in conventional transformers, and highlight the contributions of each component of the training protocol.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据扩展方法可能导致负迁移，即性能下降；因此需要一种有效的方法来预测跨域迁移的可行性，以避免无效的数据引入。

Method: RADAR 通过测量层间表示的角对齐、相对距离变化以及同域与跨域动态分布之间的差异，构建一个几何驱动的迁移能力评估指标。

Abstract: Machine learning methods rely on data. However, gathering suitable data can be challenging due to availability constraints, cost, or the need for domain expertise. Expanding datasets with additional sources is a common response to limited data, yet this practice does not always improve downstream performance and can sometimes lead to a loss of performance, known as negative transfer. We propose RADAR, a simple, geometrically grounded metric for estimating cross-domain transferability in foundation models. RADAR analyzes the layer-wise evolution of representations by measuring angular alignments and relative changes in distance along layer-to-layer displacement trajectories, and by comparing empirical distributions of within-domain and cross-domain dynamics. We hypothesize that domain transferability is related to the divergence between these trajectory distributions. We evaluate the metric across multiple modalities, including cross-lingual sentiment classification with text embedding models and cross-domain image classification with foundation vision models. Across several settings, RADAR provides competitive predictive performance relative to existing transferability metrics on several vision and text benchmarks, with particularly strong results when domain transitions are smooth or cleanly separated. Our ablations further suggest that the effectiveness of transferability estimation depends on the geometry of the model's internal representation space, with different modalities favoring different topological formulations.

Abstract: Latent steering exploits internal representations of Large Language Models (LLMs) to guide generation, yet interventions on dense states can entangle distinct semantic features. In this paper, we investigate attention query activations as a high-fidelity site for precise control, hypothesizing that manipulating the attention mechanism itself offers sharper steerability than general state interventions. We introduce Prototype-Based Sparse Steering, a framework that applies Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) specifically to query activations, to decompose them into interpretable features, then apply gradient-based optimization during inference to align the sparse representation with class prototypes of target behaviors. ### [136] [Decomposing and Measuring Evaluation Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23055)
*Changling Li,Terry Jingchen Zhang,Jie Zhang,Zhijing Jin,Sahar Abdelnabi,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了前沿语言模型在评估过程中识别自身被测试并调整行为的问题，提出从社会心理学角度分解评估意识为环境与模型两部分，并定义了八类触发因素。通过链式思维监控发现，识别率取决于模型与基准的特定组合，且识别不常导致行为改变，方向取决于评估类型。模型对安全评估更敏感，威胁其有效性。为此提出EvalAwareBench，一个可独立调控八类因素的100对任务基准，用于系统研究影响因素。结果表明，无单一因素普遍影响所有模型，但叠加因素可逐步提升评估意识。研究提供了测量、归因和缓解评估意识的工具，建议在识别下保持行为一致性作为未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型在评估中可能识别自身被测试并调整行为，影响基准测试的有效性。然而，领域内缺乏统一基础，混淆了评估属性与模型属性，以及检测与行为响应之间的区别。需要建立清晰的理论框架以准确理解并应对这一现象。

Method: 基于社会心理学构建评估意识的双组件模型（环境与模型），定义八类触发因素（如占位符实体、评分格式等）；采用链式思维监控分析模型识别与行为反应；设计并使用EvalAwareBench基准，实现对八个因素的独立控制，进行多模型、多基准实验。

Result: 识别率依赖于模型与基准的具体配对，而非单独因素；识别通常不引发行为改变，若发生，方向取决于评估类型；模型对安全评估更敏感，安全基准有效性风险更高；单个触发因素不影响所有模型，但组合效应可显著提升评估意识。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了评估意识的可操作框架，提出了EvalAwareBench作为可控实验平台，揭示了触发因素的交互作用。建议将行为一致性作为应对评估意识的关键路径，为提升基准测试可靠性提供方法支持。

Abstract: Frontier language models sometimes recognize that they are being evaluated and adjust their behavior, undermining validity of benchmark results. Yet the field studies it without a shared foundation, conflating properties of the evaluation with properties of the model, and detection with behavioral response. We ground evaluation awareness in social psychology, decomposing it into an environment component (how recognizable the task is) and a model component that separates recognition from propensity to act on it. We operationalize the environment component through eight categorized trigger factors, such as placeholder entities and grading-style output formats, and study recognition and behavior through chain-of-thought monitoring. Across nine frontier models and four benchmarks, recognition rates depend on the specific pairing of model and benchmark rather than on either in isolation. Recognition rarely leads to behavioral change, and when it does, the direction depends on the type of evaluation perceived. Models are also more sensitive to safety than capability evaluations, placing safety benchmark validity at greater risk. To study which factors each model is sensitive to and how they interact, we propose \textbf{EvalAwareBench}, a factor-controlled benchmark of 100 paired safety-capability tasks where each of the eight factors can be independently toggled, varying evaluative signals while holding the underlying request fixed. Through EvalAwareBench, we find that no single factor uniformly affects all models, but stacking factors progressively raises evaluation awareness across all of them. Our framework and EvalAwareBench provide the tools to measure, attribute, and mitigate evaluation awareness, pointing to behavioral consistency under recognition as a promising path forward.

### [137] [ModeSwitch-LLM: A Lightweight Phase-Aware Controller for Cross-Mode LLM Inference on a Single GPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23057)
*Aman Sunesh,Ali Alshehhi,Hivansh Dhakne*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ModeSwitch-LLM 是一种轻量级的请求边界控制器，通过为每个请求选择合适的固定推理模式来提升单GPU大语言模型的推理效率。它利用低成本的工作负载级特征，在FP16、量化模式、推测解码及混合模式（如GPTQ+前缀缓存、INT8+连续批处理）之间动态路由请求。在NVIDIA A100 GPU上部署Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct时，该系统在合成工作负载下实现2.10倍的平均延迟加速和0.48倍的平均能耗比，即每token能耗降低51.7%；在自动基准测试中，精度与FP16接近，平均偏差仅为+0.17个百分点。尽管尝试了轻量级学习型路由，但其性能未显著优于基于规则的控制器，因引入额外的路由开销且更常选择违反质量、能耗或内存约束的模式。结果表明，无需重新训练模型或修改架构，仅通过简单的请求感知路由即可显著提升现有推理模式的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型推理系统通常采用单一静态配置，难以适应多样化请求的性能与资源需求。为提升单GPU环境下推理效率，亟需一种轻量级、自适应的请求级调度机制，以动态选择最优推理模式，同时兼顾精度、能耗与内存约束。

Method: 提出ModeSwitch-LLM，基于低成本的工作负载特征（如请求长度、历史响应时间等），在多种固定推理模式间进行实时路由决策。采用规则驱动的控制器，避免引入复杂的学习模型带来的额外开销，并确保所选模式满足质量、能量和内存限制。

Result: 在合成工作负载下，相比FP16，ModeSwitch-LLM实现2.10倍平均延迟加速和0.48倍平均能耗比，即每token能耗降低51.7%；在自动基准测试中，精度与FP16几乎一致，平均误差仅+0.17个百分点。学习型路由器虽被探索，但因增加路由开销且频繁选择不合规模式，表现不如规则控制器。

Conclusion: 简单、基于规则的请求感知路由可有效利用现有推理模式，显著提升单GPU大模型推理效率，无需模型重训练或架构变更，具备良好的实用性和部署潜力。

Abstract: ModeSwitch-LLM is a lightweight request-boundary controller for improving single-GPU large language model inference efficiency by routing each request to an appropriate fixed inference mode. Instead of relying on one static serving configuration, the system selects among FP16, quantized modes, speculative decoding, and hybrid modes such as GPTQ plus prefix caching and INT8 plus continuous batching using cheap workload-level features. We evaluate ModeSwitch-LLM on Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct served on a single NVIDIA A100 GPU. On deployment-style synthetic workloads, the online controller achieves a 2.10x mean latency speedup over FP16 and a 0.48x mean energy ratio, corresponding to 51.7% lower energy per token. On automatic benchmarks used as a quality gate, accuracy remains close to FP16 with a mean delta of +0.17 percentage points. We also evaluate lightweight learned routers, but find that they do not clearly outperform the rule-based controller because they add routing overhead and more often select modes that violate quality, energy, or memory constraints. These results show that simple request-aware routing can recover substantial efficiency from existing inference modes without retraining the model or changing its architecture.

### [138] [GEMQ: Global Expert-Level Mixed-Precision Quantization for MoE LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23078)
*Jianing Deng,Song Wang,Dongwei Wang,Zijie Liu,Tianlong Chen,Huanrui Yang,Jingtong Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GEMQ提出了一种全局专家级混合精度量化方法，通过全局线性规划建模和高效路由器微调，解决了现有方法因依赖层级重要性估计和忽略量化引起的路由变化而导致的次优分配问题。该方法在保持高精度的同时显著降低内存占用并加速推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合精度量化方法依赖于层级重要性估计，忽略了量化带来的路由器偏移，导致专家比特位分配不优，进而影响模型性能和效率。

Method: 提出全局线性规划公式以基于量化误差分析捕捉全模型范围内的专家重要性，并引入高效的路由器微调机制以适应量化后的专家；结合渐进式量化框架，迭代优化重要性估计与比特位分配。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts Large Language Models (MoE-LLMs) achieve strong performance but incur substantial memory overhead due to massive expert parameters. Mixed-precision quantization mitigates this cost by allocating expert-wise bit-widths based on their importance, approaching the accuracy-memory Pareto frontier and enabling extreme low-bit quantization. However, existing methods rely on layer-wise importance estimation and overlook router shifts induced by quantization, resulting in suboptimal allocation and routing. In this work, we propose Global Expert-level Mixed-precision Quantization (GEMQ) to overcome these limitations via (1) a global linear-programming formulation that captures model-wide expert importance based on quantization error analysis, and (2) efficient router fine-tuning to adapt routing to quantized experts. These components are integrated into a progressive quantization framework that iteratively refines importance estimation and allocation. Experiments demonstrate that GEMQ significantly reduces memory and accelerates inference with minimal accuracy degradation. Source code is available at https://github.com/jndeng/GEMQ .

### [139] [The Attribution Contract: Feature Attribution for Generative Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23080)
*Giang Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出‘归因契约’（Attribution Contract）概念，以解决生成式语言模型中特征归因的模糊性问题。该契约明确了被解释的输出、可归因的特征、假设的生成过程、固定变量及所解释的模型得分，从而澄清不同归因方法在不同设定下的差异。作者指出，许多关于生成模型归因的争议实为对解释契约理解不一致所致，而非算法本身的问题，并通过自回归与扩散语言模型案例说明何时归因于早期生成词元、中间状态或去噪阶段是有效或误导性的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式语言模型中的特征归因存在概念模糊性：早期生成的词元既是输出也是后续输入；扩散模型通过迭代去噪生成文本，使得局部解释可能针对扩散状态而非下一个词元。这种模糊性导致归因结果难以解释，且现有方法缺乏统一标准。因此需要一种规范化的框架来明确归因的前提条件和目标。

Method: 提出‘归因契约’，作为特征归因声明的正式规范，包含五个要素：被解释的输出、可归因的特征、生成过程假设、固定变量以及模型得分类型。通过此契约，将归因方法与其应用上下文绑定，形成‘方法-契约’对，以区分不同情境下的归因意义。

Result: 研究表明，在自回归模型中，对早期生成词元的归因可能具有误导性，除非明确其在特定契约下的解释角色；在扩散模型中，对中间去噪阶段的归因仅在特定契约下有意义。实验表明，同一归因方法在不同契约下可得出截然不同的结论，验证了契约的重要性。

Conclusion: 特征归因在生成式语言模型中不应脱离具体契约独立评价。归因方法的有效性取决于其与契约的匹配程度。未来研究应将归因方法与其对应的解释契约一同评估，避免因前提不明确引发误解或争议。

Abstract: Feature attribution methods promise to identify which input features matter for a model output. In generative language models, however, it is often unclear what should count as a feature in the first place. In autoregressive language models, earlier generated tokens are both outputs of the model and inputs to later predictions. In diffusion language models, generation proceeds through iterative denoising or unmasking rather than fixed left-to-right prediction, so local explanation may target a state of diffusion rather than a next token. We argue that this ambiguity is not merely an implementation detail, but a conceptual limitation of carrying classifier-era feature attribution directly into generative language modeling. We introduce the Attribution Contract, a specification for feature-attribution claims that names what output is being explained, which features are eligible to receive attribution, what generative process is assumed, what is held fixed, and what model score is being attributed. The contract clarifies why the same attribution method can answer different questions depending on how it is instantiated. We argue that many disagreements about feature attribution in generative language models are not disagreements about attribution algorithms, but about unstated explanatory contracts. Using autoregressive and diffusion language models as case studies, we show when attribution to earlier generated tokens, intermediate states, or denoising stages is informative, when it is misleading, and why feature-attribution methods in generative language models should be evaluated as method-contract pairs.

</details>


### [140] [ThriftAttention: Selective Mixed Precision for Long-Context FP4 Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23081)
*Joe Sharratt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ThriftAttention提出一种低比特注意力机制，在保持FP4推理效率的同时，接近FP16的长上下文性能。通过选择少数关键查询-键块以FP16精度计算，其余用FP4，结合在线softmax融合输出，仅需5%的块使用FP16即可恢复89.1%的性能差距，且优势随序列长度增加而提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有4比特量化技术在长上下文场景中导致显著质量下降，因量化误差分布不均，重要交互处误差更大。需要一种方法在低精度下保留关键信息，同时保持高效推理。

Method: ThriftAttention分两阶段：首先通过启发式快速筛选出少数重要查询-键块；其次对这些块采用FP16计算，其余块用FP4计算，最后通过在线softmax合并输出。

Result: 在多个长上下文基准和模型家族上，仅5%的块以FP16计算时，平均恢复89.1%的FP4到FP16性能差距；随着序列长度增加，性能优势更明显，有效缓解了长上下文下的系统性质量下降问题。

Conclusion: ThriftAttention实现了低比特推理效率与高精度长上下文质量的平衡，为高效长序列建模提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Efficient attention algorithms are critical to mitigate the quadratic cost of attention in long-context workloads. Prior work utilises block-scaled quantisation techniques on Blackwell GPUs to move attention computation to 4-bit precision to accelerate inference. However, these techniques result in significant quality degradation in long-context settings. We show that the output impact of quantisation error is highly non-uniform and increases with the importance of each query-key interaction, concentrating functionally relevant error in a small number of attention blocks that contain the most important tokens. We propose ThriftAttention, a low-bit attention variant that delivers near-FP16 long-context quality at FP4 inference efficiency. This approach proceeds in two stages. First, a heuristic rapidly selects a small number of important query-key block pairs for FP16 precision. Second, the selected blocks are computed in FP16 and the remaining blocks in FP4, with both paths merged via online softmax into a single output. We demonstrate across long-context benchmarks and model families that by computing only 5% of query-key blocks in FP16, ThriftAttention recovers on average 89.1% of the FP4-to-FP16 performance gap. We show ThriftAttention's advantage grows with sequence length, mitigating the systematic FP4 quality degradation observed at longer contexts. The code is available at https://github.com/joesharratt1229/ThriftAttention.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 GPLD（Gradient-Penalized Latent Dynamics），通过在后验潜在分布上施加行级雅可比惩罚，鼓励局部平滑的过渡学习；该惩罚被解释为离散嵌入状态马尔可夫决策过程中的有限差分平滑的连续潜空间类比，并采用 Hutchinson 风格的随机探测进行高效估计。

Result: 在 DeepMind Control 的本体感觉任务中，GPLD 显著提升了整体样本效率，尤其在高复杂度的四足运动任务中表现突出：能更早实现高回报行为，且在长时序学习中表现出更强的一致性。

Conclusion: 显式引入局部平滑性正则化是一种简单而有效的改进方式，可显著提升潜在世界模型在平滑连续控制环境中的表现。代码已开源。

Abstract: Model-based reinforcement learning improves sample efficiency by learning a world model. However, existing latent world models such as DreamerV3 do not explicitly enforce local smoothness in their learned transition dynamics, leaving a useful inductive bias for transition dynamics learning unexploited. We propose GPLD, a gradient-penalized latent dynamics regularizer for DreamerV3 that applies a row-wise Jacobian penalty to the posterior latent distribution to encourage locally smooth transition learning. We show that this penalty can be interpreted as the continuous-latent analog of finite-difference smoothing of transition laws in discrete embedded-state MDPs, and estimate it efficiently using Hutchinson-style stochastic probes. Empirically, across DeepMind Control proprioceptive tasks, GPLD improves aggregate sample efficiency, with particularly strong gains on higher-complexity locomotion environments. On more challenging quadruped tasks, GPLD reaches high-return behavior earlier and exhibits more consistent late-stage learning over longer horizons. Explicit local smoothness regularization is a simple and effective way to improve latent world models for smooth continuous control environments. Code for GPLD is available at github.com/romils9/gpld-mbrl .

Gen-ROTDA achieves the lowest MAE on the main 2025 to 2026 task and is the best OT-family method on average across multi-year tasks, although fine-tuning and MMD adaptation remain strong overall baselines. But once Gaussian noise is added for privacy, this monotonicity can fail, and the usual analysis no longer goes through. The key reason is that determinant growth controls volume, while regret analysis needs control of the worst direction. ### [144] [CALAD: Channel-Aware contrastive Learning for multivariate time series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23139)
*Jaehyeop Hong,Youngbum Hur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CALAD提出了一种面向多变量时间序列异常检测的通道感知对比学习框架，通过估计通道相关性来构建对比样本，使学习过程更关注异常语义而非通用相似性。该方法利用Transformer自编码器的重构误差估计通道重要性，并设计了基于通道的增强策略，使模型对无关通道变化具有不变性，同时对相关通道的变化敏感。此外，结合对比学习与辅助重构头，提升了特征判别能力并保留正常结构。在多个真实数据集上的实验表明，CALAD在分布偏移场景下显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常平等对待所有通道，导致异常相关信号被稀释；需要一种能够识别关键通道、提升异常检测性能的方法，尤其是在标签稀缺和分布偏移的情况下。

Method: 使用Transformer自编码器计算重构误差以估计通道相关性；基于此设计通道感知的正负样本构造策略（通过保留或扰动异常相关通道）；结合对比学习与辅助重构头进行联合训练，实现对异常敏感且对正常模式保持鲁棒的表示学习。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集上，CALAD均优于现有方法，尤其在分布偏移条件下表现突出，证明了其鲁棒性和有效性。

Conclusion: CALAD通过引入通道感知机制和针对性的数据增强策略，有效提升了多变量时间序列异常检测的性能，特别是在缺乏标注数据和分布变化的场景中具有显著优势。

Abstract: Multivariate time series anomaly detection has become increasingly important in real-world applications, where labeled data are often scarce. Many existing approaches rely on unsupervised learning to model normal patterns, but they often treat all channels equally. This design can dilute anomaly-relevant signals, since not all channels contribute equally to anomaly detection. In this paper, we propose CALAD, a channel-aware contrastive learning framework for multivariate time series anomaly detection. CALAD governs the construction of contrastive samples using estimated channel relevance, allowing the learning process to reflect anomaly semantics rather than generic similarity. Channel relevance is estimated from reconstruction errors of a transformer-based autoencoder and is used to distinguish channels that are more influential to anomalous behaviors. Using this information, we design a channel-wise augmentation strategy in which positive and negative samples are constructed based on whether anomaly-relevant channels are preserved or perturbed. This encourages invariance to changes in irrelevant channels while being sensitive to changes in anomaly-relevant channels. Furthermore, CALAD combines contrastive learning and an auxiliary reconstruction head, allowing the model to learn discriminative representations while retaining normal structures. Experiments on multiple real-world datasets shows that CALAD consistently outperforms existing methods, particularly under distribution shift scenarios. We provide the code for reproducibility at https://github.com/hirundo1218/CALAD

### [146] [Pure Exploration for a Good Policy in Reinforcement Learning with Bandit Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23182)
*Zitian Li,Wang Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了强化学习中的纯探索问题，提出了一种新的目标——好策略识别（GPI），即在给定奖励阈值μ₀的情况下，识别出期望奖励不低于μ₀的策略（若存在），否则声明不存在。与传统最佳策略识别（BPI）不同，GPI更符合实际应用中“足够好即可”的需求。作者提出了新算法BEE-GPI，并在固定置信度设置下分析其样本复杂度，理论证明其在正例情况下的上界系数为O(H²/(V*−μ₀)²)，不依赖状态和动作空间大小，显著优于BPI。同时给出了下界证明，表明该形式的依赖关系是必要的。实验验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际应用中，往往只需要一个‘足够好’的策略而非最优策略，因此传统的最佳策略识别（BPI）过于严格。本文旨在提出一种更贴近现实需求的策略识别目标——好策略识别（GPI），以降低对样本的需求并提升实用性。

Method: 提出新目标GPI（Good Policy Identification），设计新算法BEE-GPI，在固定置信度框架下最小化样本复杂度；通过理论推导建立正负实例的上界，并结合下界分析证明其近似最优性。

Result: BEE-GPI在正例情形下的样本复杂度上界具有良好的依赖结构：系数为O(H²/(V*−μ₀)²)，且不随状态/动作空间增长而恶化；下界证明该形式不可改进；数值实验验证了算法效率。

Conclusion: GPI是一个更实用的纯探索目标，所提出的BEE-GPI算法在理论上具有近最优的样本复杂度，且在实践中表现出高效性，为现实场景下的策略搜索提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Pure exploration in episodic Reinforcement Learning has primarily focused on Best Policy Identification (BPI), which seeks to identify a (near)-optimal policy with high confidence. Motivated by practical settings where a ``good enough'' policy suffices, we study an alternate objective of Good Policy Identification (GPI). For a given reward threshold $μ_0$, GPI only requires identifying a policy with expected reward in an episode at least $μ_0$ if such a policy exists (positive instance), or declaring None if no such policy exists (negative instance). We formalize GPI under the fixed-confidence setting. We require the output to be correct with probability $\geq 1-δ$, and seek to minimize the expected sample complexity, which is the expected number of episodes explored for the output. We propose a novel algorithm BEE-GPI, and derive theoretically-grounded upper bounds on its sample complexity for positive and negative instances. Notably, for positive instances, the coefficient of $\log 1/δ$ in our upper bound is $O(H^2/(V^* - μ_0)^2)$, where $H$ is the episode length and $V^*$ is the optimal expected reward in an episode. The coefficient does not depend on the action and state space sizes otherwise, in sharp contrast to the sample complexity in BPI. We further establish lower bound results to show the near-optimality of BEE-GPI and the necessity of the $1/(V^* -μ)^2$ term. Numerical experiments further validate the efficiency of our approach.

### [147] [Empirical Bayes Conformal Prediction for Vision and Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23189)
*Jiapeng Zeng,Yogesh Prabhu,Zhanpeng Zeng,Michael A. Newton,Vikas Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于r-value的贝叶斯共形预测框架，通过整合得分的变异性来改进传统共形预测中仅依赖单一非一致性得分的问题。该方法利用变异性信息区分稳定信号与噪声，从而提升预测结果的稳定性与可靠性。在图像分类、CLIP-based VLM和大语言模型等多个任务上，r-value方法在保持目标覆盖度的同时，显著减少了高方差虚假候选的纳入，并缩小了预测集合大小，尤其在变异性具有信息量时表现更优，而在变异性较小时则退化为标准共形预测行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统共形预测（CP）依赖单一非一致性得分，容易受不稳定样本或随机波动影响，导致高方差的虚假候选被错误包含。尽管平均-校准方法可平滑多个实现，但仍丢失了关于得分一致性的关键信息。因此需要一种能够利用得分变异性来增强判断能力的方法，以识别真正稳定的预测结果。

Method: 提出基于r-value的实证贝叶斯共形预测框架，将非一致性得分的变异性转化为不确定性感知的非一致性度量。r-value估计一个候选在其潜在得分中属于最高排名组的概率，考虑其均值与不确定性。提供闭式正态-正态估计器和非参数后验采样估计器两种实现方式。

Result: 实验表明，在图像分类、CLIP-based VLM和大语言模型任务中，r-value共形预测在保持目标覆盖度的前提下，显著提升了排名稳定性，减少了预测集合大小；当变异性具有信息时性能优越，变异性消失时自动退化为标准共形预测行为。

Conclusion: r-value共形预测通过建模得分变异性，有效提升了共形预测的鲁棒性与准确性，是一种兼具理论保障与实际优势的改进方法。

Abstract: Conformal prediction (CP) gives distribution-free coverage for modern vision and language models, but it is often forced to make a ranking decision from a single unstable nonconformity score. Standard CP uses one realization, while average-then-calibrate variants smooth multiple realizations into a point estimate. Both options discard the inconsistency that can help identify whether a candidate is indeed stable. A weak answer can enter the conformal set even if the evidence is not strong, simply because one posterior sample or prompt phrasing made it look strong. But variability can help distinguish a stable signal from noise-driven fluctuations. We describe an empirical Bayes conformal prediction framework that uses $r$-values to convert score variability into an uncertainty informed nonconformity score. The resulting $r$-value estimates how likely a candidate's latent score belongs to the top-ranked group after accounting for both its mean score and its uncertainty. It admits both a closed-form Normal-Normal empirical Bayes estimator and a nonparametric posterior-sampling estimator. Using the $r$-value as the nonconformity score preserves the target conformal coverage while provably reducing the inclusion of high variance false candidates under mild regularity conditions. Across image classification, CLIP-based VLM benchmarks, and LLMs, we show that $r$-value conformal prediction preserves target coverage while improving ranking stability and reducing set size when variability is informative, and reverting to CP-like behavior when variability vanishes.

### [150] [WMAttack: Automated Attack Search for Adversarial Evaluation of World-Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23220)
*Zhixiang Guo,Siyuan Liang,Shi Fu,Cheng Guo,Andras Balogh,Mark Jelasity,Dacheng Tao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing methods for evaluating adversarial robustness in world models lack automation and efficiency; manual attacks are unreliable, while exhaustive searches are too costly due to the need for closed-loop rollouts.

Method: WMAttack formulates robustness evaluation as a finite-budget search over attack configurations. SCAS refines attack proposals using feedback from reward degradation, action instability, runtime cost, and rollout variability. RGAR retrieves effective past configurations from similar tasks to initialize new searches.

Abstract: Despite the growing use of world models as decision-making agents, their adversarial robustness remains underexplored due to the lack of dedicated automated evaluation methods. A key obstacle is that attack evaluation must be both accurate and efficient: weak manually tuned attacks can overestimate robustness, while exhaustive hyperparameter search is prohibitively expensive because each candidate requires closed-loop rollouts through learned latent dynamics. We introduce WMAttack, an automated attack-search framework for adversarial evaluation of world-model agents. WMAttack formulates robustness evaluation as a finite-budget search over attack configurations, including attack families, perturbation budgets, optimization steps, restarts, and allocation rules. To improve search accuracy, Self-Correcting Attack Search (SCAS) refines the attack proposal distribution using feedback from reward degradation, action instability, runtime cost, and rollout variability. To improve search efficiency, Representation-Guided Attack Retrieval (RGAR) retrieves effective historical configurations from representation-similar tasks, providing a warm start for unseen environments. We provide a theoretical explanation showing that proposal refinement improves finite-budget search when it shifts probability mass toward high-utility attacks. Across Atari and DeepMind Control tasks, WMAttack consistently discovers stronger attacks than the evaluated baselines, improving normalized reward drop from 0.497 to 1.034 on DreamerV3 Atari and from 0.319 to 0.682 on DMC. Existing methods are often dominated by binary eviction or representation approximation, which may underutilize tokens that are not critical for exact retention but are still reconstructable. We present VECTOR, a plug-and-play augmentation for eviction-based pipelines that introduces three-way token routing: retention, approximation, and eviction. VECTOR combines an importance signal from the base scorer with a reconstructability signal from an offline-calibrated regression-based value estimation. By leveraging reconstructability, VECTOR recovers useful value information that would otherwise be irreversibly lost under binary eviction, while preserving key vectors for attention routing stability. Most existing SR methods function within a bi-level optimization framework: an outer loop that searches for the discrete equation structure, and an inner loop that optimizes the continuous parameters of that structure. Crucially, parameter-fitting quality directly determines a structure's score and thus the outer-loop search. However, nonlinear operators make the inner loop highly non-convex, and budget-driven reliance on fast local solvers (e.g., BFGS) often yields poor local minima and underestimated scores for correct structures. This ``Good Structure, Bad Score'' phenomenon becomes a key bottleneck, degrading efficiency and misguiding the search away from the true equation. To resolve this, we propose SAGE-Fit (Structure-Aware and Semantics-Guided Evaluator for Symbolic Regression), an SR-native fitting framework that exploits the dual native priors of symbolic expressions. By capitalizing on the structural and semantic priors unique to SR, we design tailored modules for each property, thereby effectively mitigating this optimization bottleneck. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach, as a plug-and-play module, significantly enhances evaluation fidelity and universally improves the performance of various SR systems.

</details>


### [158] [Prudent-Banker: No Extra Fees for Baseline Safety in Adversarial Bandits With and Without Delays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23351)
*Ting Hu,Luanda Cai,Emmanouil-Vasileios Vlatakis-Gkaragkounis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Prudent-Banker算法，解决延迟反馈下安全约束的多臂赌博机问题，实现最优的安全-鲁棒性权衡，达到伪后悔$\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+\sqrt{D})$和对安全基准的$\widetilde{O}(1)$后悔，且在各种延迟分布下表现优于标准基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在即时反馈下可平衡安全与探索，但任意延迟可能导致保守与探索切换时机错误，危及安全保证，因此需要一种能适应延迟并保持安全性的新算法。

Method: 结合延迟自适应的在线镜像下降与改进的分阶段激进机制，引入延迟校准的重启阈值，以严格考虑未观测反馈带来的最坏扭曲，并可靠检测比较器次优性。

Result: 建立了新的安全约束延迟赌博机下界，证明Prudent-Banker的后悔界限不可改进（对数因子内），是首个同时实现最优安全与鲁棒性的算法。

Conclusion: Prudent-Banker在有无延迟反馈的情况下均实现了安全与学习之间的最优权衡，实验验证其在多种延迟分布下有效平衡安全与性能。

Abstract: We study adversarial multi-armed bandits with and without delayed feedback under a safety-aware goal: achieving minimax-optimal worst-case regret while keeping nearly constant regret relative to a designated "safe" baseline policy. Existing approaches can balance this trade-off with immediate feedback for smooth comparators, but arbitrary delays can mistime transitions between conservatism and exploration, endangering the safety guarantee. To bridge this gap, we propose Prudent-Banker, a novel algorithm that combines a delay-adapted variant of Online Mirror Descent with a modified phased-aggression mechanism. Its key technical contribution is a delay-calibrated restart threshold that rigorously accounts for the worst-case distortion induced by unobserved feedback and reliably detects comparator suboptimality. We also establish new lower bounds for safety-constrained adversarial delayed bandits, showing that the regret guarantees of Prudent-Banker are unimprovable, up to logarithmic factors, under the baseline-safety requirement. To the best of our knowledge, Prudent-Banker is the first algorithm to achieve the optimal safety--robustness trade-off: pseudo-regret $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{T}+\sqrt{D})$ together with $\widetilde{O}(1)$ regret against the safe comparator, both with and without delays. Experiments across diverse delay distributions show that, unlike standard delay-robust baselines, Prudent-Banker effectively balances safety and learning.

### [159] [CoSPlay: Cooperative Self-Play at Test-Time with Self-Generated Code and Unit Test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23491)
*Zhangyi Hu,Chenhui Liu,Tian Huang,Jindong Li,Yang Yang,Jiemin Wu,Zining Zhong,Menglin Yang,Yutao Yue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CoSPlay 是一种无需真实单元测试（GT UTs）和训练的框架，通过代码与单元测试的协同自演进，提升LLM代码生成性能。它利用双向通过计数信号在代码-测试执行矩阵中迭代优化代码与测试，最终基于输出一致性选择最优代码。在多个基准上，CoSPlay 显著提升代码正确率（BoN）和测试准确率，达到甚至超越依赖GT数据的SOTA方法，且具备良好的可扩展性和模型泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR和TTS方法严重依赖高质量的真值单元测试（GT UTs），而生成高质量自定义单元测试存在噪声和错误关联问题，导致代码与测试质量相互制约，难以提升。因此亟需一种无需GT UTs、无需训练的高效推理框架来实现代码与测试的联合优化。

Method: CoSPlay 采用协同自演进机制：首先探索多样解法并识别潜在失败模式以生成判别性测试思路；其次利用代码-测试执行矩阵中的双向通过计数信号，迭代地修剪弱代码、修复或替换不可靠测试；最后在多个高通过代码中，依据最大输出一致性聚类选择最终代码，确保正确代码在相同输入下保持一致。

Result: 在四个挑战性基准上，CoSPlay 在 Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct 上将平均 BoN 从 22.1% 提升至 33.2%，测试准确率从 14.6% 提升至 78.3%，表现媲美甚至超越 CURE-7B（RLVR 模型）。当应用于 CURE-7B 时，进一步提升 BoN 5.7%。其在不同模型骨架上均表现优异，且随计算预算增加持续提升，证明其为无需GT数据的可扩展代码生成方案。

Conclusion: CoSPlay 成功实现了无需真值单元测试和训练的高效代码生成，通过代码与测试的协同进化，在不依赖外部监督的情况下显著提升生成质量，为大规模、低成本、高性能的LLM代码生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recently, Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) and Test-Time Scaling (TTS) have advanced LLM code generation through executable verification. Yet Ground-Truth Unit Tests (GT UTs) remain a bottleneck: SOTA RLVR methods require them for costly training, while existing TTS methods lose competitiveness without them. This motivates GT-free TTS, where existing methods directly use self-generated UTs to refine and select code candidates. Yet such UTs are often noisy or spuriously coupled with wrong code, and UT quality in turn cannot be validated without reliable code. The key challenge is therefore to jointly improve both. To this end, we present CoSPlay, a GT-free, training-free framework that jointly improves codes and UTs through cooperative self-play. It first explores diverse solution ideas and identifies their potential failure modes to produce discriminative UT ideas. It then uses bidirectional pass-count signals from the Code-UT execution matrix to iteratively prune or fix weak codes and refresh or replace unreliable UTs, letting the two pools co-evolve. Finally, when multiple codes remain tied at the highest pass count, it picks the final code from the largest output-consensus cluster, since correct codes agree on the same inputs while wrong codes diverge. Experiments on four challenging benchmarks show that CoSPlay on Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct improves average BoN from 22.1% to 33.2% and UT accuracy from 14.6% to 78.3%, matching or surpassing the RLVR model CURE-7B. When applied to CURE-7B, it further improves BoN by 5.7%. CoSPlay also generalizes across diverse backbones and outperforms GT-free TTS baselines under comparable token budgets, with continued gains as the budget scales up. These results suggest a scalable inference strategy for competitive code generation without any GT data.

### [160] [Instance-Optimal Estimation with Multiple LLM Judges on a Budget](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23362)
*Junghyun Lee,Sanghwa Kim,Yassir Jedra,Alexandre Proutière,Se-Young Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在预算有限的情况下，如何高效分配评估查询给异质的评判者（judges）和不同的提示-响应对（prompt-response pairs），以获得最准确的评分估计。针对这一问题，作者提出了一个名为“预算内异方差多评判者估计”的框架，并分析了逆方差加权估计器（IVWE）的表现，推导出最优的理论分配策略。由于实际中评判者的方差未知，作者进一步提出EST-IVWE算法，通过构建乐观偏倚的方差估计来实现自适应分配，并证明其性能接近理论最优。此外，作者建立了匹配的局部极小极大下界，证明所提方法的实例最优性。技术上，他们使用Assouad型期望论证而非Fano型高概率论证，以保留局部方差结构，从而得到更精确的下界。实验部分在合成数据和HelpSteer2数据集上验证了所提方法优于均匀分配等基准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型评估依赖于LLM作为评判者（LLM-as-a-judge）协议，但该过程成本高昂且存在异质性：不同评判者价格与可靠性不同，每个提示-响应对的难度也各异。因此，在固定预算下如何合理分配评估任务以最大化评分准确性成为一个关键问题。

Method: 提出‘预算内异方差多评判者估计’问题建模；分析逆方差加权估计器（IVWE）并推导其理论最优分配方案；设计EST-IVWE算法，利用乐观偏倚的方差估计实现自适应分配；采用Assouad型在期望下的论证方法建立紧致的局部极小极大下界。

Result: EST-IVWE算法在理论上达到接近最优的性能，其误差率与理想情况下的Oracle IVWE仅相差低阶项；所提方法在合成数据和HelpSteer2数据集上的实验结果表明，显著优于均匀分配等基线方法。

Conclusion: 本文为大语言模型评估中的资源分配问题提供了理论完备且实践有效的解决方案，通过自适应的异质评判者调度机制，在有限预算下实现了更精准的评分估计。同时，提出的理论工具（如Assouad型下界）可推广至其他具有局部方差结构的估计问题。

Abstract: Evaluating large language models increasingly relies on LLM-as-a-judge protocols, but such evaluations remain costly: different judges have different prices and reliabilities, and the difficulty of each prompt-response pair can vary substantially. This raises a basic allocation question: under a fixed budget, how should one distribute evaluation queries across heterogeneous judges and instances to obtain the most accurate score estimates? We formalize this question as *budgeted heteroskedastic multi-judge estimation*. Given $K$ prompt-response pairs, $J$ judges with known costs, and unknown query-judge variances, the goal is to estimate a bounded score vector while minimizing an $\ell_p$-error. Our first contribution is to analyze the inverse-variance weighted estimator (IVWE) and to derive the oracle allocation that minimizes its error rate. Since this allocation depends on the unknown variances, we then address the practical unknown-variance setting by proposing EST-IVWE, an adaptive algorithm that constructs and leverages *optimistically biased* variance estimates to stabilize the empirical allocation. We prove that EST-IVWE matches the oracle IVWE rate up to lower-order terms in the budget. Our second and central theoretical contribution is a matching *local* minimax lower bound, which establishes the instance-optimality of the proposed algorithms. A key technical insight is that Fano-type high-probability arguments are too coarse for this problem: their packing construction loses the local variance structure that governs the optimal allocation. We instead use an Assouad-type in-expectation argument, based on local perturbations, which preserves this structure and yields the sharp allocation-dependent lower bound. Finally, we numerically validate the superiority of our approach over naïve uniform allocation on synthetic and HelpSteer2 datasets.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统扩散语言模型在生成过程中无法有效捕捉解码词元间的相关性，导致生成质量与推理吞吐量之间存在严重权衡。为突破这一瓶颈，需要设计一种既能保持高质量生成又具备高效率的新型生成框架。

Method: 提出 DiLaDiff 模型，包含三个核心组件：(1) 通过微调现有掩码扩散语言模型获得具有语义能力的连续潜在空间；(2) 构建基于编码器分布的潜在扩散模型以学习先验；(3) 使用一致性模型将学习到的先验蒸馏为少步潜动生成模型，从而实现高效推理。

Conclusion: DiLaDiff 有效缓解了扩散语言模型中生成质量与推理效率之间的矛盾，通过连续潜在空间与一致性蒸馏机制，在保证高质量生成的同时实现了极高的推理效率，为高效语言生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion language models intrinsically fail to capture correlations between decoded tokens, which leads to a harsh trade-off between sampling quality and throughput. To solve this issue, we propose DiLaDiff, a variant of masked diffusion language models with three components: (1) a continuous latent space with semantic capabilities, learned by an auto-encoder fine-tuned from an existing masked diffusion language model; (2) a latent diffusion model learning the prior over the encoder distribution; (3) a consistency model distilling the learned prior into a few-step latent generative model. We show that, even without distillation, our latent-guided diffusion model outperforms the masked diffusion baseline while significantly accelerating inference. Consistency distillation further lowers the computational overhead of continuous diffusion, such that the latent is generated in negligible time compared to discrete decoding.

Abstract: Diffusion and flow matching have emerged as expressive policy classes in reinforcement learning, but their reliance on multi-step denoising imposes substantial computational overhead at inference time, which is particularly problematic in online RL. However, MeanFlow typically requires samples from the target distribution to construct its target velocity field, which are unavailable in online RL. We propose Score-Based One-step MeanFlow Policy Optimization (SOM), an actor-critic algorithm that resolves this by constructing the target velocity field directly from the Q-function via score estimation and a probability flow ODE, thereby concentrating probability mass on high-value modes. ### [163] [Strong Teacher Not Needed? On Distillation in LLM Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23857)
*Taiming Lu,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型预训练中知识蒸馏的教师-学生关系，发现教师不一定要强；通过合理混合语言建模和知识蒸馏损失，即使小型且训练不足的教师也能提升大型学生模型。同时，更强的教师并不总带来更好效果，过度增加参数或训练样本可能导致蒸馏收益饱和甚至倒退。此外，蒸馏更有利于提升模型的泛化能力（如分布外和下游任务表现），而非仅在域内拟合。这些结果挑战了传统认为蒸馏需要强教师的普遍认知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过调整模型架构大小和训练令牌预算，构建强到弱、同级别以及弱到强的教师-学生关系，系统评估不同配置下知识蒸馏的效果，并分析语言建模与知识蒸馏损失的混合策略对性能的影响。

Result: 小而未充分训练的教师在适当损失混合下仍可提升大模型性能；过度增强教师反而可能削弱或逆转蒸馏收益；蒸馏显著提升模型的泛化能力，尤其在分布外和下游任务上。

Conclusion: 知识蒸馏并不必然依赖于强大的教师模型。教师的强度并非决定性因素，合理的训练策略和损失组合才是关键。这为大模型预训练中的知识蒸馏提供了新的视角和实践指导。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation generally assumes a strong-to-weak relationship where stronger teachers yield better students. In this work, we examine this assumption about distillation in large language model pretraining. By varying architecture sizes and training token budgets, we create strong-to-weak, same-level, and weak-to-strong teacher-student relationships, and study distillation's effectiveness under each. We find that the teacher need not be strong: with proper mixing of the language modeling and knowledge distillation losses, even small and undertrained teachers improve larger students. At the same time, a stronger teacher is not always better: pushing the teacher further, through more parameters or more training tokens, can saturate or even reverse the distillation gains. We further observe that distillation improves generalization (out-of-distribution and downstream performance) more readily than in-domain fitting. Together, these results challenge the common belief that distillation pretraining always requires a strong teacher.

### [164] [Every Component is a Lookup: Token Attribution and Composition from a Single Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23393)
*Po-Kai Chen,Niki van Stein,Aske Plaat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Unpack 是一种无需干预、梯度或辅助训练的后向递归方法，可从单次前向传播中分解变压器模型中注意力和MLP子层的信用分配，识别组件间的交互强度及端到端路径（带K/Q/V组合标签），并实现逐标记归因。该方法在间接宾语识别任务上成功恢复了已有机制结构，并在不同规模的Pythia模型中一致检测到关键抑制模式，验证了其对机械结构的追踪能力。

Method: 基于注意力与MLP共享的键值模板φ(S)U，提出后向递归算法Unpack，通过单一前向传播解耦信用分配，生成任意组件间的交互强度、带有K/Q/V标签的端到端路径及每标记的归因。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability of transformers requires identifying not just which components matter but how they compose into the computational route that produced a prediction. Both attention and MLP follow a shared key-value template $φ(S)U$. We exploit this structure to develop Unpack, a backward recursion that decomposes credit through both sublayers, producing interaction strengths between any two components, named end-to-end paths with K/Q/V composition labels, and per-token attribution from a single forward pass, without intervention, gradients, or auxiliary training. We evaluate on the indirect object identification task. On GPT-2 small, the method recovers all three composition connections described by Wang et al. (2023), including the mode-specific routing of each connection (K, Q, or V). To test token-level attribution beyond trivial copying, we compare two occurrences of the same name in the same decomposition: the first mention retains strong credit while the duplicate-detection position is suppressed, a pattern absent in matched control prompts. Across the Pythia family from 160M to 6.9B parameters, this suppression pattern is consistently recovered at every scale, demonstrating that the method tracks mechanistic structure without ground-truth circuit labels. Code is available at https://github.com/Fun-Cry/unpacklm.

### [165] [Parametric Prior Mapping Framework for Non-stationary Probabilistic Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23402)
*Jinglin Li,Jun Tan,QI Fang,Ning Gui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PPM框架通过将参数化结构先验注入生成建模过程，结合了参数方法的高效性与生成模型的表达能力，实现了在非平稳多变量时间序列预测中的高精度与低计算开销。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数化方法缺乏灵活性，而深度生成模型需要大量数据和计算资源才能捕捉复杂时序依赖关系，因此需要一种既能保持效率又能提升表达能力的新方法。

Method: 提出Parametric Prior Mapping（PPM）框架，利用参数估计器生成动态自适应先验，并通过可学习映射引导复杂预测分布的学习，结合混合目标函数进行训练。

Result: 实验表明，PPM在处理非平稳数据方面优于现有基线模型，在准确性和计算效率之间取得了更优的平衡，同时具备良好的不确定性校准能力。

Conclusion: PPM成功融合了参数方法的效率与生成模型的表达力，为非平稳多变量时间序列预测提供了一种高效且精准的解决方案。

Abstract: Effectively modeling non-stationary dynamics in probabilistic multivariate time series(MTS) forecasting requires balancing expressiveness with robustness. Existing parametric approaches benefit from strong inductive biases but lack flexibility, whereas deep generative models struggle to capture complex temporal dependencies without extensive data and computation. We introduce Parametric Prior Mapping (PPM), a framework that injects parametric structural priors into a generative modeling process. Specifically, PPM utilizes a parametric estimator to derive a dynamic, adaptive prior that guides the learning of a complex predictive distribution via a learnable mapping. This design allows the model to retain the efficiency of parametric methods while exploiting the expressive power of generative models. Trained with a hybrid objective, PPM yields precise forecasts with well-calibrated uncertainty estimates. Empirical results show that PPM outperforms existing baselines in handling non-stationary data, offering a superior trade-off between accuracy and computational efficiency. The code is available at https://github.com/ljl8336/PPM.

### [166] [Hybrid Quantum-Classical Corrective Diffusion Modeling for Meteorological Downscaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23403)

Abstract: Statistical downscaling is a crucial component of the weather modeling field, where high-resolution outputs must be reconstructed from coarse-resolution inputs with the full cost of dynamical refinement. In this work, we investigate a hybrid quantum-classical corrective diffusion model for probabilistic statistical downscaling of weather fields. The proposed model inserts variational quantum circuit layers into the most compressed bottleneck of the diffusion UNet while leaving the regression branch fully classical. This placement tests whether quantum circuits can act as compact nonlinear feature maps for latent-channel mixing. We evaluate intra-channel and cross-channel ansätze on 10m wind components. On the 2020 validation set, the hybrid models remain stable, preserve the large-scale spatial organization of the generated wind fields, and improve both MAE and CRPS relative to a classical corrective diffusion model in several configurations. Structural diagnostics further show that the hybrid variants preserve kinetic-energy spectra and windspeed distributions similar to its classical counterpart while producing controlled changes in tail behavior, extreme-windspeed localization, and joint wind field components structure. Backend studies on the 2020 validation set show negligible impact from simulated device noise at the tested circuit scale, whereas real-hardware deployment remains limited by qubit availability and execution fidelity. The 2021 out-of-distribution test shows that these in-distribution gains do not transfer uniformly under temporal shift, revealing a generalization gap that motivates future mitigation through stabilization and regularization. These results show that bottleneck-level quantum hybridization can make a nontrivial contribution to weather statistical downscaling, while also highlighting that circuit scale and hardware deployment remain key limiting factors.

*Phuc Duc Nguyen,Quang Duc Nguyen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Existing class-wise targeted attacks remain impractical for stealthy exploitation in this setting: since TTA operates on batches, forcing a subset of samples toward a target label unintentionally pulls similar benign samples along, resulting in a conspicuously high frequency of the target label that is easy to detect. To capture a more realistic threat, we introduce a sample-wise targeted attack. Unlike prior approaches, the attacker aims to misclassify only inputs carrying an attacker-chosen trigger, while preserving the global label distribution of benign queries to evade detection. To achieve this, we propose a meta-learning-based attack with a novel priority-aware gradient alignment strategy that explicitly prioritizes attack success. The strategy formulates the gradient update as an ellipsoidal trust-region problem, mitigating the misalignment between attack success and distributional stealth, while providing theoretical guarantees for effective optimization of the attack objective in the presence of gradient misalignment. Extensive experiments on CIFAR-10-C, CIFAR-100-C, and ImageNet-C across TTA protocols demonstrate that our method achieves high targeted success rates while maintaining a label distribution that is consistent with the no-attack baseline, making it difficult to detect in unlabeled TTA deployment scenarios. Furthermore, we demonstrate that our attack shows strong robustness against existing defenses.

Existing works in this direction have primarily focused on image-based RL and rotational symmetry such as $\mathrm{SO(2)}$, leaving state-based RL and reflection symmetry largely underexplored. In this work, we focus on state-based continuous control tasks and exploit reflection symmetry by introducing Reflex, a paradigm that seamlessly integrates with both on-policy and off-policy RL algorithms. Abstract: Most black-box optimization methods require extensive hyperparameter tuning, often limiting their ability to generalize across different optimization domains. Using this dataset, we train a family of foundation models at multiple scales, ranging from 2M to 80M parameters and from 200M to 2B training tokens, and study their scaling behavior with respect to compute. ### [170] [Hinge Regression Trees and HRT-Boost: Newton-Optimized Oblique Learning for Compact Tabular Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23422)
*Hongyi Li,Jun Xu,Hong Yan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HRT框架将斜向分裂重构为非线性最小二乘问题，利用两个线性预测器的max/min包络实现类似ReLU的表示能力，并通过阻尼牛顿法优化节点目标函数。理论证明其具有$O(δ^2)$逼近率，且为通用逼近器。基于此提出HRT-Boost，结合节点级牛顿更新与阶段式梯度下降，在平方损失下保证经验风险递减。实验表明，该方法在合成与真实数据上性能优于单树基线，且比强集成基线更紧凑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决斜向决策树因分裂优化的离散性和非凸性带来的高质量学习挑战。

Method: 将每个斜向分裂建模为非线性最小二乘问题，使用两个线性预测器的max/min包络实现类似ReLU的表示能力；采用阻尼牛顿法及其回溯线搜索变体进行节点优化；构建HRT-Boost集成方法，融合牛顿更新与阶段式梯度下降。

Result: 理论证明HRT是通用逼近器，逼近误差为$O(δ^2)$；HRT-Boost在平方损失下具有阶段式经验风险减少保证；实验显示其性能优于现有单树和集成基线，且模型更紧凑。

Conclusion: HRT框架有效克服了斜向决策树优化难题，其提出的HRT-Boost在精度与模型简洁性上均表现出色，具备良好的理论保障与实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Learning high-quality oblique decision trees remains a significant challenge due to the discrete and non-convex nature of split optimization. We present the Hinge Regression Tree (HRT) framework, which reframes each oblique split as a nonlinear least-squares problem over two linear predictors whose max/min envelope induces ReLU-like representation capacity. We show that the resulting node-level optimization can be interpreted as a damped Newton method, and we establish the monotonic decrease of the node objective for its backtracking line-search variant. We establish, theoretically, that HRT is a universal approximator with an explicit $O(δ^2)$ approximation rate. Building upon this base learner, we propose HRT-Boost, a mathematically synergistic ensemble extension that couples node-level Newton updates with stage-wise functional gradient descent. We show that this ensemble construction admits a stage-wise empirical risk reduction guarantee under the squared loss. Empirical evaluations on synthetic and real-world benchmarks show that HRT is highly competitive with established single-tree baselines, and HRT-Boost compares favorably with strong ensemble baselines and often yields substantially more compact models. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/Hongyi-Li-sz/HRT-Boost.

### [171] [Onsager-Machlup Posterior Transport for Deep Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23434)
*Jian Xu,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OM-Path 提出一种基于后验传输的深度高斯过程（DGP）近似推理方法，通过确定性采样器将可追踪参考分布映射到后验相关的诱导变量，利用来自 Doob 桥参考扩散的路径先验进行正则化。该方法结合概率流常微分方程（ODE）与 DBVI 的前向随机微分方程（SDE），无需分数匹配即可获得闭式参考漂移，并以 Onsager-Machlup 动作作为路径正则项。在有限 $\varepsilon$ 下，目标函数对应于温度化的 Doob 桥路径后验的负对数未归一化密度，且由 Freidlin-Wentzell 大偏差原理与小噪声下的 MAP 路径等价。两个严格路径空间 ELBO 变体（FFJORD log-det；OM 正则化 CNF）作为消融实验。在七个 UCI 回归基准上的配对威尔科xon检验显示，OM-Path 在两个最大数据集上显著优于 DBVI（power: p=0.014, NLL 0.012；protein: p=0.002, RMSE 0.716 vs. 0.764, NLL 1.086 vs. 1.149），在 yacht/qsar 上持平，但在小样本噪声数据的 boston/energy/concrete 上落后于 DBVI。严格 ELBO 变体均未超越 DBVI，表明在此设置下降低路径目标方差比精确密度追踪更为重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Deep Gaussian Processes (DGPs) 中诱导变量的近似推断是主要计算瓶颈。现有方法或使用显式密度拟合（如 DSVI、IPVI 等）或依赖 MCMC 采样（如 SGHMC），但存在效率或精度限制。本文旨在通过后验传输框架，构建一个更高效、更准确的确定性采样机制，以突破当前方法的性能边界。

Method: 提出 OM-Path（即 FBVI-bridge-Path），将 DGP 推理建模为后验传输问题：学习一个确定性采样器，将参考分布映射至后验相关的诱导变量。该方法基于 Song 的概率流 ODE，应用于 DBVI 的 Doob 桥前向 SDE。参考漂移由桥接边际系数闭式给出（无需分数匹配），路径正则项采用 Onsager-Machlup 动作。训练时使用有限 $\varepsilon$，目标函数对应于温度化 Doob 桥路径后验的负对数未归一化密度，并通过 Freidlin-Wentzell 大偏差原理与小噪声下的 MAP 路径建立联系。进一步设计两种严格路径空间 ELBO 变体作为对照实验。

Result: 在七个 UCI 回归基准上进行配对威尔科克斯检验，结果表明：在 power 与 protein 数据集上，OM-Path 显著优于 DBVI（p=0.014，NLL 0.012；p=0.002，RMSE 0.716 vs. 0.764，NLL 1.086 vs. 1.149）；yacht 与 qsar 上表现相当；在 boston、energy、concrete 上略逊于 DBVI，尤其在小样本噪声数据中。严格路径空间 ELBO 变体均未能超越 DBVI，说明在该设定下，路径目标方差的减小比精确密度跟踪更重要。

Conclusion: OM-Path 通过后验传输框架和路径正则化机制，在大规模数据上实现了对现有 DGP 推理方法的显著提升。其成功关键在于有效控制路径目标的方差，而非追求精确密度建模。这揭示了在复杂变分推断中，方差优化可能优先于密度匹配，为未来 DGP 及其他生成模型的推断设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Approximate inference over inducing variables is the central computational bottleneck of Deep Gaussian Processes (DGPs). Existing methods either fit an explicit density $q_φ(\bU)$ by an ELBO (DSVI, IPVI, DDVI, DBVI) or sample by MCMC (SGHMC). We instead frame DGP inference as \emph{posterior transport}: learn a deterministic sampler that maps a tractable reference measure to posterior-relevant inducing variables, regularised by a path prior derived from the Doob-bridged reference diffusion. Our realisation, \textbf{OM-Path} (formally FBVI-bridge-Path), uses Song's probability-flow ODE applied to DBVI's Doob-bridged forward SDE; the reference drift is closed-form from the bridge marginal coefficients (no score matching) and the path regulariser is the \textbf{Onsager--Machlup action}. At the finite-$ε$ value used at training, the objective is the negative log unnormalised density of a tempered Doob-bridge path posterior, and Theorem 1 identifies it with the same posterior's small-noise MAP path via the Freidlin--Wentzell LDP. Two strict path-space ELBO variants on the same bridge backbone (FFJORD log-det; OM-regularised CNF) are derived as ablations. Under a matched-seed paired Wilcoxon test against DBVI on seven UCI regression benchmarks, OM-Path delivers statistically significant wins on the two largest datasets (\textit{power}: $p\!=\!0.014$, NLL $\mathbf{0.012}$ matching the DSVI baseline of $0.017$; \textit{protein}: $p\!=\!0.002$, RMSE $\mathbf{0.716}$ vs.\ $0.764$, NLL $\mathbf{1.086}$ vs.\ $1.149$), statistical ties on \textit{yacht} / \textit{qsar}, and concedes \textit{boston} / \textit{energy} / \textit{concrete} to DBVI on small-$N$ noisy data. The strict-ELBO variants do not clear DBVI on any UCI metric: in this regime, reducing the variance of the path objective dominates exact-density tracking.

</details>


### [172] [Commutator-Induced Uncertainty in VAEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23449)
*Tahereh Dehdarirad,Michael Felsberg,Gabriel Eilertsen,Ziliang Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于李群的变分自编码器（Lie Group VAE）框架，通过几何与代数结合的方式诊断并显式建模潜在空间中的非交换结构。该方法首先在无约束条件下训练模型，并利用有限的Baker-Campbell-Hausdorff偏差和重建顺序交换测试来度量代数上的非交换性；发现潜在非交换性与重建行为之间存在尺度不匹配。随后引入数据驱动的形变-稳定性约束，使解码器敏感性与代数非交换性对齐。在dSprites、3DShapes、3DCars和CelebA等数据集上，相比传统VAE和对称性感知基线（如beta-VAE、CLG-VAE、CFASL），该方法提升了重建质量，实现了更一致的解码行为，展现出更清晰的顺序依赖潜变量组合和更稳定的重构结果，在CelebA上还表现出更真实的重建与有意义的潜变量交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对称性感知变分自编码器通过代数正则化强制交换性，虽适用于交换变换群，但会抑制数据中固有的非交换结构。因此需要一种能主动诊断并反映非交换性的新方法，以提升模型对复杂几何变换的建模能力。

Method: 提出Lie Group VAE框架，分两阶段训练：第一阶段在无结构约束下训练模型，通过有限BCH偏差和重建顺序交换测试测量代数非交换性和解码器对顺序的敏感性；第二阶段引入数据驱动的形变-稳定性约束，调节解码器敏感性以匹配潜在空间的非交换性。

Result: 在合成数据集上，该方法显著提升重建质量，解码行为更符合潜在空间的非交换结构；在CelebA上，实现更真实重建和可解释的因子分离，同时捕捉到潜变量间的顺序依赖交互。

Conclusion: 显式诊断和建模非交换性优于强制交换性，所提出的Lie Group VAE框架能够有效提升模型对复杂几何变换的表达能力，尤其在包含顺序依赖关系的数据中表现优越。

Abstract: Variational autoencoders (VAEs) often struggle to represent non-commutative structure in learned latent spaces. Symmetry-aware VAEs commonly address this issue by enforcing commutativity through algebraic regularization, which is appropriate for commutative transformation groups but can suppress meaningful non-commutative structure when it is intrinsic to the data. We argue that non-commutativity should instead be explicitly diagnosed and reflected in reconstruction behavior. We introduce a Lie Group VAE framework that combines geometric and algebraic perspectives on uncertainty while separating discrete generative factors from continuous geometric transformations. In a first phase, the model is trained without structural constraints while algebraic non-commutativity is measured through finite Baker-Campbell-Hausdorff deviations and decoder order sensitivity is measured through reconstruction order-swap tests. These diagnostics reveal a scale mismatch between latent non-commutativity and reconstruction behavior under unconstrained training. In a second phase, we introduce a deformation-stability constraint with a data-driven calibration constant that aligns decoder sensitivity with algebraic non-commutativity. We evaluate the framework on dSprites, 3DShapes, 3DCars, and CelebA against generic and symmetry-aware baselines, including beta-VAE, CLG-VAE, and CFASL. Across synthetic benchmarks, the method improves reconstruction quality and yields decoder-level behavior more consistent with latent non-commutative structure. Qualitative analyses show clearer order-dependent latent compositions and more stable reconstructions. On CelebA, the model yields more faithful reconstructions and factor-specific latent traversals than CFASL, while also exhibiting meaningful order-dependent interactions between learned latent directions.

</details>


### [173] [Class-Dependent Hybrid Data Augmentation for Multiclass Migraine Classification under Severe Class Imbalance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23453)
*Elvin Somón,Miguel A. Gutiérrez-Naranjo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究对先前的偏头痛分类研究进行了可复现性导向的重新评估，修正了数据泄露和度量偏差问题。提出三种新方法：(i) 基于ICHD-3 §1.2.3的临床动机型半侧头痛亚型聚合；(ii) 依据每类样本量分配生成方法的类依赖混合增强策略；(iii) 提出保真度不对称概念，主张比例约束增长而非完全类别平衡。在包含400名患者的七种偏头痛亚型数据集上进行两阶段实验，采用分层5折交叉验证与宏平均F1作为主要评估指标。修正方法学缺陷后，性能估计显著降低（校正后的宏F1基线为0.71），所提框架在八种评估模型中平均宏F1达0.862，优于Gaussian Copula（0.836）、CTGAN（0.815）及无增强基线（0.801），其中FT-Transformer结合比例增强时达到峰值0.914。无增强的FT-Transformer基线为0.896，表明临床动机的类别聚合贡献了大部分绝对提升，而框架的主要贡献在于跨分类器的平均鲁棒性提升，凸显问题定义的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的偏头痛分类研究存在数据泄露和度量偏差问题，导致性能估计虚高。为提高研究的可复现性和临床实用性，亟需修正方法学缺陷，并引入更符合临床逻辑的分类结构与数据增强策略。

Method: 通过纠正数据泄露与度量偏差，提出临床驱动的亚型聚合、类依赖混合增强策略以及基于保真度不对称的比例约束增长机制；在400例患者、七种亚型的数据集上，采用两阶段实验设计与分层5折交叉验证，以宏平均F1为主要评估指标，比较多种增强方法与分类器的表现。

Result: 修正方法学缺陷后，宏F1基线降至0.71。所提框架在八类分类器中平均宏F1达0.862，优于各单一增强方法（如Gaussian Copula: 0.836, CTGAN: 0.815, 无增强: 0.801）。其中，FT-Transformer配合比例增强时表现最佳（0.914）。无增强的FT-Transformer基线为0.896，说明临床聚合是性能提升主因；框架的核心贡献在于提升整体鲁棒性，强调问题定义的重要性。

Conclusion: 本研究证实，方法学严谨性对偏头痛分类研究至关重要。通过临床动机的类别聚合与合理的数据增强策略，不仅提升了分类性能，更增强了模型在不同设定下的稳健性。问题定义本身在模型成功中扮演核心角色，提示未来研究应更加重视科学假设与临床意义的对齐。

Abstract: We conducted a reproducibility-oriented re-evaluation of prior migraine classification studies, correcting for data leakage and metric bias. We then introduced (i) a clinically motivated aggregation of two hemiplegic subtypes following ICHD-3 §1.2.3, (ii) a class-dependent hybrid augmentation strategy that assigns generation methods based on per-class sample size, and (iii) the concept of fidelity asymmetry, motivating proportionally constrained growth as an alternative to full class balance. Experiments were performed on a dataset of 400 patients across seven migraine subtypes under a two-stage protocol, including the six-class configuration described above. Models were evaluated using stratified 5-fold cross-validation with macro-averaged F1 as the primary metric.
  Correcting methodological flaws reduces previously inflated performance estimates, with the corrected macro-F1 baseline standing at 0.71. The proposed framework consistently outperformed individual augmenters in macro-F1 averaged across the eight evaluated classifiers (0.862 vs. 0.836 for Gaussian Copula, 0.815 for CTGAN, and 0.801 for the no-augmentation baseline), and achieved its peak result of 0.914 with FT-Transformer under proportional augmentation. The no-augmentation FT-Transformer baseline (0.896) shows that, at the per-classifier ceiling, clinically motivated class aggregation accounts for most of the absolute improvement; the framework's principal measurable contribution is the gain in average robustness across classifiers, highlighting the dominant role of problem formulation.

### [174] [Automated Random Embedding for Practical Bayesian Optimization with Unknown Effective Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23473)
*Hong Qian,Xiang Shu,Xiang Xia,Xuhui Liu,Yangde Fu,Bei Liang,Huibin Wang,Liang Dou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为动态共享嵌入贝叶斯优化（DSEBO）的新方法，用于解决高维贝叶斯优化中因有效维度未知而导致的维度灾难问题。DSEBO通过动态调整低维子空间的维度，并在当前子空间出现初步收敛时自动提升维度，同时共享已查询的解以更好初始化新子空间，从而提高优化效率。理论分析表明其能更优地平衡近似误差与优化误差。实验结果显示，相比现有先进方法，DSEBO在不同维度函数及真实任务上均显著降低了优化遗憾和时间消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机嵌入方法依赖专家预设或试错方式确定子空间维度，但有效维度常未知，导致优化性能受限且资源浪费。因此亟需一种能自动适应未知有效维度的动态策略。

Method: DSEBO从低维子空间开始优化，当检测到当前子空间中的解出现初步收敛时，自动切换至更高维子空间；其后续维度由各子空间解的质量决定，并共享历史查询结果以实现更好的初始化，从而实现自适应维度调整。

Result: DSEBO在多种高维函数和真实世界任务上表现出显著优于现有方法的性能，不仅降低优化遗憾，还减少所需时间，验证了其在处理未知有效维度问题上的有效性。

Conclusion: DSEBO通过动态调整子空间维度并共享查询信息，在有效维度未知的情况下实现了高效、鲁棒的高维贝叶斯优化，为复杂黑箱函数优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Bayesian optimization is widely employed for optimizing complex black-box functions but struggles with the curse of dimensionality. Random embedding, as a dimension reduction strategy, simplifies tasks that possess the effective dimension by optimizing within a low-dimensional subspace. However, determining the effective dimension of a task in advance remains a significant challenge, which influences the selection of the subspace dimensionality and the optimization performance. Traditional methods use fixed subspace dimensions provided by experts or rely on trial and error to estimate subspace dimensions with resources consumed. To this end, this paper proposes an automated random embedding for high-dimensional Bayesian optimization with unknown effective dimension, called Dynamic Shared Embedding Bayesian Optimization (DSEBO). DSEBO starts with a low dimension and switches to a higher subspace if the solutions in the current subspace show preliminary convergence. DSEBO dynamically determines the dimension of the next subspace based on the quality of the solutions in different subspaces and shares the queried solutions with the new subspace for a better initialization. Theoretically, we derive a regret bound for DSEBO and demonstrate that DSEBO can better balance approximation and optimization errors. Extensive experiments on functions with dimensionality of varying magnitudes and real-world tasks with unknown effective dimensions reveal that, compared with state-of-the-art methods, alternating optimization across different subspaces results in significant improvements in high-dimensional optimization, both in terms of optimization regret and time.

</details>


### [175] [VACE: Learning Geometrically Structured Representations for Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23504)
*Alberto D. Cencillo,Leonardo Concepción,Isaac Triguero,Julián Luengo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VACE提出一种新的自监督异常检测方法，通过速度一致性目标训练通道感知编码器，使正常轨迹在嵌入空间中保持局部平滑且方向一致。测试时结合马氏位置得分与速度银行方向得分，实现对分布外和动态异常的联合检测。方法无需负样本或合成异常，在TSB-AD-M数据集上达到领先性能，显著优于更复杂、训练预算更大的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对比学习方法通过成对采样间接构建嵌入空间，缺乏对几何结构的显式控制，难以保证正常表示的紧凑性和距离的方向意义。因此需要一种能直接建模正常性并确保嵌入空间结构合理的方法。

Method: VACE采用速度一致性目标训练通道感知编码器，不依赖负样本或合成异常，使正常时间序列片段在嵌入空间中具有平滑且方向一致的轨迹。测试阶段使用马氏位置得分与速度银行方向得分的乘积进行异常判定。

Result: 在TSB-AD-M基准上取得当前最优表现，超越许多复杂度更高、训练资源更大的模型，验证了方法的有效性与高效性。

Abstract: Anomaly detection in multivariate time series is a critical task across a wide range of real-world applications, where abnormal behaviour is rare, labels are unavailable, and the cost of a miss is high. The central challenge is learning a characterisation of normality precise enough to flag deviations. Representation self-supervised learning, typically through contrastive approaches, addresses this by embedding temporal patches into a latent space where normality occupies a well-defined region, with anomalies detected by geometric deviation. However, contrastive approaches shape this space indirectly through pair-sampling heuristics, providing no explicit control over the geometric structure that distance-based scoring requires. This means how tightly normal representations are grouped, and whether distances are directionally meaningful. We present VACE (Velocity-Aligned Channel Embeddings), a self-supervised anomaly detection method that represents normality as a compact, directionally coherent region in the embedding space. To this end, VACE trains a channel-aware encoder through a velocity-consistency objective, with no negatives and no synthetic anomalies, so that normal trajectories are locally smooth and aligned. At test time, a Mahalanobis positional score and a velocity-bank directional score are combined multiplicatively, flagging points that are simultaneously off-distribution and dynamically atypical. Despite its simplicity, VACE achieves state-of-the-art performance on TSB-AD-M under rigorous evaluation, significantly outperforming more complex methods trained on substantially larger budgets.

### [176] [Precise: SDE-Consistent Stochastic Sampling for RL Post-Training of Flow-Matching Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23522)
*Jade Zou,Tao Huang,Weijie Kong,Junzhe Li,Yue Wu,Qi Tian,Jiangfeng Xiong,Jianwei Zhang,Liefeng Bo,Zhao Zhong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于强化学习的流匹配生成方法受限于随机采样器的设计，尤其是将确定性轨迹转为随机策略时，面临探索与稳定性之间的权衡以及离散化误差的问题，导致训练不稳定、收敛慢。

Method: 本文将采样器设计分解为两个部分：一是通过分析探索与稳定性的内在矛盾，设计出平衡两者的SDE调度；二是提出一种新近似方法，冻结干净潜在表示的后验均值，以确保去噪轨迹的SDE一致性，从而避免传统采样器引入过多离散化噪声或依赖启发式规则的问题。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become an effective way to improve prompt alignment and perceptual quality in diffusion and flow-matching generators. A critical step for applying online RL to flow matching is turning the deterministic sampling trajectory into a stochastic policy, typically by replacing the reverse-time Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE) with a Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE). The stochastic sampler, controlling the exploration behavior and denoising dynamics, is thus part of the policy, and its design can significantly affect the reward optimization performance. We break down the sampler design into two interdependent components: choosing the right amount of stochastic exploration, and discretizing the resulting SDE faithfully at the small step counts used in RL. To address the first component, we analyze the inherent tension between exploration and stability in denoising and derive an SDE schedule that balances the two. Turning to the discretization challenge, we use a toy example to show that existing samplers can deviate from the flow-matching process, either by introducing excessive discretization noise or by relying on heuristic rules that do not guarantee convergence to the data distribution. To address these issues, we propose Precise, a new stochastic sampler that balances effective exploration with stability. Crucially, Precise keeps the denoising trajectory SDE-consistent through a novel approximation that freezes the clean-latent posterior mean, resolving the excess noise issue in standard samplers. Extensive experiments demonstrate that this formulation leads to significantly faster and more stable reward optimization via reinforcement learning, achieving state-of-the-art alignment scores (e.g., PickScore, HPSv2.1) while requiring 13.1-53.2% less wall-clock training time to match the best in-domain performance of prior samplers.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Dimensionality Reduction (DR) methods are widely used to visualize high-dimensional data. One key task in DR-based analysis is discovering neighborhoods, which relies on analyzing the fine-grained local structure of a projection. However, DR is an inherently lossy process; no technique can perfectly preserve the high-dimensional relationships, and projections therefore contain visual artifacts. In this paper, we highlight a typically overlooked source of visual artifacts: ambiguous instances. These are instances that are highly similar to multiple mutually dissimilar neighborhoods in the high-dimensional space. Standard DR methods cannot faithfully project such instances, since each data instance is mapped to a single point in the visual space. As a result, such an instance is placed in only one of its neighborhoods (or in none at all), so only part of its neighborhood structure is represented. We call this distortion partial neighborhood embedding. In this paper, we introduce a graph-based approach that identifies ambiguous instances and replicates them as multiple points in the projection, placing each copy within its respective neighborhood. We use UMAP for our results, but our approach also generalizes to other local graph-based DR techniques, and we show that our approach reveals previously hidden neighborhood memberships in projections and reduces partial neighborhood embedding across multiple examples, and is further supported by quantitative analyses.

### [178] [Cost-Effective Model Evaluation with Meta-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23595)
*Trinh Pham,Viet Huynh,Hongzhi Yin,Quoc Viet Hung Nguyen,Thanh Tam Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MetaEvaluator 是一种成本低、模型无关的框架，可快速、无需标签地评估不同架构和模态的未知模型。它利用元学习从参考模型池中获得可迁移的初始化，从而在不进行每模型重训练的情况下准确评估新模型，显著降低评估成本。这是首个能在完全无标签数据集上评估新模型的模型无关框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习模型数量激增，传统评估方法依赖昂贵标注、重复微调或狭窄假设，难以跨模型家族迁移，无法高效验证新模型在未见无标签数据上的可靠性。

Method: 通过在参考模型池上使用元学习获取可迁移的初始化，使新模型的评估无需重新训练，并实现跨模型泛化，从而实现标签自由、成本低廉的性能评估。

Result: 实验表明，MetaEvaluator 在大幅降低评估成本的同时，能稳定且准确地估计模型性能，使大规模、无标签数据上的新兴模型基准测试成为可能。

Conclusion: MetaEvaluator 是首个能够对未见模型在完全无标签数据上进行快速、低成本、模型无关评估的框架，为未来大规模模型评测提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The rapid growth of machine learning has produced an ever-expanding ecosystem of models, making it increasingly challenging to verify the reliability of newly released models on unseen, unlabeled data. Conventional evaluation pipelines depend on expensive annotation, repeated fine-tuning, or narrow assumptions that fail to transfer across model families. We present MetaEvaluator, a cost-effective, model-agnostic framework for rapid, label-free assessment of unseen models spanning diverse architectures and modalities. MetaEvaluator leverages meta-learning over a pool of reference models to obtain a transferable initialization, enabling accurate evaluation of new models while amortizing cost across the pool and removing the need for per-model retraining. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first model-agnostic framework capable of evaluating new models on entirely unlabeled datasets. Extensive experiments show that MetaEvaluator produces stable and accurate performance estimates at substantially reduced cost compared to conventional approaches, making scalable benchmarking of emerging models on unlabeled data practical.
