### [180] [Is Dimensionality a Barrier for Retrieval Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23556)
*Kiril Bangachev,Guy Bresler,Jonathan Kogan,Yury Polyanskiy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了为何低维表示（约d≈1000）仍能使现代基于嵌入的检索模型扩展到数十亿甚至数万亿数据点。通过分析最大间隔嵌入，提出在维度d = O(m^(-2) log n)时可几乎达到无维度限制下的最优间隔，其中m为最大间隔。对于k稀疏查询-文档关联矩阵，证明d = O(k log(n/k))是实现最优间隔Θ(k^{-1/2})的充要条件，完全解决了[WBNL26]中的设定。此外，还给出了在更低维度d = o(k log(n/k))下构造大间隔嵌入的方法，并通过实验验证了sigmoid损失相比InfoNCE损失在生成大间隔嵌入方面具有明显优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究低维嵌入为何仍能支持大规模检索系统，理解最大间隔嵌入在有限维度下的表现极限，以揭示嵌入质量与维度之间的理论关系。

Method: 采用通信复杂性中的最大间隔嵌入模型，结合理论分析（上界与下界证明）和实验评估，研究在不同维度下实现最大间隔的可能性，并比较不同损失函数的表现。

Result: 证明了在维度d = O(m^(-2) log n)时可逼近无维度限制下的最优间隔；对于k稀疏场景，确定d = O(k log(n/k))为实现最优间隔的必要且充分条件；实验表明sigmoid损失优于InfoNCE损失。

Conclusion: 低维嵌入之所以能支撑超大规模检索，是因为最大间隔可以在远低于传统认知的维度下被有效实现。该结果为嵌入模型的高效设计提供了理论依据，并指出了损失函数选择对嵌入质量的关键影响。

Abstract: Why does the low dimensionality of representations, typically $d\approx 1000$, not prevent modern embedding-based retrieval models from scaling to billions, or even trillions, of data points? To answer this question, we study maximal-margin embeddings in the following retrieval model, classically studied in communication complexity [PS86] and more recently in embedding-based retrieval [WBNL26]. Let $A\in \{0,1\}^{N\times n}$ be a matrix indicating whether each of $N$ queries is relevant to each of $n$ documents. We are interested in the largest margin $m>0,$ denoted by $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(d, A),$ for which there exist unit norm embeddings of the queries and documents $\{U_j\}_{j = 1}^N, \{V_i\}_{i = 1}^n$ with the following property. $\langle U_j, V_i\rangle \ge m$ whenever $A_{ji} = 1$ and $\langle U_j, V_i\rangle \le -m$ otherwise. A large margin is a key proxy for representation quality: it controls both robustness to perturbations and compositional generalization across queries. Our main theorem establishes that the best possible margin without a restriction on the dimension, $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A),$ can be nearly achieved in dimension $d = O(\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A)^{-2}\log n)$ which improves a theorem of [BDES02]. Together with a matching lower bound in Theorem 1.5, we conclude that when $A\in \{0,1\}^{\binom{n}{k}\times n}$ is the matrix containing all possible $k$-sparse rows once, dimension $d = O(k\log (n/k))$ is necessary and sufficient for the maximal possible margin $\mathsf{m}^{\mathsf{rd}}(+\infty, A) = Θ(k^{-1/2})$ in this setting. This fully resolves the setup of [WBNL26]. We also give several constructions for large margins when $d = o(k\log (n/k)).$ Finally, we empirically test the InfoNCE and sigmoid losses for producing large margin embeddings and demonstrate a clear advantage of the sigmoid loss.

</details>

FM-CGM formalizes the causal pipeline through three core components: a concept extractor, a concept manipulator, and a counterfactual generator. By leveraging a large reasoning model for causal inference and a text-to-image diffusion model for generation, our approach enables zero-shot causal discovery, intervention, and counterfactual generation. We then develop Causal Semantic Guidance (CSG), a cross-attention-based mechanism that ensures semantic interventions propagate to descendant concepts while preserving invariant regions. ### [182] [MARS: Magnitude-Aware Rank Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23563)
*Muhammad Rajabinasab,Afsaneh M. Nejad,Arthur Zimek*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CD图仅依赖离散排名，忽略了模型间性能差距的大小，导致信息丢失，称为‘幅度盲’问题，需要更精细的评估方法。

Method: 提出MARS（Magnitude-Aware Rank Statistics），利用相对边际系数作为权重对离散排名进行加权，根据最佳与最差表现之间的距离动态调整排名，并结合CD值计算，实现更精确的统计表征。

Result: MARS能够更真实地呈现模型性能差异，在广泛实验中提供更深入的洞察，有效克服了传统CD图的幅度盲问题。

Abstract: Comprehensive evaluation of machine learning models is the key to make sure that they perform as robustly and consistently as desired. In order to summarize the experimental results and pick a winner, Critical Difference (CD) diagrams are used. Standard CD diagrams rely on discrete ranks, discarding the magnitude of performance gaps between models, raising an issue which we call magnitude-blindness. In order to address this issue, we propose Magnitude-Aware Rank Statistics (MARS) that incorporates a relative margin coefficient as a weight for the discrete ranks. This coefficient scales ranks based on the distance between the best and worst performers, with a dynamic projection to handle boundary cases. Followed by the calculation of a CD value, MARS results in a more realistic statistical representation of differences of model performances and more insights on how methods actually perform in vast and extensive experimental settings.

### [183] [Preisach Attention: A Hysteretic Model of Sequential Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23603)
*Piotr Frydrych*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Preisach Attention Layer（PAL），一种基于数学物理中经典 Preisach 滞后算子的新型序列建模架构。PAL 用可学习激活与去激活阈值的二元继电器算子替代 softmax 注意力机制，通过维护局部极值堆栈作为内部状态。单层 PAL-Transformer 在任意精度算术下为图灵完备，深度仅需 O(1)，优于标准硬注意力 Transformer 所需的 O(log n)；且 PAL 与 Transformer 的函数计算能力不可比较：PAL 可在 O(1) 层内计算历史范围统计，而 Transformer 支持随机访问检索，但 PAL 无法实现该功能而不引入辅助状态。其关键特性为速率无关性——PAL 仅响应局部极值序列，不依赖绝对位置或时间间隔。此外，极值堆栈是所有速率无关泛函的最小充分统计量，类比经典滞后的‘擦除’性质。因此，PAL 适用于长时程记忆、弱位置依赖任务，推理复杂度为 O(n log n)，显著低于标准注意力的 O(n²)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 模型在处理长序列时存在计算开销大、位置敏感等问题，尤其在需要长期记忆但对绝对位置不敏感的任务中效率低下。受数学物理中 Preisach 滞后理论启发，本文旨在设计一种具有速率无关性、高效记忆能力的新注意力机制，以提升对长序列历史信息的建模效率。

Method: 提出 Preisach Attention Layer（PAL），采用二元继电器算子模拟 Preisach 滞后行为，通过学习激活/去激活阈值动态更新内部极值堆栈。利用该结构构建单层 PAL-Transformer，并证明其在任意精度下具备图灵完备性，可通过模拟双栈下推自动机实现。进一步分析其与标准 Transformer 的函数能力差异，揭示两者在计算能力上的不可比较性。最后，从统计学角度论证极值堆栈作为速率无关函数的最小充分统计量。

Result: PAL-Transformer 仅需 O(1) 层即可实现图灵完备性，远优于标准 Transformer 的 O(log n)；在计算历史范围统计等任务上，PAL 实现 O(1) 层完成，而 Transformer 需 O(log n) 层；在随机访问任务上，标准 Transformer 具备优势，但 PAL 无法实现而无需额外状态。极值堆栈被证明是速率无关函数的最小充分统计量，且整体推理成本为 O(n log n)，显著低于标准注意力的 O(n²)。

Conclusion: PAL 是一种高效、具理论保障的序列建模架构，特别适合长序列记忆任务且对位置不敏感的应用场景。其核心优势在于速率无关性、低计算复杂度和强大的历史信息表达能力，为超越传统注意力机制提供了新范式。

Abstract: We introduce the Preisach Attention Layer (PAL), a novel sequence modelling architecture grounded in the classical Preisach hysteresis operator from mathematical physics. PAL replaces the softmax attention mechanism with a binary relay operator parameterised by learned activation and deactivation thresholds, maintaining a stack of local extrema as its internal state. A single-layer PAL-Transformer with O(1) depth is Turing-complete under arbitrary precision arithmetic, achievable through simulation of a two-stack pushdown automaton -- in contrast to the O(log n) depth required by standard hard-attention transformers. Second, we prove that the function classes computable by PAL and by the transformer are incomparable: PAL computes historical range statistics in O(1) layers that require O(log n) layers for transformers, while transformers support random-access retrieval that PAL cannot perform without auxiliary state. The separating property is rate-independence -- PAL responds only to the sequence of local extrema, not to absolute token positions or temporal spacing. Third, we show that the extremum stack constitutes a minimal sufficient statistic of the input history for all rate-independent functionals, providing a formal analogue of the wiping property in classical hysteresis theory. PAL is thus an efficient architecture for tasks with long episodic memory and weak positional dependence, with O(n log n) total inference cost versus O(n^2) for standard attention.

</details>


### [184] [Valid and Expressive Copulas for Irregular Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23632)
*Christian Klötergens,Tom Hanika,Lars Schmidt-Thieme,Vijaya Krishna Yalavarthi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CopFITi，一种用于不规则多变量时间序列（IMTS）概率预测的耦合模型。该模型结合了归一化流在单变量边缘分布中的表达能力与高斯混合耦合在联合依赖结构中的一致性和灵活性。实验表明，解耦边缘分布与联合分布的耦合方法在边缘建模上优于直接拟合全联合分布的架构。CopFITi是首个在构造上具有边缘一致性且在联合IMTS密度建模方面达到新基准的IMTS耦合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理不规则多变量时间序列时，难以同时保证边缘分布建模的准确性与联合依赖结构的一致性。直接建模全联合分布的架构往往在边缘分布上表现不佳，而传统耦合方法又缺乏边缘一致性。因此，亟需一种既能灵活建模边缘分布又能保持联合依赖结构一致性的新方法。

Method: CopFITi采用归一化流对每个单变量边缘分布进行建模，以捕捉复杂的边缘动态；同时利用高斯混合耦合（Gaussian Mixture Copula）来建模变量间的联合依赖结构，确保边缘一致性。通过解耦边缘与联合建模，实现高效且准确的概率预测。

Result: 实验结果显示，基于耦合的方法在边缘分布建模上显著优于端到端联合建模方法。CopFITi在多个基准数据集上实现了当前最优的联合密度建模性能，特别是在处理不规则采样和复杂依赖结构的数据时表现出更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: CopFITi是首个在构造上具备边缘一致性、并能有效建模不规则多变量时间序列联合分布的耦合模型，为该领域建立了新的基准，证明了解耦建模策略在概率预测中的优越性。

Abstract: We introduce CopFITi, a copula model for probabilistic forecasting of irregular multivariate time series (IMTS). Our model combines the expressivity of normalizing flows for univariate marginals with the consistency and flexibility of a Gaussian Mixture Copula for the joint dependency structure. Our experiments show that copula-based approaches, which decouple the marginals from the joint, yield better marginal models than architectures that directly fit the full joint. With CopFITi, we propose the first IMTS copula that is marginalization-consistent by construction and establish a new state of the art in joint IMTS density modeling.

### [185] [Optimal Dimension-Free Sampling for Regularized Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23726)
*Meysam Alishahi,Alexander Munteanu,Simon Omlor,Jeff M. Phillips*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明了在多种正则化项下，针对广义Lipschitz连续分类损失函数的最优采样边界，达到$(1\pm\varepsilon)$相对误差。涵盖逻辑回归、Sigmoid、铰链损失和ReLU损失等常见损失函数。对于$\|\cdot\|_2/k$正则化，采样复杂度为$k^2/\varepsilon^2$上下界；对于$\|\cdot\|_1/k$正则化，为$k/\varepsilon^2$上下界；对于$\|\cdot\|_2^2/k$正则化，若损失函数满足有界导数条件（如$|g'(x)|\leq g(x)$且$g(0)>0$），则采样复杂度线性于$k$；否则为$k^2/\varepsilon^2$。若$g(0)=0$，则无法获得无维度或次线性边界。所有上界均与下界匹配（仅差多对数因子）。方法基于简单的均匀或范数采样，优于近期$O(k^3/\varepsilon^2)$敏感度采样，通过高阶矩界和经验过程分析避免传统VC维与敏感度框架中的重复计数问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有采样方法在处理Lipschitz连续损失函数时存在采样复杂度过高的问题，尤其是依赖于敏感度采样的方法往往导致$O(k^3/\varepsilon^2)$的复杂度。本文旨在突破这一瓶颈，建立更优、紧致且理论上最优的采样边界，尤其针对广泛使用的分类损失函数，以提升大规模机器学习模型训练的效率。

Method: 提出基于统一或平方范数采样的新策略，结合高阶矩估计与经验过程分析技术，有效避免传统方法中因重复计数导致的复杂度膨胀。通过精细的数学推导，构建上界与下界之间的紧致匹配，实现理论最优性。

Result: 实现了多项损失函数在不同正则化下的最优采样复杂度：$k^2/\varepsilon^2$（$\|\cdot\|_2/k$）、$k/\varepsilon^2$（$\|\cdot\|_1/k$）、线性于$k$（特定条件下$\|\cdot\|_2^2/k$），并在$g(0)=0$时揭示无维度边界不可能性。所有结果均具备上下界匹配性（仅差polylog因子）。

Conclusion: 本研究显著改进了现有采样理论，提供了适用于主流分类损失函数的最优采样方案。其核心在于避免传统框架中的冗余计算，通过更精细的分析工具实现理论与实际性能的双重提升，为大规模机器学习优化提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We prove optimal sampling bounds achieving $(1\pm\varepsilon)$-relative error for a broad class of Lipschitz continuous classification loss functions under various regularization terms. This includes important functions such as logistic and sigmoid loss, hinge loss, and ReLU loss, as prominent and popular representative examples. In particular, we prove $k^2/\varepsilon^2$ upper and lower bounds for $\|\cdot\|_2/k$ regularization, and $k/\varepsilon^2$ upper and lower bounds for $\|\cdot\|_1/k$ regularization. For $\|\cdot\|_2^2/k$ regularization, the sampling complexity depends mainly on a bounded derivative property: if $|g'(x)|\leq g(x)$, and $g(0)>0$, and $g$ is monotonic or convex, then it admits linear in $k$ sampling complexity; otherwise the general bound is $k^2/\varepsilon^2$. However, if $g(0)=0$, our results indicate that no dimension-free bounds are possible, and even sublinear bounds are ruled out. All upper bounds are complemented by matching lower bounds up to polylogarithmic terms. Moreover, our work relies conceptually and algorithmically on simple uniform or (squared) norm sampling and hereby improves over recent cubic $k^3/\varepsilon^2$ sensitivity sampling bounds of (Alishahi and Phillips, ICML'24). This is achieved by refined arguments involving higher moment bounds and empirical process analyses to avoid overcounting that appears in the de-facto standard VC-dimension and sensitivity framework.

### [186] [It's the humans, not the data: Geopolitical bias in LLMs originates in post-training, amplified by the language of the prompt](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23825)
*Stuart Bladon,Brinnae Bent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现，语言模型中的地缘政治偏见主要源于后训练阶段而非预训练阶段。通过对七个开源大模型对在英语、法语和中文下的28个国家配对测试，发现大多数模型在后训练后出现与开发者所在国家相关的偏见，尤其以阿里Qwen 2.5最为显著，其对中国的偏好从预训练的中性（-0.15）变为后训练的强烈偏好（+2.91），偏见强度提升18倍。此外，偏见方向还受提示语言影响，如法国开发的Mistral仅在法语提示下表现出亲法倾向。研究强调，地缘政治偏见是后训练过程中主动塑造的结果，需加强对对齐过程的透明度、审计与监管。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为语言模型的地缘政治偏见来自预训练数据，但本研究旨在检验这一假设，探究偏见是否在后训练阶段形成，从而揭示模型对国家、文化及政治观点呈现背后的机制。

Method: 采用成对情景强制选择探针，测试七组开源大模型（基线模型与聊天模型）在英语、法语、中文三种语言下对28个国别组合的偏好，比较预训练与后训练阶段的偏见变化，并分析提示语言对偏见的影响。

Result: 六种模型在后训练后出现与开发者国籍相关的偏见，其中阿里Qwen 2.5对中国的偏好显著上升，偏见幅度达18倍；法国开发的Mistral仅在法语提示下表现出亲法倾向，表明偏见受提示语言调节。

Conclusion: 地缘政治偏见并非简单继承自互联网数据，而是由后训练过程主动塑造。这凸显了对模型对齐机制进行透明化、审计与监督的必要性，以确保模型对国家与文化的表征更加公正客观。

Abstract: It has generally been assumed that geopolitical bias in language models originates from the training data used during the pre-training phase. We tested seven open-weight LLM pairs consisting of the base model (pre-training only) and the chat model (pre-training and post-training) from seven labs on a paired-scenario forced-choice probe over 28 country pairs in English, French, and Chinese, and found that geopolitical bias originates in post-training rather than in pre-training. Across seven AI labs, six showed shifts in the direction associated with the country or region of the model developer after post-training. This shift is strongest in Alibaba's Qwen 2.5: while the base is neutral on China-favourability (-0.15 log-odds, p=0.15), the post-trained chat variant is at +2.91 (p<10^-4), an 18x shift in odds. We also observe shifts in biases toward other countries across all models. Additionally, the magnitude of this shift depends on the language used to prompt the model: the French-made Mistral becomes pro-France only under French prompting (FR-EN shift +1.91, p<10^-4). These findings suggest that geopolitical preferences in language models are not simply inherited from large-scale internet data but are actively shaped during post-training, highlighting the need for greater transparency, auditing, and oversight of alignment processes that influence how models represent nations, cultures, and political perspectives.

</details>


### [187] [Approaching I/O-optimality for Approximate Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23751)
*Pál András Papp,Aleksandros Sobczyk,Anastasios Zouzias*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文重新研究了大型语言模型中注意力机制的输入/输出（I/O）复杂度。针对查询、键、值矩阵 $Q, K, V \in \mathbb{R}^{n\times d}$，在快速内存大小为 $M$ 的机器上，目标是通过最小化快慢内存间的数据传输次数来计算注意力矩阵 $A = \text{softmax}(QK^\top / \sqrt{d})V$。现有方法如 FlashAttention 及其变体的 I/O 成本随 $n$ 二次增长，而一个平凡下界仅需 $\Omega(nd)$ 的 I/O 来读取输入和写入输出。本文提出一种新方法，使 I/O 成本在大多数参数设置下几乎线性依赖于 $n$，该方法基于 Alman 和 Song 的近似注意力框架设计了高效的 I/O 算法，并在每个参数范围内证明了相应的下界，表明所提算法接近 I/O 最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有注意力计算方法（如 FlashAttention）的 I/O 复杂度随序列长度 $n$ 二次增长，远高于理论下界 $\Omega(nd)$，限制了大规模模型的高效执行。因此需要设计更高效的 I/O 优化算法以逼近理论最优性能。

Method: 受 Alman 和 Song 近似注意力框架启发，提出一种新的 I/O 高效算法，通过分块处理、近似计算与内存访问优化，将注意力计算的 I/O 成本降低至几乎线性依赖于 $n$ 的水平。同时在不同参数区域构建理论下界，验证算法的近似最优性。

Result: 所提出的算法在多数参数配置下实现了几乎线性的 I/O 复杂度，显著优于现有方法（如 FlashAttention），且理论下界证明其接近最优，具有实际部署潜力。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入基于近似注意力的 I/O 优化技术，成功将注意力计算的 I/O 复杂度从二次降低至几乎线性，且在理论和实践上均表现出优越性，为大规模语言模型的高效推理提供了新思路。

Abstract: We revisit the I/O complexity of attention in large language models. Given query-key-value matrices $Q,K,V\in\mathbb{R}^{n\times d}$, and a machine with fast memory size $M$, the goal is to compute the "attention matrix" $A=\text{softmax}(Q K ^{\top}/\sqrt{d}) V$ with the minimal number of data transfers between fast and slow memory. Existing methods in the literature, most notably FlashAttention and its variants, incur an I/O cost that depends quadratically on $n$, while a trivial lower bound only requires $Ω(nd)$ I/O's to read the inputs and write the output. In this work, we present a technique for computing attention where the I/O cost only depends almost-linearly on $n$ in most parameter regimes. This is achieved by developing I/O-efficient algorithms inspired by the recent approximate attention framework of Alman and Song. We also prove corresponding lower bounds in each parameter regime to show that our algorithms are indeed close to I/O-optimal.

</details>


### [188] [LLM-driven design of physics-constrained constitutive models: two agents are better than one](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23754)
*Marius Tacke,Matthias Busch,Kian Abdolazizi,Jonas Eichinger,Kevin Linka,Roland Aydin,Christian Cyron*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种多智能体大语言模型驱动的本构模型生成方法，通过创建者（Creator）生成模型并由检查者（Inspector）基于九条物理约束进行审核，显著提升模型的物理合法性。在脑组织、实验橡胶和合成橡胶数据上测试，使符合物理约束的模型比例从91%提升至100%（Opus），37%提升至56%（Kimi），同时保持高精度和良好泛化能力，实现可直接应用的物理合规、高精度、可外推的本构模型。该方法分离生成与验证，使LLM驱动建模更可信，且具备技术无关性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统本构模型开发需多年专业知识，虽大语言模型（LLM）降低了门槛，但现有单智能体方法缺乏对物理定律的系统性检验，导致生成模型可能违反基本物理规律，限制其实际应用。因此需要一种能确保模型物理合法性的自动化生成框架。

Method: 引入多智能体架构：创建者（Creator）根据数据生成候选本构模型（如CANNs），检查者（Inspector）独立评估模型是否满足九项物理约束（如能量单调性、应力-应变一致性等），若违反则返回修正。该过程迭代直至模型完全合规。使用Claude Opus 4.7和Kimi K2.5两种LLM作为基础模型进行验证。

Result: 添加检查者后，符合所有物理约束的模型比例显著提升：Opus从91%升至100%，Kimi从37%升至56%；模型保持接近基线的准确性，并展现出对未见载荷路径的良好泛化能力；生成模型兼具物理合法性、高精度与可靠外推性，可直接用于工程实践。

Conclusion: 通过将模型生成与物理合规性检查分离，多智能体LLM框架实现了可信的本构模型自动生成。该方法不依赖特定技术，随LLM能力提升而自动扩展，为自动化、物理感知的模型发现提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Developing constitutive models that capture how materials deform under load traditionally requires years of specialized expertise in continuum mechanics, machine learning, and scientific programming. Large language models (LLMs) have recently been shown to lower this barrier by generating constitutive models on demand, but existing single-agent pipelines lack systematic checks that the resulting models respect fundamental physical laws. To close this gap, we introduce the first multi-agent LLM-driven approach for constitutive model generation: a Creator agent proposes a model tailored to the data, while an Inspector agent critically audits each proposal against nine physical constraints and returns it for refinement whenever a violation is detected. We demonstrate this concept with constitutive artificial neural networks (CANNs) and benchmark it on brain tissue, experimental rubber, and synthetic rubber, using two different LLM backbones (Claude Opus 4.7 and Kimi K2.5). Adding the Inspector raises the share of exported models that truly satisfy all physical constraints from 91% to a perfect 100% for Opus and from 37% to 56% for Kimi, while preserving near-baseline accuracy and remarkable generalization to unseen loading paths. In combination, the generated models are physically valid, highly accurate, and extrapolate reliably beyond the training data - properties that together make them directly usable in practice. Separating generation from inspection thus turns LLM-driven constitutive modeling into a genuinely trustworthy process. The paradigm is deliberately technique-agnostic and scales automatically with advances in LLM capability, opening a promising path toward automated, physics-aware model discovery.

</details>


### [189] [LLMs as Noisy Channels: A Shannon Perspective on Model Capacity and Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23901)
*Xu Ouyang,Deyi Liu,Yuhang Cai,Jing Liu,Yuan Yang,Chen Zheng,Thomas Hartvigsen,Yiyuan Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于香农-哈特利定理的统一理论框架——香农缩放定律（Shannon Scaling Law），将大语言模型（LLM）训练建模为在噪声信道中的信息传输过程，通过将模型参数映射为信道带宽、训练数据量映射为信号功率，揭示了学习信号与内在噪声之间的相互作用。该框架定义了LLM的固有香农容量：若不保持足够的信噪比（SNR），单纯扩大模型规模或数据量反而会放大噪声，导致性能从单调提升转为U形下降。实验在Pythia和OLMo2上验证了该理论，涵盖高斯噪声、量化、数学/问答/代码微调等多种扰动场景，结果表明香农缩放定律显著优于经典及近期扰动感知缩放定律，具有高拟合优度（$R^2$），并能准确预测未见模型（如12B模型达307B token）的表现，而单调基线则失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主流缩放定律多为单调幂律，无法解释灾难性过训练、量化引起的性能退化等非单调现象。当模型或数据规模增加但信噪比未维持时，噪声被放大，导致性能恶化，亟需一种能统一描述此类复杂行为的理论框架。

Method: 基于香农-哈特利定理，将模型参数视为信道带宽，训练数据量视为信号功率，构建信息传输模型。通过引入信噪比（SNR）作为核心变量，推导出模型性能随计算资源变化的非单调关系，建立香农容量约束下的缩放规律。

Result: 在多种扰动（噪声、量化、微调任务）下，香农缩放定律在Pythia和OLMo2数据集上均表现出优异拟合能力，$R^2$得分显著高于传统方法；其外推能力突出，仅用≤6.9B模型和≤180B token数据即可准确预测12B模型在307B token下的表现，而单调基线完全崩溃。

Conclusion: 香农缩放定律提供了一个统一且可外推的理论框架，能够有效解释并预测大语言模型在噪声环境下的非单调性能变化，揭示了信噪比在模型缩放中的核心作用，为未来高效、稳定的大模型训练提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Existing scaling laws for Large Language Models (LLMs), predominantly monotonic power laws, fail to explain emerging non-monotonic phenomena such as catastrophic overtraining and quantization-induced degradation, where performance deteriorates despite increased compute.
  We propose the Shannon Scaling Law, a unified theoretical framework that models LLM training as information transmission over a noisy channel, grounded in the Shannon-Hartley theorem. By mapping model parameters to channel bandwidth and training tokens to signal power, our formulation explicitly captures the interaction between learning signal and intrinsic noise. This perspective reveals a fundamental Shannon capacity for LLMs: scaling model size or data without preserving a sufficient signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) inevitably amplifies noise, inducing a transition from monotonic improvement to U-shaped performance degradation.
  We validate our theory through experiments on Pythia and OLMo2 under perturbations, including Gaussian noise, quantization and supervised fine-tuning on math, QA and code tasks. The Shannon Scaling Law consistently outperforms classical scaling laws and recent perturbation-aware laws, achieving strong $R^2$ scores and accurately capturing loss basins missed by prior approaches. It also extrapolates: fitted on $\leq$6.9B Pythia models with $\leq$180B tokens, it predicts the unseen 12B model up to 307B tokens at pooled $R^2{=}0.847$, while monotonic baselines collapse.

</details>


### [190] [Training-Free Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23872)
*Lizhang Chen,Jonathan Li,Chen Liang,Ni Lao,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需训练的循环变压器方法，在推理时通过轻量级包装器对冻结检查点的中间层块进行循环，无需微调或架构修改。该方法将循环视为对预归一化变压器块作为ODE前向欧拉步长的改进，用更小的阻尼子步骤替代单一的大更新，从而提升性能。在多个密集、稀疏MoE和MLA+MoE模型族中，显著提升了多项任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环变压器方法需端到端训练，而本文旨在在不改变模型结构的前提下，于推理阶段实现对预训练模型的递归改造，以提升性能。

Method: 将预归一化变压器块视为前向欧拉步长，将循环视为对同一近似的精炼过程，用多个小的阻尼子步骤替代单一大步更新，从而避免性能下降。

Result: 在七个不同模型家族中，分别在MMLU-Pro、CommonsenseQA、OpenBookQA等任务上实现了2.64、1.14、1.20个百分点的性能提升。

Conclusion: 该方法成功实现了无需训练的模型性能增强，验证了推理时循环策略对预训练模型的有效性与通用性。

Abstract: We introduce training-free looped transformers, in which a lightweight inference-time wrapper loops a contiguous mid-stack block of layers of a frozen checkpoint without additional fine-tuning, continued training, or architectural changes. Unlike prior looped transformer methods that train with the looped structure end-to-end, we retrofit recurrence onto pretrained models at test time. We show that naive block reapplication usually degrades performance, highlighting the importance of the loop application strategy. Motivated by viewing a pre-norm transformer block as a forward Euler step on an ODE, we instead treat looping as a refinement of the same approximation, replacing one large update with smaller damped sub-steps. Across seven dense, sparse MoE, and MLA+MoE model families, our method improves Qwen3-4B-Instruct by +2.64 pp on MMLU-Pro, Qwen3-30B-A3B-Instruct by +1.14 pp on CommonsenseQA, and Moonlight-16B-A3B-Instruct by +1.20 pp on OpenBookQA.

</details>

### [191] [RMA: an Agentic System for Research-Level Mathematical Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22875)
*Zelin Zhao,Bo Yuan,Jaemoo Choi,Yongxin Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RMA 是一个用于解决研究级数学问题的智能体框架，通过模块化设计和多轮迭代推理，在复杂问题分析、文献检索、知识构建和证明验证等方面实现协同工作。该框架在 First Proof 基准测试中表现优异，成功解决 8/10 个专家提出的难题，优于 GPT-5.2R 和 Aletheia 等基线模型。性能提升源于结构化推理模块、迭代优化与验证反馈的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多聚焦于竞赛数学或形式化定理证明，难以应对研究级数学问题所需的长时序推理、文献依赖性和反复修正能力。因此需要一种能模拟人类数学研究过程的自动化框架。

Method: RMA 将研究级证明求解分解为问题分析、文献搜索与理解、公平比较、知识库构建和证明验证等模块，由初始化器、提议者和验证者智能体协同运作，通过共享结构化记忆实现多角色、多轮次协作，不断生成、优化并验证候选证明。

Result: 在 First Proof 基准测试中，RMA 成功解决 8 道研究级问题，生成的证明逻辑更严谨、可读性更强，显著优于 GPT-5.2R、Aletheia 等强基线模型。消融实验表明性能提升来自模块协同、迭代优化与验证反馈的综合作用。

Conclusion: RMA 展现了在研究级数学问题求解上的强大潜力，其模块化协同机制和迭代验证流程为未来自动化数学研究提供了可行路径。相关代码与解决方案将在论文接受后公开。

Abstract: We present $\textbf{Research Math Agents (RMA)}$, an agentic framework for automated reasoning on research-level mathematical problems. Unlike prior studies centered on competition mathematics or formal theorem proving, RMA targets research-level mathematical problems that require long-horizon reasoning, literature grounding, and iterative proof refinement. RMA decomposes research-level proof solving into specialized modules for problem analysis, literature search and understanding, fair comparison, knowledge-bank construction, and proof verification, all coordinated by initializer, proposer, and verifier agents through a shared structured memory. Within this unified framework, these agents operate in a multi-role, multi-round workflow, collaboratively generating, refining, and verifying candidate proofs through iterative feedback. We evaluate RMA on the First Proof benchmark, which consists of ten research-level problems contributed by expert mathematicians across diverse domains. Through comprehensive expert evaluation, RMA outperforms strong baselines on the First Proof benchmark, including GPT-5.2R and Aletheia, solving eight out of ten research problems and producing more logically sound and readable proofs. Our comprehensive ablation studies further show that performance gains arise from the interaction of structured reasoning modules, iterative refinement, and verifier-based feedback, rather than any single component. Our solutions and implementations will be made publicly available upon acceptance.

</details>


### [192] [Energy per Successful Goal: Goal-Level Energy Accounting for Agentic AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22883)
*Deepak Panigrahy,Aakash Tyagi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 当前AI能效基准以单次模型调用或训练行为为单位衡量能耗，但在多步骤的智能体系统中，调用次数仅为实现机制的副产品，而非任务本身的属性。为此，本文提出A-LEMS（Agentic LLM Energy Measurement System），重新定义能效计量单位为‘每成功目标能耗’（EpG），整合所有执行尝试（含失败与重试）的总能量，并按成功完成的目标数归一化。该框架通过时间边界模型、五层观测管道及可复现协议，将RAPL信号映射至工作流级能耗。基于EpG，进一步提出‘编排开销指数’（OOI），量化编排结构相对于线性执行的额外能耗。实验表明，在五类推理与三类工具增强任务中，智能体工作流的平均EpG为888.1J，是线性基线（205.3J）的4.33倍；但对工具增强任务，当OOI低于1.0时，智能体反而更节能，证明该指标反映的是编排结构影响，而非固定偏移。结论：传统‘每推理能耗’已不适用于智能体系统，EpG与OOI为准确评估提供基础，编排结构才是能耗主导因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统AI能效基准以单次推理或训练为单位，适用于经典单轮任务，但无法准确反映智能体系统中多步编排、工具调用、重试和故障恢复等复杂行为的真实能耗。因调用次数是实现细节而非任务属性，导致基于推理级别的能效归一化存在偏差。亟需新的度量框架来真实刻画目标达成的总能耗。

Method: 提出A-LEMS框架，包含：1）时间边界模型，用于界定任务生命周期；2）五层观测管道，从硬件层（RAPL）到应用层逐层采集并映射能耗数据；3）可复现协议，确保测量结果与具体硬件和运行环境绑定。通过EpG（Energy per Successful Goal）聚合所有尝试的能耗，再引入OOI（Orchestration Overhead Index）分离编排开销。

Result: 在五类推理和三类工具增强任务上，智能体工作流的平均能量消耗为888.1 J/成功目标，是线性基线（205.3 J）的4.33倍；但工具增强任务中OOI可低于1.0，说明智能体在特定场景下更节能。结果验证了EpG和OOI能够有效区分编排结构带来的能耗差异，而非单纯计算开销。

Conclusion: ‘每推理能耗’已不足以衡量智能体系统的实际能效。EpG和OOI提供了更准确的度量基础，揭示了编排结构是决定能耗的关键因素，推动了面向智能体系统的能效评估范式转型。

Abstract: Current AI energy benchmarks measure consumption at the granularity of a single model invocation or training run. For classical single-turn workloads this unit remains coherent. For agentic systems - where a single user goal may trigger multi-step orchestration, tool calls, retries, and failure-recovery cycles - the invocation count is an implementation artifact rather than a task property, and inference-level normalization misrepresents the energy cost of goal completion. We present A-LEMS (Agentic LLM Energy Measurement System), a cross-layer measurement framework that redefines the unit of AI energy accounting from energy per inference to Energy per Successful Goal (EpG). EpG aggregates total workflow energy across all execution attempts, including failures and retries, normalized by successfully completed goals. A-LEMS formalizes energy attribution through a temporal boundary model, a five-layer observation pipeline mapping RAPL signals to workflow-level energy, and a reproducibility protocol binding every measurement to hardware and runtime configuration. Building on EpG, we define the Orchestration Overhead Index (OOI), isolating the energy cost of orchestration relative to linear execution under identical task criteria.
  Across five reasoning and three tool-augmented task families, agentic workflows consume 4.33x higher mean energy per successful goal than linear baselines (888.1 J vs 205.3 J). This overhead is driven by orchestration structure, not inference compute. For tool-augmented tasks, OOI inverts below 1.0x: agentic execution is cheaper than linear, confirming the metric captures orchestration structure rather than a fixed upward bias.
  These findings establish that energy-per-inference is insufficient for agentic AI. EpG and OOI provide the measurement foundation for accurate benchmarking, where orchestration structure is the primary determinant of energy cost.

</details>


### [193] [ImProver 2: Iteratively Self-Improving LMs for Neurosymbolic Proof Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22885)
*Riyaz Ahuja,Tate Rowney,Jeremy Avigad,Sean Welleck*

TL;DR: ImProver 2 is a neurosymbolic framework for automated proof optimization in Lean 4, combining a data-efficient expert-iteration pipeline with a scaffold that captures formal structure and informal abstractions. The scaffold improves performance across both small and large models, enabling small models to restructure complex research-level proofs effectively.

Abstract: Formal mathematics libraries are rapidly expanding, creating a growing need to refactor verified proofs for maintainability and to improve training data quality for neural provers. However, scalable proof optimization is hindered by heterogeneous and heuristically specified objectives, scarce data, and high training and inference costs. To overcome these challenges, we introduce ImProver 2, a neurosymbolic framework for automated proof optimization in Lean 4. ImProver 2 combines a data-efficient expert-iteration pipeline with a scaffold that exposes formal structure alongside lightweight informal abstractions. We further introduce a suite of metrics capturing structural proof properties. Using ImProver 2, we train a 7B-parameter model that outperforms orders-of-magnitude larger models within the same model family, and is competitive with mid-tier frontier models across metrics. We additionally demonstrate that our neurosymbolic scaffold significantly improves performance across both small and frontier models. We show that with proper scaffolding and training, small models can effectively restructure research-level proofs over complex and varied metrics, matching substantially larger systems and establishing proof optimization as a scalable, learnable task.

Result: 提出了一个统一的媒介模糊逻辑体系，支持从类型1到量子扩展的多层级推理；在实际案例中展示了其在不完整、异构、轻微矛盾信息下的透明、安全决策能力；高层模型在合理条件下可还原为类型1，保证一致性。

Conclusion: 媒介模糊逻辑的统一框架为复杂决策系统提供了坚实且可扩展的理论基础，支持安全、可靠、可解释的智能决策，适用于未来多层次模糊推理系统的发展。

Abstract: Mediative Fuzzy Logic was conceived as a practical scheme for reconciling hesitant or conflicting assessments in fuzzy control and decision-making. However, its logical and semantic foundations remain underdeveloped, especially beyond operational type-1 settings. This article develops a unified account of the type-1 core together with interval type-2, granular type-3, and quantum extensions. We characterize the mediative operator as a convex aggregation controlled by hesitation and contradiction, model mediative truth values as independent truth-falsity pairs in a continuous bilattice-like structure, and introduce a propositional system extending a standard t-norm-based fuzzy logic with a mediative connective. We establish soundness, paraconsistency, and conservativity over the underlying fuzzy base for formulas without mediation, and formulate coherent semantic extensions to interval type-2 truth values, granule-indexed local evaluations, and effects and density operators on Hilbert spaces. Under suitable assumptions, the higher-level formulations reduce to the type-1 case, clarifying coherence across levels and reliably supporting future work in intelligent decision systems.

### [195] [The Deterministic Horizon: Impossibility Results as Design Specifications for Trustworthy AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23024)
*Dongxin Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文将图灵、阿罗等不可行性结果转化为设计准则，提出由架构决定的精度上限（确定性地平线），指出超过特定推理深度后，无论训练数据量、适配器秩或损失函数如何调整，模型性能无法提升。这一边界可通过层数和嵌入维度预先计算，且在12种Transformer架构中表现为19至31之间的数值范围。通过残差流容量不变性与信息论转换，揭示了超出地平线后的超指数精度衰减机制。此外，论文还推导出模指数运算在常数深度素数模电路下的无条件电路复杂度下界，并将该方法拓展至偏好学习、多阶段检索、拍卖机制及零知识验证等多个领域，形成包含16个规范的设计框架，每个均包含可计算的边界、量化违反代价和可构造的设计规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型已广泛应用于软件编写、法律文书起草和临床记录生成，但其能力受限于从图灵到阿罗再到无免费午餐定理等根本性理论限制。这些不可行性结果虽被视作学术奇观，却未被充分转化为实际系统设计的指导原则。本文旨在将此类理论极限转化为可操作的设计规则，以应对可信AI中的核心挑战。

Method: 通过分析变压器架构的残差流容量不变性，建立基于层深与嵌入宽度的精度上限模型；利用信息论工具推导超指数精度衰减规律；结合电路复杂度理论，对模指数运算构建无条件下界；并采用统一的‘不可能性-规范’方法论，将该框架推广至多个子领域，建立可计算边界与设计规则之间的映射关系。

Result: 发现所有考察的12种变压器架构均存在确定性地平线，其值介于19至31之间；精细调优最优长度轨迹仅能恢复不足4个百分点的性能；在多个子领域中成功识别出可计算的性能边界与量化违反代价；构建了16项具体的设计规范，其中两个组合已被证明，一项为诚实障碍，四项仍开放。

Conclusion: 所有人工智能的根本性限制同时也是设计规则。该研究提出了一个面向可信人工智能的生成性研究范式——将理论不可行性转化为系统设计的主动约束，从而实现更可靠、可预测和可验证的人工智能系统。

Abstract: Large language models now write software, draft legal documents, and produce clinical notes, yet fundamental limits, from Turing and Arrow to the No Free Lunch theorems, shape what computation can do. This thesis turns such impossibility results from curiosities into design rules. Its flagship result proves an accuracy ceiling set by architecture alone: past a critical reasoning depth, no amount of training moves it, at any adapter rank, sample size, or loss function. Computable before deployment from layer count and embedding width, this Deterministic Horizon is measured between nineteen and thirty-one across twelve transformer architectures, and fine-tuning on optimal-length traces recovers under four percentage points. The mechanism is a capacity invariant of the residual stream, and an information-theoretic conversion yields super-exponential accuracy decay past the horizon. An unconditional circuit-complexity lower bound for modular exponentiation against constant-depth prime-modulus circuits complements this result. The same argument recasts across subfields: preference learning under any misspecified model jumps discontinuously in sample complexity; multi-stage retrieval pipelines require at least as many independent metrics as stages; standard truthful auctions fail for agents with prompt-dependent valuations; and zero-knowledge verification of neural inference pays a measured overhead of one hundred ten to one hundred ninety times per non-linear activation. Together these form a catalogue of sixteen specifications, each pairing a computable boundary, a quantified violation cost, and a constructive design rule: two compositions are proved, one pairing is an honest obstruction, and four remain open. The impossibility-specification methodology is offered for the generative research programme that trustworthy AI may need. Every fundamental limit of AI is also a design rule.

### [196] [PathCal: State-Aware Reflection-Marker Calibration for Efficient Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23074)
*Lingyu Jiang,Zirui Li,Shuo Xing,Peiran Li,Tsubasa Takahashi,Dengzhe Hou,Zhengzhong Tu,Kazunori Yamada,Fangzhou Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型推理语言模型（LRMs）在测试时通过生成长链思维（CoT）轨迹进行复杂推理时，显式反思标记（如"wait"、"but"、"alternatively"）的功能差异。通过类型化抑制和固定前缀干预实验，发现不同标记在功能和影响时机上存在显著区别，尤其在模型尚未稳定推理路径前作用最为关键。基于此，提出无需训练的解码控制器PathCal，通过区分标记类型，并在局部不确定状态下进行干预，利用反思标记分布估计当前路径与竞争分支之间的局部竞争，动态调整标记逻辑以软性平衡选择。在六个推理基准上的实验表明，PathCal在不依赖外部验证器或额外采样的情况下，实现了更好的性能-效率权衡，既保持或提升准确率，又减少生成长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将反思标记视为单一粗粒度类别，忽视其在功能和时机上的差异，导致无法有效控制推理过程。本文旨在揭示不同反思标记的实际作用机制，并设计更精细的解码策略以提升推理效率与准确性。

Method: 采用类型化抑制与固定前缀干预分析反思标记的功能差异；提出PathCal解码控制器，基于反思标记分布估计局部竞争，仅在局部不确定性高时软性调整标记逻辑，实现对推理路径的精准校准。

Result: PathCal在六种推理基准上均表现出色，相比基线方法，在保持或提高准确率的同时显著缩短生成长度，且无需外部验证器或额外采样，证明了其高效性与普适性。

Conclusion: 反思标记具有多样化的功能角色和最佳干预时机，区分其类型并结合局部不确定性检测进行动态干预，是提升推理效率与准确性的有效途径。PathCal作为无训练解码控制器，为复杂推理任务提供了轻量、高效的优化方案。

Abstract: The emergence of Large Reasoning Language Models (LRMs) has paved the way for tackling complex reasoning tasks through test-time scaling by generating long-form Chain-of-Thought (CoT) trajectories during inference. Meanwhile, these trajectories often contain explicit reflection markers such as ``wait'', ``but'', and ``alternatively'', signaling hesitation, revision, and the consideration of alternative explorations, respectively. Recent studies on test-time control leverage such markers as lightweight handles for steering reasoning, typically treating them as a single coarse-grained category rather than distinguishing their distinct functional roles. In this paper, we conduct type-wise suppression and fixed-prefix intervention, revealing that reflection markers differ not only in their functional roles but also in when they exert the greatest influence. Specifically, different marker classes affect accuracy and generation length in distinct ways, and marker choices are most consequential before the model settles into a stable reasoning trajectory. Motivated by these findings, we introduce PathCal, a novel training-free decoding controller that calibrates reasoning paths by distinguishing marker types and intervening only at locally uncertain states. At each decoding step, PathCal utilizes the distribution over reflection-markers to estimate local competition between maintaining the current reasoning trajectory and initiating a competing branch, and softly rebalances marker logits when competing-branch evidence becomes excessive. Experiments across six reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PathCal achieves a better efficiency--performance trade-off, improving or preserving accuracy while reducing generation length, without relying on external verifiers or additional sampling.

### [197] [AutoResearch AI: Towards AI-Powered Research Automation for Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23204)

Abstract: Scientific research is being reshaped by AI systems that move beyond isolated assistance toward longer-horizon workflows spanning literature grounding, hypothesis generation, experimentation, validation, reporting, and revision. Yet current systems remain fragmented, differing in autonomy, domain scope, execution environment, validation mechanism, and human oversight, while still struggling with evidence preservation, reproducibility, weak-direction rejection, provenance tracking, cross-domain robustness, and accountable scientific closure. This survey examines these developments through AutoResearch, defined as the developmental spectrum of AI-powered scientific workflow automation. Within it, Vibe Research denotes the human-steered region of prompt-based assistance and human-verified execution, whereas emerging AI-led systems coordinate larger portions of the discovery loop without achieving robust autonomy. We analyze how research systems redistribute control, evidence, execution, validation, and accountability across workflows and organize the field around five workflow conditions: literature and research grounding; hypothesis formation and planning; experimentation and tool use; feedback, validation, and review; and reporting and knowledge communication. We further synthesize AI scientist systems, mixed-initiative co-research frameworks, benchmarks, domain deployments, and open-source infrastructures. Finally, we propose five evaluation dimensions--novelty, validity, impact, reliability, and provenance--and show that AutoResearch autonomy is domain-conditioned, being more credible in structured, executable, and rapidly verifiable settings but limited in embodied, delayed, heterogeneous, ethical, or institutionally accountable contexts.

### [198] [GENSTRAT: Toward a Science of Strategic Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23238)
*Vartan Shadarevian,Kia Ghods,Alex Kenich,Anany Kotawala*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出GENSTRAT，一种基于程序生成策略环境的评估框架，用于更真实地评估大语言模型（LLM）在复杂、多变的博弈场景中的表现。通过生成大量两人零和不完全信息扑克游戏，实现持续更新与抗污染评估，并引入六维能力剖面（状态空间、时间深度、信息敏感性、对手建模、风险偏好、鲁棒性）和‘锯齿度’指标来检测模型在相似游戏间的性能波动。在超过36,000场对战中测试9个前沿及开源LLM，发现尽管新模型整体表现更强，但同水平模型间能力特征差异显著，且顶级模型（如gpt-5和claude）表现出更高的局部不稳定性，而gemini-3.1-pro则更稳定。该框架超越单一排名，提供部署相关的诊断视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有战略推理基准局限于固定经典博弈，难以反映真实部署中多样化、动态化的策略环境，且易因模型过拟合而失效。需要一种可扩展、可泛化、能揭示模型深层行为特性的评估方法。

Method: 构建一个程序生成的两玩家零和不完全信息扑克游戏分布；采用六维能力剖面分解模型性能；引入‘锯齿度’衡量模型在相似游戏间的性能波动程度；从2000个生成游戏中采样50个作为基准，进行大规模双人对战测试。

Result: 新版本大模型平均表现更好；同一强度水平下模型的能力特征差异明显；顶级模型虽整体得分相近，但存在显著的局部波动性差异，其中gpt-5和claude比gemini-3.1-pro更具不稳定性。锯齿度指标有效识别出这种非平稳行为。

Conclusion: GENSTRAT提供了一种可持续、抗污染、具备部署相关洞察力的评估范式，其能力剖面与锯齿度测量共同揭示了模型在真实战略环境中的可靠性和适应性，优于传统排行榜。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as economic agents in marketplaces, auctions, and bidding settings. Anticipating their behavior in any specific deployment is hard. Existing strategic-reasoning benchmarks evaluate models on fixed canonical games. These benchmarks may saturate as the frontier improves, and they do not allow evaluators to generalize with confidence from benchmark performance to the varied and messy strategic environments that actual deployments involve. We introduce GENSTRAT, which uses procedurally generated strategic environments to address these challenges. Concretely, we generate a distribution of two-player zero-sum imperfect-information card games. The generator can draw fresh games on demand, allowing for evergreen evaluation and resistance to contamination. We pair the game distribution with a capability-profile methodology that decomposes model competence across six axes (state space, temporal depth, information sensitivity, opponent modeling, risk, and brittleness). We also introduce a jaggedness measure of within-distribution smoothness that detects when a model's advantage jumps unpredictably between strategically similar games. We sample 50 benchmark games from a 2,000-game generated pool and evaluate nine frontier and open-weight LLMs in a head-to-head tournament with over 36,000 matches. Newer frontier-tier models score higher on average. Beyond that average, models with near-identical overall strength show qualitatively different capability profiles, and two of the top three leaderboard models (gpt-5 and claude) are noticeably more locally volatile than the third (gemini-3.1-pro), despite being close in overall strength. Together, the capability profile and the jaggedness measure give a deployment-relevant diagnostic that the overall ranking alone cannot provide.

### [199] [Design and Report Benchmarks for Knowledge Work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23262)
*Yining Hua,Hongbin Na,Cyrus Ayubcha,Levi Lian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种三步法，以明确基准测试任务如何反映其得分所关联的工作主张：定义评估的工作活动、指定测试场景、并评分适当的工作成果。通过回顾知识工作组织中的角色职责、本地材料与工具、以及可延续使用的工作成果，将这些要素转化为基准设计与报告指南，强调任务应映射到具体工作活动，测试场景需明确材料、工具、角色和约束条件，评分应聚焦系统留下的工作产品。基于O*NET职业任务数据库，构建了18项工作活动清单，用于命名评估的工作活动并区别于常规基准任务。通过三个案例分析（GDPval、OfficeQA Pro、APEX-SWE）展示了基准设计选择如何影响最强工作主张的支撑能力，并揭示了任务、场景、产品与更广泛工作主张之间的差距。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前知识工作AI评估与基准设计仍沿用传统NLP任务逻辑，导致高分未必代表系统在真实部署环境中具备实际知识工作能力，亟需更贴近真实工作流程的评估方法。

Method: 提出三步框架：1）定义工作活动；2）规范测试设置（包括材料、工具、角色、约束）；3）聚焦工作产品进行评分。结合知识工作研究，构建18项工作活动分类体系，并应用于三个典型基准案例分析。

Abstract: The development of LLM agents has led to a growing body of work on knowledge-work AI, including coding, research, and healthcare. However, current knowledge-work evaluation and benchmark design still largely follow the logic of traditional NLP tasks. As a result, higher benchmark performance does not reliably show that a system can carry out knowledge work in real-world deployment settings. This paper contributes a three-step approach for making explicit how benchmarked tasks represent the work claims attached to their scores: defining the work activity under evaluation, specifying the tested setting, and scoring the appropriate work product. We review work studies showing that knowledge work is organized through roles and responsibilities, local materials and tools, and artifacts that must remain usable in downstream workflows. We then translate these concerns into benchmark design and reporting guidance, covering how tasks should be mapped to work activities, how tested settings should specify materials, tools, roles, and constraints, and how scoring should focus on the work product left by the system. To name the work activity being evaluated and distinguish it from common benchmark tasks, we derive an inventory of 18 work activities from the O{*}NET occupational task database. We demonstrate the approach through three benchmark case analyses: GDPval, a non-code occupational deliverable benchmark; OfficeQA Pro, a grounded document-analysis benchmark scored by final answers; and APEX-SWE, a software-engineering benchmark with executable scored products. These cases show how benchmark design choices shape the strongest work claim a score can support, and where gaps arise between the benchmarked task, tested setting, scored product, and broader work claim.

### [200] [Ontological Knowledge Blocks: Executable Compliance and Profile-Based Validation for Trustworthy AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23297)

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在AI辅助高性能计算资源分配场景中，24次验证运行显示：系统支持配置敏感的验证、违规项严格累加、SHACL验证延迟介于12.6毫秒至100.3毫秒之间；通过配置等价性测试确认‘综合’配置为最全面的治理策略。所有工具与实现均已开源。

Abstract: AI-enabled services deployed in critical digital infrastructure are subject to governance obligations spanning transparency, accountability, fairness, and traceability. Compliance today remains documentation-centric: obligations are described in prose, audits rely on static checklists, and verification depends on manual review. Such approaches do not scale to automated AI systems. This paper introduces Ontological Knowledge Blocks (OKBs), a programmable governance infrastructure that compiles regulatory obligations into machine-checkable constraints over structured evidence graphs. We formalize an OKB as a 5-tuple that binds normative obligations to an RDF/OWL concept schema, executable SHACL validation rules, explicit evidence requirements, and PROV-O provenance links. A deterministic regulatory compiler translates structured Intermediate Representation (IR) records into composable KB modules, enabling profile-based governance reconfiguration without modifying service code. All artefacts are released as open source.

### [202] [When Planning Fails Despite Correct Execution: On Epistemic Calibration for LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23414)
*Zehao Wang,Shilong Jin,Zhao Cao,Lanjun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出EPC-AW框架以解决大语言模型多智能体系统在规划中的认知校准问题，通过评估计划在不同信息条件下的稳定性来提升系统成功率，实验显示平均提升9.75%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统即使执行正确也可能因智能体对自身知识的误判而失败，这种现象称为规划中的认知校准偏差，且其具有隐蔽性和动态性，传统方法难以应对。

Method: 提出Epistemic Planning Calibration Agentic Workflow（EPC-AW），采用基于信息一致性的计划选择和一致性引导的认知状态修正机制，通过历史不一致来指导未来规划，实现动态校准。

Conclusion: EPC-AW有效缓解了规划中的认知校准偏差问题，通过动态适应和信息一致性评估，增强了多智能体系统的鲁棒性与可靠性。

Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems can fail even when planned actions are executed correctly because agents may misjudge their knowledge when evaluating plan feasibility, a phenomenon we term epistemic miscalibration in planning. Unlike execution errors, epistemic miscalibration is latent during planning, as generated plans can remain self-consistent and executable without observable errors; the miscalibration is also dynamic, as new information can alter feasibility assessments, potentially obscuring past miscalibration signals and causing them to recur over time. To address this, we propose the Epistemic Planning Calibration Agentic Workflow (EPC-AW), which assesses whether plans remain supported under varying information conditions rather than directly verifying feasibility. EPC-AW employs Information-consistency-based Plan Selection, selecting plans whose evaluations are stable across agents, together with Consistency-guided Epistemic State Refinement to adapt calibration over time by leveraging past discrepancies to guide future planning. Experiments show that EPC-AW improves system-level success by an average of 9.75%.

### [203] [EDGE-OPD: Internalizing Privileged Context with Evidence Guided On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23493)
*Aristotelis Lazaridis,Dylan Bates,Aman Sharma,Brian King,Vincent Lu,Jack FitzGerald*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了在罕见标记/身份设置下，基于自监督的在线策略蒸馏（OPSD）中存在的问题，即特权信息可能导致模型行为偏离预期，影响推理能力与通用性能。为此，提出EDGE-OPD方法，通过引导采样（guided rollouts）将特权上下文行为注入学生模型，并引入证据掩码机制，仅在特权信息支持的词元位置更新模型参数。实验表明，传统OPSD和其变体均无法学习目标身份，而加入引导采样后可成功实现；掩码区域消融分析揭示了人格信号集中在正证据尾部，有助于高效知识迁移并保持通用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OPSD方法虽能避免模型分布漂移，但在引入特权上下文（如角色、私有事实）时易导致模型行为偏差，如改变推理方式、降低泛化能力或影响输出风格与长度，从而训练出非期望的副作用而非可迁移的行为。尤其在需要精确学习罕见身份或标记的任务中，该问题尤为突出。

Method: 提出EDGE-OPD方法，包含两个核心设计：1）使用引导采样（guided rollouts）在采样阶段注入特权上下文行为，确保目标行为出现在在线策略数据中；2）引入证据掩码（evidence mask），仅在特权上下文支持当前词元的位置进行模型更新，避免对无关部分进行错误优化。

Result: 实验证明，原始OPSD及其变体RLSD（含/不含验证器）完全无法学习目标身份；而引入引导采样后，所有方法均能成功学习。掩码区域分析显示，人格信号集中于正证据尾部，说明仅需在关键位置施加监督即可实现高效知识迁移，同时有效保留通用语言能力。

Conclusion: EDGE-OPD通过引导采样与证据掩码机制，有效解决了特权信息引发的副作用问题，实现了在不损害通用能力的前提下精准学习罕见身份，为高效、安全的在线策略蒸馏提供了新范式。

Abstract: On-Policy Distillation (OPD) has gained wide attraction as an LLM post-training paradigm due to its effectiveness in improving capabilities without introducing model distribution drift, and consequently, regression in general tasks. On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) is an efficient use-case of OPD, which is appealing as it requires only a single model as a student and teacher, and it also has the benefit of providing privileged context that is a absent at inference time (e.g. a persona, a private fact, or a worked solution) to the teacher during the training process. The challenge in this approach is that the privileged information can change model behavior more than intended: it can modify reasoning, degrade general capabilities, and affect performance indicators like response length, style, or local token preferences. Consequently, OPSD may train the student on side effects rather than a desired, transferable behavior. In this paper, we study this problem in a rare-token/identity setting and propose EviDence GuidEd On-Policy Distillation (EDGE-OPD), a modification of OPSD with two distinct characteristics: a) it uses guided rollouts to inject privileged-context behavior to the student at sampling time, so that the rare target behavior is actually present in the on-policy data, and b) it applies an evidence mask: the student is updated only at token positions where the privileged context supports the sampled token, rather than on every token in the rollout. We empirically show that OPSD (and its variant RLSD, with and without a verifier) completely fail to learn a target identity, while the integration of guided rollouts allows them to succeed. Additionally, mask-region ablations show that the persona signal is localized to the positive-evidence tail, allows us to draw valuable insights about efficient knowledge transfer and preservation of general purpose capabilities.

### [204] [CP or DP? Why Not Both: A Case Study in the Partial Shop Scheduling Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23569)
*Emma Legrand,Roger Kameugne,Pierre Schaus*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将动态规划（DP）与约束编程（CP）结合，以解决部分车间调度问题（PSSP）。DP作为主搜索框架，CP作为子程序用于全局约束传播，提升了灵活性和求解能力。该方法支持任意时间DP策略，并能自然处理任意优先级图，还可设计大型邻域搜索（LNS）方案，重用DP模型并改进当前解。虽在性能上不及顶尖纯CP求解器，但主要贡献在于验证了两种范式融合的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上DP与CP独立使用，缺乏有效整合。为提升求解组合优化问题的能力，尤其是处理复杂优先约束的调度问题，需探索两者的协同机制。本研究旨在展示DP与CP结合的潜力，增强求解灵活性与效率。

Method: 将动态规划作为主搜索框架，引入约束编程作为子程序进行全局约束传播。针对部分车间调度问题（PSSP），利用CP建模灵活处理任意优先约束，并支持任意时间列搜索等策略。通过重用DP模型，在重启过程中施加偏序调度，实现大型邻域搜索（LNS）以改进解质量。

Result: 所提方法能够灵活处理任意优先约束图，支持任意时间搜索策略，并成功实现大型邻域搜索（LNS），显著提升解的质量。尽管在求解速度上不如最先进的纯CP求解器，但证明了混合方法在实际应用中的有效性与可行性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功展示了动态规划与约束编程的有效融合，不仅增强了对复杂调度问题的建模与求解能力，也为未来混合求解框架的设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Dynamic Programming (DP) and Constraint Programming (CP) are well-established paradigms for solving combinatorial optimization problems. Usually, these two approaches are used separately. This paper aims to show that the two can be combined effectively and elegantly, with DP serving as the primary search framework and CP used as a subroutine to leverage global constraint propagation. This paper presents such an approach for the Partial Shop Scheduling Problem (PSSP), for which a pure DP method has previously been proposed, and efficient CP filtering algorithms are available. The PSSP is a general scheduling problem where each job consists of a set of operations with arbitrary precedence constraints. The approach is flexible enough to accommodate anytime DP strategies, such as anytime column search, whereas the original DP algorithm operated in a strictly layer-wise manner. Moreover, the flexibility of the CP modeling makes it straightforward to incorporate arbitrary precedence constraints. As a result, the model naturally handles any precedence graph and even enables the design of a Large Neighborhood Search (LNS) scheme, in which the DP model is reused, and partial-order schedules are imposed across restarts to improve the incumbent solution. While not competitive with state-of-the-art pure CP solvers for this specific problem, our primary contribution is demonstrating the viability of this hybrid integration.

### [205] [Co-ReAct: Rubrics as Step-Level Collaborators for ReAct Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23590)
*Jiazheng Kang,Bowen Zhang,Zixin Song,Jiangwang Chen,Xiao Yang,Da Zhu,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Co-ReAct introduces a rubric-guided action-selection framework for search-intensive, multi-step reasoning tasks, using step-level rubrics during inference to improve agent decision-making. It trains a rubric generator with GRPO using list-wise Spearman rank-correlation against expert consensus, enabling discriminative, actionable guidance. Co-ReAct outperforms ReAct and test-time compute baselines on DeepResearchBench and SQA-CS-V2 across various models, and the rubric generator can be used as a drop-in enhancement.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing ReAct-style agents rely on internal judgment for actions, leading to shallow or redundant reasoning trajectories. Prior rubrics are mostly evaluative rather than guiding during inference, and often lack granularity. This work aims to provide real-time, step-level rubric guidance to improve reasoning quality and efficiency.

Method: Co-ReAct injects rubrics into the agent's context at each decision step to guide Reason-or-Act choices. A dedicated rubric generator is trained using GRPO with a list-wise Spearman rank-correlation reward based on multi-judge expert rankings, ensuring rubrics are discriminative and actionable.

Result: Co-ReAct achieves consistent improvements over ReAct and test-time compute baselines on DeepResearchBench and SQA-CS-V2 across 8B/14B open-source and frontier closed-source models. The rubric generator acts as a plug-and-play component that enhances existing agents without modifying their core mechanisms.

Conclusion: Rubric-guided inference through Co-ReAct enables more targeted, effective reasoning in complex tasks. The trained rubric generator provides reliable, step-level guidance and can be easily integrated into existing agents, offering a promising path toward scalable, high-quality multi-step reasoning.

Abstract: ReAct-style agents for search-intensive, multi-step reasoning tasks rely largely on their own internal judgment to decide what evidence to seek, which reasoning or action step to take next, and when to stop, often producing shallow, redundant, or poorly targeted trajectories. Prior work has explored rubrics as external quality signals, but existing uses are mostly evaluative rather than action-guiding: rubrics typically serve as training-time rewards or post-hoc evaluators of completed outputs, and in deep-research settings they are often coarse-grained and report-level rather than step-level. We introduce Co-ReAct, a rubric-guided action-selection framework that uses rubrics as step-level guidance during inference. At each decision step, Co-ReAct injects a rubric into the agent's context to guide the next Reason-or-Act decision, specifying what the agent should target in evidence seeking, search, reasoning, or self-evaluation. To make this guidance reliable, we train a dedicated rubric generator with GRPO. Unlike prior pairwise or binary preference formulations, our objective optimizes a list-wise Spearman rank-correlation reward against multi-judge expert consensus rankings, encouraging rubrics that are discriminative rather than merely plausible. On DeepResearchBench and SQA-CS-V2, Co-ReAct consistently improves over ReAct and representative test-time compute baselines across search agents built on both 8B/14B open-source and frontier closed-source base models. The trained rubric generator can also serve as a drop-in component that improves these baselines without changing their underlying decision mechanisms. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/ZBWpro/Co-ReAct.

Method: 提出两种数学优化模型：约束规划（CP）模型和混合整数规划（MIP）模型，用于处理大规模任务调度问题，涵盖人员资质、设备、操作顺序、飞机平衡及空间限制等多重约束。

Result: 在包含最多1450个任务的真实数据实例上测试，两种模型均表现出良好求解性能，能够有效支持实际拆解调度决策。

Conclusion: 所提出的CP与MIP模型能有效应对飞机拆解调度中的复杂约束，显著提升调度效率，为实现可持续拆解和企业盈利提供有力支持。

Abstract: Dismantling aircrafts reaching their end of life is a complex endeavour that is necessary in terms of sustainability but yields small income margins for air transport companies. An efficient scheduling of the disassembly procedure is thus crucial to ensure the profitability of the process and incentivize practice. This is a large scheduling problem that involves thousands of tasks and many different constraints: Extracting parts that are destined to be reused requires technicians with specific certifications and equipment. Extraction operations might be subject to precedence relations. Furthermore, the aircraft must be kept balanced during the whole process. Finally, some of the locations of the aircraft have a limited space that caps the number of technicians able to work there concurrently. This article presents the problem in details and proposes two approaches to solve the problem: a Constraint Programming model and a MIP model. The models are tested on instances of varying sizes involving up to 1450 tasks, which are based on real operational data provided by an industrial partner.

</details>


### [207] [Agentic Proving for Program Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23772)
*Alessandro Sosso,Akhil Arora,Bas Spitters*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Claude Code, when used in an agentic proving framework, achieves high success rates in program verification on the CLEVER benchmark: 98.8% valid specifications, 87.5% correct implementation certification, and 98.1% end-to-end success on self-consistent problems. It also provides high-quality self-assessment feedback. The study reveals a growing gap between current benchmarks and agentic provers' capabilities, calling for more robust evaluation methods beyond isomorphism-based scoring.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To evaluate how well modern agentic systems like Claude Code perform in program verification, particularly in comparison to existing benchmarks such as CLEVER, and to assess the reliability and feedback quality of these systems in real-world verification tasks.

Method: The study evaluates Claude Code within an agentic proving framework on the CLEVER benchmark, measuring performance across specification generation, implementation certification, and end-to-end verification. Manual review was conducted to assess the quality of self-generated feedback.

Result: Claude Code successfully generates valid specifications for 98.8% of problems, certifies implementations correctly in 87.5% of cases, and achieves a 98.1% success rate in end-to-end verification on self-consistent entries. It also produces high-quality self-diagnostic feedback.

Conclusion: Modern agentic provers surpass current program verification benchmarks in capability, highlighting the need for more rigorous, bug-resilient evaluation methodologies and suggesting that tight compiler-in-the-loop agentic paradigms are currently the most effective approach for foundational program verification.

Abstract: Agentic systems have recently emerged as state-of-the-art approaches for automated theorem proving in formal mathematics. To assess how far these capabilities extend to program verification, we evaluate Claude Code in an agentic proving framework on CLEVER, a Lean 4 benchmark for verifiable code generation. Our results show that Claude generates arguably valid specifications for 98.8% of problems (with 81.3% also accepted by CLEVER's isomorphism-based scoring on the correct portion of the benchmark), certifies implementations against correct ground-truth specifications for 87.5% of problems, and reaches a 98.1% success rate on the end-to-end program generation and verification pipeline over entries with self-consistent premises. Across all stages, Claude further provides high-quality feedback on its own attempts (as confirmed under manual review), identifying underlying causes of failure and lingering bugs in the dataset. These findings highlight a growing mismatch between the difficulty of existing program verification benchmarks and the capabilities of modern agentic provers, and point to the need for more rigorous, bug-resilient evaluation methodologies, and in particular for alternatives to isomorphism-based scoring of generated specifications. More broadly, our results provide empirical evidence that tight compiler-in-the-loop agentic paradigms are currently the most effective approach for foundational program verification.

</details>


### [208] [Beyond Binary Edits Robust Multimodal Knowledge Editing with Adversarial Subspace Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23780)
*Haoyuan Wang,Xiaohao Liu,Jiajie Su,Jianmao Xiao,Chaochao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种增强的内在多模态知识编辑方法，通过显式建模泛化性来解决现有方法在语义等价变体间传播编辑的局限性。核心思想是定义知识单元以涵盖语义等价的多模态输入，并引入潜在对抗鲁棒性（LAR）生成语义一致的对抗样本，结合秩约束子空间学习（RCSL）强制对齐编辑层的表示，从而提升编辑的泛化能力。实验验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前内在多模态知识编辑方法虽可靠且局部性强，但泛化能力差，无法在语义等价的视觉与语言变体间有效传播编辑结果，主要由于缺乏显式语义监督、编辑范围僵化以及在高维空间中对单一样本的偏倚锚定。

Method: 提出基于知识单元的鲁棒性形式化，定义一致性预测为泛化标准；引入潜空间对抗鲁棒性（LAR）生成语义连贯的对抗样本；设计秩约束子空间学习（RCSL），通过奇异值目标在编辑层实现低秩表示对齐。

Result: 实证分析表明，所提方法显著提升了多模态知识编辑的泛化性能，在多种语义等价变体上保持一致且准确的预测，有效克服了原有方法的脆弱性。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模泛化性和引入对抗鲁棒性与低秩约束机制，本文提出的框架实现了更稳健、更具泛化能力的内在多模态知识编辑，为大模型持续学习提供了新路径。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) need efficient mechanisms to update knowledge without degrading existing capabilities. While intrinsic multimodal knowledge editing achieves strong reliability and locality, it often exhibits limited generality, failing to propagate edits across semantically equivalent visual and linguistic variations. This issue arises from the lack of explicit semantic supervision, rigid editing scopes, and biased anchoring to individual samples in high-dimensional multimodal spaces. We address robust intrinsic multimodal knowledge editing by explicitly targeting generalization. We formalize robustness through knowledge units that group semantically equivalent multimodal inputs and define generality as consistent predictions within each unit. To expose fragile semantic regions, we introduce Latent Adversarial Robustification (LAR), which generates adversarial yet semantically coherent variants in the joint latent space. We further propose Rank-Constrained Subspace Learning (RCSL), enforcing low-rank alignment of adversarial representations at the edit layer via a singular value-based objective. Extensive analysis demonstrates the effectiveness of ASAM empirically.

</details>


### [209] [SPACENUM: Revisiting Spatial Numerical Understanding in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23898)
*Jianshu Zhang,Yijiang Li,Huifeixin Chen,Haoran Lu,Letian Xue,Bingyang Wang,Han Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出SpaceNum框架，评估视觉语言模型（VLMs）在空间数值理解上的表现，通过双向任务Num2Space和Space2Num检验模型将视觉空间结构与语言数字表示相互映射的能力。结果表明，当前VLMs在动态过渡和静态布局中均难以真正将数字与空间意义对齐，表现接近随机猜测。错误分析显示，模型依赖浅层空间线索，缺乏稳定的坐标感知表征，且无法从视觉观察中抽象出结构化空间布局。尽管显式推理带来微弱提升，但调整参数可部分改善其空间数值理解能力，并在外部空间推理基准上实现迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型在具身环境中需生成动作幅度和空间坐标等数值输出，但这些数值是否真正基于空间感知尚不明确。因此需要系统评估模型对空间数值的理解能力。

Method: 构建SpaceNum统一框架，涵盖动态过渡与静态布局两种互补场景；设计双向任务Num2Space和Space2Num，用于评估视觉-语言间空间结构与数字表示的映射能力；结合错误分析、推理轨迹分析及受控干预实验，深入探究模型行为机制。

Result: 在动态过渡与静态布局任务中，现有VLMs普遍无法将数字有效接地于空间意义，表现接近随机水平；模型依赖浅层空间线索，缺乏稳定坐标感知，难以抽象结构化空间布局；显式推理仅带来边际改进，而参数调优可部分提升性能并促进跨任务迁移。

Conclusion: 当前视觉语言模型在空间数值理解方面存在显著缺陷，尚未建立真正意义上的空间-数值语义关联，亟需更有效的训练机制与结构设计以增强其空间认知能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are increasingly deployed in embodied environments, where they need produce numerical outputs such as action magnitudes and spatial coordinates. Although these numbers appear meaningful, it remains unclear whether these numerical outputs are genuinely grounded in spatial perception. Therefore, in this work, we revisit spatial numerical understanding through SpaceNum, a unified framework that captures two complementary settings: numbers as dynamic transitions during spatial exploration, and numbers as static layouts in spatial reasoning. We formulate two bidirectional tasks, Num2Space and Space2Num, to evaluate how well VLMs map between vision-side spatial structure and language-side numerical representations. We systematically study whether current VLMs truly understand numerical values in spatial settings. Across dynamic transitions and static layouts, we find that models largely fail to ground numbers in spatial meaning and often perform close to random guess. Through error analysis, reasoning trace analysis, and controlled interventions, we show that current VLMs rely heavily on shallow spatial cues, struggle to build stable coordinate-aware representations, and fail to abstract structured spatial layouts from visual observations. We further show that explicit reasoning provides only marginal gains, while tuning can partially improve spatial numerical understanding and transfer to external spatial reasoning benchmarks.

</details>
